# استعاذۃ
*Source: KASHKOLE, Binder 34 (Quranic Studies), Chapter 162. 10 topics. Language: ur.*

<!-- section 1 (id=5751, raw_sort=1): DRAFT -->
Plan of Shaytan

We begaun with the ⟪ar:استعاذہ⟫..... which is seeking the protection of Allah from the cursed Shaytan..... And what we learnt in our study of the Istiaza..... and Surah AlFalaq and Surah AlNaas..... is that Allah identifying for us..... or rather pointing out our worst enemy to us..... which is Iblees..... and all of his followers who are Shayateen..... What Allah does is..... he discloses for us ALL of Shaytan's plans..... He tells us about his short term goals..... his long term goals..... how he sets his traps for us..... how he..... very patiently..... puts us on the path of destruction..... Because he has one single goal..... All his whisperings have one single agenda..... to get human beings to take off their clothes.....
⟪ar-quote:فَوَسْوَسَ لَهُمَا ٱلشَّيْطَنُ لِيُبْدِىَ لَهُمَا مَا وُۥرِىَ عَنْهُمَا مِن سَوْءَتِهِمَا⟫

Shaytan whispered to them..... to expose..... what was covered off their ugliness..... their private parts..... Allah honored..... and dignified Adam AS and his children with clothing..... Why?..... To elevate them ABOVE animals..... because animals don't care for clothing..... There's no reason to honor and dignify animals..... because they are base creatures..... But Allah gave Adam AS and his children..... the intellect..... made them his representative on earth..... and therefore honored them with clothing..... And Shaytan wants to get humanity to remove their clothings..... He wants them to remove that honor and degrade and humiliate themselves down to that base level of animals..... And what is the ULTIMATE humiliation?.....
⟪ar-quote:رَبَّنَآ إِنَّكَ مَن تُدْخِلِ ٱلنَّارَ فَقَدْ أَخْزَيْتَهُۥ⟫

Oh master! No doubt..... the one you entered in hell fire has been truly humilated.....

So this is what he wants..... But he does this in such a subtle way..... He doesn't just tell us to do the wrong thing..... He makes the wrong thing beautiful to us..... and then we do it ourselves.....  And we see evidence of that all around us today..... People are so happy to take off their clothes..... to show some skin as they say.....
⟪ar-quote:لِيُبْدِىَ لَهُمَا مَا وُۥرِىَ عَنْهُمَا مِن سَوْءَتِهِمَا⟫

to expose to them what was covered of their ugliness..... Human being..... Intellectual being..... Khaleefatul Allah..... Allah's representative on this earth..... the one he created to manifest His divine attributes on this earth..... reduced to the level of an animal..... This is what Shaytan is doing..... this is what he's already done..... Look at us today..... Not only do we do this today..... we are damn proud of it too..... We talk about it..... We announce it..... post it on facebook..... We make fun of those who DON'T do it..... call them backward..... and cavemen..... and what not..... It's really amazing if you think about it..... How Shaytan has changed our perspective of beautiful..... One step at a time..... without us even realizing it..... Making it extremely logical..... Oh I have freedom..... Freedom to express my sexuality..... Why did Allah make me beautiful if he didn't want me to show it off..... I mean some of the reasons I hear just amaze me.....  SubhanAllah! ..... You don't even use your phones without a cover..... Because they'll get scratched..... because they'll become ugly..... It's so beautiful..... I need to protect its beauty..... But when it comes to you own beauty..... The beauty that is a manifestation of the divine essence..... AlJameel..... The most beautiful..... He gave you something from his own divine names..... and you are throwing that name around in front of the entire world.....  You value your phone more than the divine name of Allah.....  Astaghfirullah!.....  What amazing logic!!! ..... But this is what Shaytan does..... Because he's a trickster..... He'll come up with the most PERFECT logic..... He'll convince you..... and prove to you..... that fire is better than clay..... Because logic is his thing.....

Shaytan is a liar

Junaid baghdadee relates that he once had a dream in which he met Iblees..... And he has this dialogue with Iblees in his dream..... He asked Iblees..... Why wouldn't you do Sajda to Adam AS?..... Why would you disobey Allah? ..... How could you be so stupid to refuse and stand against Allah when he gave you a command?..... What's wrong with you..... And Iblees replies..... Ya Junaid..... How could I do Sajda to anyone other than Allah?..... And Junaid got completely thrown off..... He's like WOAH..... That's deep dude!..... And so he goes in this state of complete confusion..... Because now what Iblees just said to him made perfect sense..... But you see this is what Iblees does..... He's a trickster..... He presents prefect logic.....

So Junaid goes to Imam AS and tells him about his dream..... Imam AS said..... الابلیس ھو الکذاب..... Iblees is a liar..... That could not be the reason he refused to disobey Allah..... because what he's saying..... that I couldn't bow down to anyone other than Allah..... that's from the Adab..... That's from the ettiquettes..... But .....  الامر فوق الادب..... The command of Allah is greater than all etiquettes..... If you are the president of your school..... or a teacher of your class..... And the school principal tells you do something..... like repreimand a student for something he did..... That may not be the best ettiquetes..... It may not be a nice thing to do..... But you have to do it..... Because the command came from someone who is superior in rank..... So even though I wouldn't do sajda to anyone other than Allah..... but if it is Allah himself commanding me to do Sajda..... I have to do it..... I won't do sajda if you tell me to do it..... But if Allah himself is issuing a direct command..... I HAVE to obey..... because .....  الامر فوق الادب..... Command trumps etiquettes..... ..... But this is what Iblees does..... He ticks and confuses through logic.....

Speech of Shaytan

And so through these Quranic stories..... Allah informs us how Shaytan completely destroyed people before us..... How he deceived them..... and humiliated them into the hell fire.....  by pretending to be their best friend..... right?..... So by telling us about our past..... Allah is warning us about our present.....  to protect our future..... Look! He did this to the people before you..... this is where they ended up..... And now's he's doing exactly the same thing to you..... Be careful..... Don't take him for your friend.....

But then Allah doesn't stop there..... He even goes further and tells us what's going to happen in the future..... On judgment day..... He says Iblees will stand before his followers on judgment day..... and deliver a speech.....
⟪ar-quote:وَقَالَ ٱلشَّيْطَنُ لَمَّا قُضِىَ ٱلْأَمْرُ⟫

 when the affair is over.....
⟪ar-quote:فَرِيقٌۭ فِى ٱلْجَنَّةِ وَفَرِيقٌۭ فِى ٱلسَّعِيرِ⟫

A group has been sent to hell ..... and a group has been sent to paradise..... .....  that's when Iblees says
⟪ar-quote:إِنَّ ٱللَّهَ وَعَدَكُمْ وَعْدَ ٱلْحَقِّ وَوَعَدتُّكُمْ فَأَخْلَفْتُكُمْ⟫

Allah promised you a true promise.....  and I promised you a false promise..... This is what he says in hell.....  He gives a sermon..... he gives a khutba in hell.....  And all the members of hell are present there to listen to this sermon and that's what he says to them..... Allah promised you the truth..... Everything that was in the Quran was the truth..... Everything that was in the Torah was true..... Everything that wasn't the Gospel was true..... All those prophet spoke the truth.......... He gets all of them..... that harvest of humanity..... the whole lot that disobeyed Allah..... he gets all of them and that and this is what he says

Allah promised you and I promised you.....  you believed me and you did not believe Allah..... I betrayed you.....  and then he says
⟪ar-quote:وَمَا كَانَ لِىَ عَلَيْكُم مِّن سُلْطَنٍ⟫

 I had no authority over you.....
⟪ar-quote:إِلَّآ أَن دَعَوْتُكُمْ فَٱسْتَجَبْتُمْ لِى⟫

 the only thing that I could do was invite you to sin..... .....  and you responded.....  I invited you to be miserly.....  I scared you..... I said ..... what is going to happen to your children if you do not collect all this money.....  what's going to happen to your children if you do not build these big houses for them.....  I scared you with poverty.....  Put aside put aside.....
⟪ar-quote:قِرش أَبیَد بِیَومَ الاسْوَد⟫

as the Arabs say..... A white penny for a black day..... put aside..... put aside..... that's Shaytan.....

I brought forth temptations and desires for you.....
⟪ar-quote:فَلَا تَلُومُونِى وَلُومُوٓا۟ أَنفُسَكُم⟫

So don't blame me ..... just blame yourself.....
⟪ar-quote:مَّآ أَنَا۠ بِمُصْرِخِكُمْ وَمَآ أَنتُم بِمُصْرِخِىَّ⟫

 I can't save you now and you can't save me.....  that's what Shaytan says to everybody.....

And on that day Allah says to this group..... this harvest of hell fire..... Allah says.....
⟪ar-quote:أَلَمْ أَعْهَدْ إِلَيْكُمْ يَبَنِىٓ آدَمَ أَن لَّا تَعْبُدُوا۟ ٱلشَّيْطَنَ ۖ⟫

Did I not make you promise of children of Adam..... to not become a slave of Shaytan.....
⟪ar-quote:إِنَّهُۥ لَكُمْ عَدُوٌّۭ مُّبِينٌۭ⟫

I told you ..... no doubt..... he is your worst enemy.....
⟪ar-quote:وَأَنِ ٱعْبُدُونِى ۚ هَذَا صِرَطٌۭ مُّسْتَقِيمٌۭ ‎⟫

Be my slave instead..... worship me instead of him..... This is the striaght path.....

Allah identified our enemy for us

So Allah basically revealed everything I need to know about Shaytan..... The past..... the present..... and the future..... Now when I read about this..... it makes me think..... ..... Who does that? ..... Who would point out for me..... who my enemy is..... where he's hiding..... how he plans to attack me..... why I should not listen to him..... and then collect and present all the evidence against him..... show me how he has already hurt so many others who believed him..... Who would do that for me?.......... 

Sounds like a friend to me..... A friend who loves me..... who cares about me..... Someone who is genuinely concerned for my well being?..... But then you know what's more amazing?..... He didn't just point out all of this and just leave me by myself..... right?

Think about your best friend in school..... Let's say he finds out that someone is going to hurt you..... let's say he's planning to ambush you after class..... So your friend tells you..... Listen!..... this guy..... He's going to come to you after class.....  and sweet talk you into walking with him down this particular path..... But I overheard him talking to his buddies..... they'll be 2 guys hiding behind the 4th tree on the left side of this path..... And as soon as you go past that tree..... they will jump you..... and then they'll beat the crap out of you.....  and steal your stuff..... So no matter what this guy says..... don't listen to him..........

Basically your friend tells you everything about this guy who's planning to hurt you..... Now.....  JUST doing that much for you..... qualifies him as a true friend!..... doesn't it?..... That alone will convince you that he really loves you and cares about you..... But then he says..... you know what?..... I know you're as sucker for ice cream..... And as soon as he tells you there is an ice cream truck down that path..... and they have chocolate flavor..... I know once you heart that..... you'll forget EVERYTHING I just said..... and you'll be like..... ugghh LEAD THE WAY!..... So you know what?..... If you want..... I'll walk with you..... I'll stop you from walking that path..... right when he tempts you.....  And if you still choose to walk the path..... I'll try to protect you when these guys try to jump you..... I won't let them hurt you..... But you just have to constantly CHOOSE to stay behind me..... I promise I won't let them harm you in any way.....

If your friend does does that..... NOW what kind of a friend would he be?.....

Allah did not just inform us about Shaytan's plots..... and then leave me to deal with it all by myself..... because he knew..... that we're dealing with an enemy that we cannot see..... and we are at a clear disadvantage against him..... So what did he do? ..... He offered his own protection to us..... He said don't worry..... I'll protect you..... IF you choose to submit to my protection..... I will protect you from Shaytan..... 

So now if I have even half a brain..... after knowing all this..... after realizing that I am not going to be able to fight Shaytan by myself..... because this is an extremley powerful and ruthless enemy..... and on top of that I can't even see him or hear him when he's whispering to me..... Therefore I need the protection of the one who CAN see him..... and who CAN hear him.....  Who is strong enough to stop him WHEN he is attacking me..... If I have at least that much sense..... I willingly and submitting myself to Allah..... I say ⟪ar:اعوذ باللہ من الشیطان الرجیم⟫.....  Oh Allah..... I see your refuge against the cursed Shaytan..... Because ONLY you can protect me from him.....

So even before we BEGIN our spiritual journey..... If we wanna have any sort of chance ..... of actually making it..... we need to first accept and submit ourself to Allah's protection..... It's like.....  before you begin any kind of serious training program..... these professional trainers..... they say..... you should first see a physician..... why? ..... Because if you have some physical condition that you're unaware of..... that you CANNOT SEE..... you want that taken care of ..... BEFORE you begin your workout..... Otherwise you will not be able to get any benefit from the workout itself..... right?

That is precisely what we're doing with the Istiaza..... We are entering Allah's protection..... so that Shaytan does not interfere with our spiritual journey..... which is the first ayah of Surah AlFateha..... BARR.....

Tie camel first in order to protect it

This is really important to understand..... We're not going to benefit from the Fateha..... if we do not mee the requirements of the Istiaaza..... Someone came to the masjid for prayers..... He had his camel with him..... He met Rasul Allah outside the masjid..... and he asked him.....
⟪ar-quote:يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ.....  أَعْقِلُهَا وَأَتَوَكَّلُ.....  أَوْ أُطْلِقُهَا وَأَتَوَكَّلُ⟫

Should I tie my camel first and then trust Allah..... or should I leave it untied and then trust Allah..... The messenger replied.....
⟪ar-quote:اعْقِلْهَا وَتَوَكَّلْ⟫

Tie the camel..... and THEN trust Allah to protect it..... So we need to tie the camel first..... We can't just can't leave the camel untied..... and then expect Allah to protect it..... We have to do OUR part first..... The camel is a symbol for our desires..... Because they are massive..... they are a powerful beast..... like the camel..... The camel is no ordinary animal..... It's a very massive..... very strong animal..... just like our desires and our temptations..... So we need to tie and bind this camel of our desires..... which if you remember..... is literally what the word Aqal means..... We have to empty the cup before we can fill it again..... Istiaza is turning over the cup..... emptying it out..... COMPLETELY..... Because that is literally what the heart is..... It is a container.....  and every container has its limits.....  And if the heart has reached its limits with the Haram.....  it will not have any room for the halaal to come in..... And taht would be disaster..... And this is why the sahaba..... (رضی اللہ عنھم) said ..... that the prophet litreally emtied us out .....  He emptied out our hearts.....  from the darkness of ignorance.....  and filled it with light..... 

So there is an emptying that has to take place BEFORE the filling.....  Just like you have to exhale before you can inhale.....  Just like the heart has to be contracted before it can be  expanded.....  This is the nature of creation..... right?.....   the diastolic the systolic.....  this is the very nature of human beings.....  The pupil expands in order to take in light.....  and then it contracts to prevent light from coming in..... These are all signs..... These are all ayaats..... Because this is the very nature ..... Allah has created us on..... Because He is AlQabid and AlBasit.....  he is the expander and he is the contractor.....  so the more we expand for Shaitan the more we contract for Al-Rehman.....  And the more we expand for the AlRehman.....  the more we contract for Shaytan..... That's La Ilaha ..... Illa Allah.......... La Ilaha..... There is no Ilah..... That's contraction..... That's tying our camel at the doorstep of Allah..... And then there is Bismillah..... that is entering the masjid of Allah.....

That's the entire concept of the Istiaaza..... We are emptying out our hearts..... We're emptying it out.....  from the whispers of Shaytan..... from all desires of the haraam..... from all forbidden temptations..... why? ..... So that we can now fill it with the Fateha..... We are closing the doors on the cursed Shaytan..... so that we can walk through the doors of Allah's mercy ..... and this is how we get to..... ⟪ar:بسم اللہ الرحمن الرحیم⟫

---

Now we begin our spiritual journey..... which is the missing verb from the Basmallah..... What is it that the Basmallah teaches us?..... It gives us an introduction..... or I should say..... a reminder ..... of who Allah (Azza Wa Jal) is..... And how do we get reminded of who Allah (Azza Wa Jal) is?..... By observing the divine attributes of Allah (Subhanhu Wa Ta'ala) WITHIN his creation..... And not everyone will do that..... This is a very specific group of people who are actually able to witness the attributes of Allah through his creation.....

And this is where the Quran and Allah's messenger comes into play.....

is the map..... I need the direction ..... And I need someone to explain the direction to me.....

I disobey my purpose..... If I do not fulfill the purpose of my existence..... and let my free will  that too must have an impact.....

So my creator must want me to submit my will to him..... He must want me to choose something.....

When I realize this..... the next thing I'm learning from the Fateha*.....*is that this incredibly powerful..... completely self-sufficent Allah..... is characterizing himself with Rehma..... He is EXTREMELY loving..... extremely caring..... extremely merciful..... And I have to think..... Does Allah actually need to be merciful?..... Does he really need to be merciful..... What if he wasn't?..... What would you and I do..... if he was not merciful..... Let's say this ayah would have read..... instead of BARR ..... what if it read.....   ⟪ar:بسم اللہ العزیز العادل⟫ ..... With the name of Allah..... the most powerful and the most just..... Instead of intense and consistent mercy..... what if he characterized himself with power and justice..... Because that would mean..... the second I do something wrong..... the all powerful decrees his justice against me..... He punishes me right away..... I miss a prayer..... and he descends angels upon me to beat me to a pulp..... Because prayer..... is Allah's right on me..... And He has the right to demand that right off me..... and punish me if I don't fulfill that right..... Because He could certainly force me to fulfill that right whether I want to or not..... We all pay taxes ever year..... so we know what that feels like.......... We can't escape a government..... which is body of creations..... thre is no way we could escape Allah.....  What if Allah ..... being my creator..... imposed a property tax on me..... I mean he'd be totally justified..... He wouldn't be wrong if he did that..... After all He is my creator..... and that makes me his property..... So He can do with me whatever he chooses..... What if my sustenance and my daily ration of food..... water..... sleep..... even oxygen..... What if all of this was given to me based on my level of obedience to him..... ? Does he has the power to do that?..... He sure does.....
مَّا مِن دَآبَّةٍ إِلَّا هُوَ آخِذٌۢ بِنَاصِيَتِهَآ

There is not a moving creature that Allah does not hold by its forelock.....

So the question becomes..... if instead of AlRehman and AlRaheem..... Allah chose to charaterize his relation with his creation ..... as that of AlAzeez AlAadil..... What would you and I have done? What COULD you and I do? ..... What could.....  you and I and all the rest of creation combined..... do  to stop him?..... Is there anything we could have done?..... No..... Absolutely not..... A VERY powerful king..... does not have to kind..... and history shows us that they're usually not..... Because they have no fear of accountability..... Is Allah accountable to someone?..... No He's not..... Everything and everyone is accountable to him.....
يَٓأَيُّهَا ٱلنَّاسُ أَنتُمُ ٱلْفُقَرَآءُ إِلَى ٱللَّهِۖ وَٱللَّهُ هُوَ ٱلْغَنِىُّ ٱلْحَمِيدُ

Oh people..... you are all in complete need of Allah..... And Allah is entirely self-sufficient without you
إِن يَشَأْ يُذْهِبْكُمْ وَيَأْتِ بِخَلْقٍۢ جَدِيدٍۢ ‎

If he so desires..... he can remove all of you..... and put in your place a new creation

But I learn from BARR..... that not only is he powerful..... He is also EXTREMELY loving..... EXTREMELYcaring..... EXTREMELY concerned for me..... EXTREMELY merciful..... even though he has ABSOLUTELY no reason to be that way..... But the relationship HE himself has decided to have with me..... is not just that of love and mercy..... but of INTENSE love and mercy..... and CONSTNAT love and mercy..... The relationship that a mother has with her child when it is in her womb.....  SubhanAllah!

And how do I expereince this?..... I mean how do I know that Alla love me..... and care for me..... and is concerned about me..... How do I know this is his relationship with me?..... I know this.....  because when I see his creation around me..... I see that they are all in a state of complete submission to Allah..... They're all following Islam..... That's what Islam means..... Submission.....

.... So then what is my purpose?.....
وَمَا خَلَقْتُ ٱلْجِنَّ وَٱلْإِنسَ إِلَّا لِيَعْبُدُونِ

And we did not create Jinn and Man except for Ibadah..... And Ibadah ..... as I mentioned earlier..... is two things..... It is worship..... and obedience..... The time when we are in salaah..... that's worship..... because worship is time based..... and the rest of the time ..... from the time we wake up to the time we sleep..... what do I have to do?..... obedience..... I have to stay in obedience to Allah.....  Just like the rest of Allah's creation..... That's exactly what they're doing.....  They're doing what they were created to do..... that's obedience..... and they're doing it WHEN they're supposed to do it..... that's worship.....

And how do I know what kind of obedience he expects of me?..... Did he give me an example of that? ..... Something I could understand and relate to?..... body and the soul.....

---

So this is where Istiaaza and the first ayah of the Fateha gets me..... After submitting to allah's protection with the Istiaaza..... I now understand who my Allah is..... through his divine attributes manifesting in his creation..... I understand the kind of relationship he has with me..... I understand now how much he loves me..... how much he cares for me..... how he is intensely and constantly merciful towards me..... even though he has absolutely no need to do that..... Recognizing all of this.....  I also now understand what my purpose is..... that I need to be in a state of constant worship and obedience to him..... I begin my jourey towards him..... That's Bismillah AlRehman AlRaheem..... I begin my journey towards him.....

Because the verb..... the action is going to prove his love for you ..... The one who truly begins with BARR..... will think about the blessings of food..... taste..... smell.....  he'll become obsessed with Allah..... constantly reminded of Allah's mercy through BARR..... that's why BARR is said before you begin something..... because the act will show you his rehma if you choose to find it.....

And as soon as I begin my journey..... what is my natural response to Allah?  seeing all his love for me..... what is my natural response?

AlHamdulillahi Rab Alalameen.....

<!-- section 2 (id=5715, raw_sort=2): ISTIAAZA: I seek refuge from Shaytan -->
The next thing I want to talk about is the ⟪ar:استعاذہ⟫which is what we commonly recite before we begin reciting the Quran itself . ⟪ar:اعوذ باللہ من الشیطان الرجیم⟫. This ayah is called the ⟪ar:استعاذہ⟫. It is not a part of Surah Al-Fateha itself.  but it is certainly linked to the Fateha. and every other surah of the Quran for that matter.  The Fateha actually starts with the Basmallah. which is ⟪ar:بسم اللہ الرحمن الرحیم⟫ . In the Arab world. this ayah ⟪ar:بسم اللہ الرحمن الرحیم⟫ is referred to the Basmallah. with a fatha or a zabar. But one thing to remember is that this basmallah is an ACTUAL PART of Al-Fateha itself. but it is NOT a part of the remaining Surahs. I'll say that again. The Basmallah is an actual part of Surah Al-Fateha. but it is NOT a part of the remaining Surahs. The Basmallah is recited before all other surahs to honor those surahs. because it contains the primary name and attributes of  Allah and AlRehman and AlRaheem. and through that we begin the recitation of Allah's holy book .  but it is not the first ayah of any of the other surahs.

But when it comes to Surah AlFateha. it IS a part of the Surah itself. it is the first ayah.  It is the leader and the king of all remaining ayats of Surah Al-Fateha. As we know Surah AlFateha has 7 ayats and the Basmallah. is the highest ranking ayah of  those 7 ayats. If you skip this ayah. you lose all the power and majesty of Surah AlFateha.  and InshaAllah when we study this ayah. you'll understand why.

So what I want you to remember is that ⟪ar:أعوذ باللہ من الشیطان الرجیم⟫ is called the ⟪ar:استعاذہ⟫. and ⟪ar:بسم اللہ الرحمن الرحیم⟫is called the Basmallah! Now before we being the ⟪ar:استعاذہ⟫. let's get an idea of what topics we are going to cover over the next few sessions.

Since this ⟪ar:استعاذہ⟫is used to seek refuge or protection of Allah from the cursed Shaytan. So InshaAllah as part of analyzing this ayah. we will try to get an in depth understanding of who Shaytan is. what made him a Shaytan. What is the difference between Shaytan and Iblees. Are they two separate entities? Or are they both the same? What is Shaytan's real agenda. and why he is so bent upon getting us into trouble. What is this guy's problem.? How does he attack? What are his whisperings? What is this thing called ⟪ar:وسوسۃ⟫. InshaAllah we will cover all these topics over the next few sessions.

As part of our analysis and study of the ⟪ar:استعاذہ⟫we will also study two surahs. Surah AlFalaq and Surah AlNaas. And the reason for that. is that these 2 surahs are in reality the explanation of the details of the ⟪ar:استعاذہ⟫. We will look at the true meaning of the word protection. and why we need Allah's protection against Shaytan. why is it that we are not able to protect ourselves. why do we need a higher power. and we will also see why it is ONLY Allah . and no other power other than Allah. that is capable of protecting us. We will see what the requirements of coming under Allah's protection are. How do we make ourselves worthy of His protection.  these are some of the things we will InshaAllah cover in the study of this ayah. and trust me. once we are done with the study of this ayah. the ⟪ar:استعاذہ⟫will take on a whole new meaning for us . We will never be able to say the ⟪ar:استعاذہ⟫. in the casual superficial way that we do today. Today when we recite the ⟪ar:استعاذہ⟫against Shaytan. he probably laughs at us.  because he knows that our ⟪ar:استعاذہ⟫ is an empty shell.  It's a fake bullet. an empty cartridge. a blunt sword. that does nothing against him. except maybe tickle him a bit. But InshaAllah after we are equipped with the knowledge of  this ayah. our ⟪ar:استعاذہ⟫will become an extremely powerful strike against Shaytan. because it will be backed up with the comprehension of not just the ayah itself. but also SurahAlFalaq and Surah AnNaas. and also because we will have met the requirements of gaining Allah's protection . ⟪ar:أنشاء اللہ تعالی⟫.

So let's begin⟪ar:بأذن اللہ .⟫

---

Meaning of ISTIAAZA

What is the ⟪ar:استعاذہ⟫? and where did it come from? The ⟪ar:استعاذہ⟫comes from the ayah of the Quran itself. Allah commands us in Surah Al-Nahal:

⟪ar-quote:فَإِذَا قَرَأْتَ ٱلْقُرْآنَ فَٱسْتَعِذْ بِٱللَّهِ مِنَ ٱلشَّيْطَنِ ٱلرَّجِيمِ⟫

When you are about to recite the Quran. then seek refuge of Allah from Shaitaan AlRajeem. Also in Surah Aeraaf Allah says

⟪ar-quote:وَإِمَّا يَنْزَغَنَّكَ مِنَ ٱلشَّيْطَنِ نَزْغٌۭ ⟪ar-quote:فَٱسْتَعِذْ بِٱللَّهِ⟫⟫

And before the shaitaan. whispers his evil into you. seek refuge of Allah

⟪ar-quote:إِنَّهُۥ سَمِيعٌ عَلِيمٌ⟫. because he is the all listener and the all knower.

Therefore. before we begin studying the actual ayaats of Surah Al-Fateha. I want us all to gain a really good understanding of this ⟪ar:استعاذہ⟫. and how it is linked to Surah AlFateha and the rest of the Quran.

**Spiritual protection**

So what does the word ⟪ar:استعاذہ⟫mean? The word ⟪ar:استعاذہ⟫comes from the word ، ⟪ar:عاذ ، یعوذ، أعوذ⟫. which means to turn to someone for protection. to turn to someone seeking their help. to tell somebody that you are in danger and you cannot defend yourself on your own. It is an acknowledgment that I need the protection of another entity. that is more powerful than myself. to help me spiritually. not to help me physically. You don't use the word ⟪ar:عاذ or ⟪ar:أعوذ⟫⟫in arabic for physical help. you ONLY use the word ⟪ar:أعوذ⟫when you require spiritual help.

When is it that we need physical help? When we are dealing with the seen. And when do we need spiritual help? When we are dealing with the unseen. Physical help are things. for which we need to dial 911. or call someone by saying. Please help me I'm being attacked. In such situations in Arabic. we would NOT say ⟪ar:عاذ .⟫We would use other words such as ⟪ar:نجد⟫or ⟪ar:نصر⟫. You understand?

SO ⟪ar:عاذ⟫is used exclusively to solicit spiritual help and protection. whose protection? Protection of a diety. a god. a divine power. an entity that is all powerful.

So these are the 2 requirements of the word ⟪ar:عاذ⟫. It is used to seek spiritual protection. and ONLY from a diety.  Only when these two requirements are fulfilled. the word ⟪ar:عاذ⟫is used in Arabic. If I turn for spiritual guidance to a religious leader. or a psychologist or a therapist. I CANNOT use the word ⟪ar:عاذ⟫. because it's not the same thing. I am not turning to them with the intention of seeking their protection. I am turning to them for gainnig knowledge. seeking guidance and help. not protection. And they are not a diety. therefore I cannot use the word ⟪ar:عاذ⟫for them. even though the guidance and help I need is spiritual in nature. you understand?

So who is that diety that we are turning to for spiritual help? ⟪ar:أعوذ باللہ⟫ . That diety is Allah! Turning to an entity in this manner is done EXCLUSIVELY for Allah (SWT). Now why is that important? It is important because. this act of the  ⟪ar:استعاذہ⟫. this act of turning to Allah seeking His spiritual protection. itself becomes an act of worship. Why is that? Because we are obeying Allah's command. Allah commanded us.

⟪ar-quote:وَإِمَّا يَنْزَغَنَّكَ مِنَ ٱلشَّيْطَنِ نَزْغٌۭ⟫ ⟪ar-quote:فَٱسْتَعِذْ بِٱللَّهِ;  إِنَّهُۥ سَمِيعٌ عَلِيمٌ⟫

BECAUSE we are turning ONLY to Allah for our spiritual protection in compliance and obedience to his command. the act of  ⟪ar:استعاذہ⟫itself becomes an act of worship. And this is important to understand. Because if I turn to another entity for spiritual protection in this way. other than Allah. then that act in itself.  becomes the very definition of Shirk. which is to hold a partner with Allah. Because that means. I believe that someone other than Allah has the power to protect me spiritually from the enemy I seek protection from. That would be equivalent to prostrating or submitting before an idol. And this is something that people before Islam used to do.

In Pre Islamic Ignorance. (⟪ar:دور الجاھلیۃ⟫) when a man would travel through the desert. and he would camp for the night. he would be scared of the attackes of jinns and deamons. He would be scared that they would attack him in the night. so he would stand up on a high cliff and announce loudly :

⟪ar-quote:أعوذ بِسَیِّدِ ھٰذا الوادی⟫

I seek refuge and protection  from the leader of the jinn of  this valley that I'm spending the night in.

And what would this do? Would the jinns protect them? No! In Surah Jinn . Allah mentions on the tongue of the jinn . that when those people did this. it only increased the jinn in their arragoance and in their efforts to mislead mankind.

⟪ar-quote:وَأَنَّهُۥ كَانَ رِجَالٌۭ مِّنَ ٱلْإِنسِ يَعُوذُونَ بِرِجَالٍۢ مِّنَ ٱلْجِنِّ فَزَادُوهُمْ رَهَقًۭا⟫

And no doubt, there were men among human beings . who took shelter with the leader of the jinns, but they only increased them in sin and disbelief.

So we do not seek this kind of spiritual protection from any other entity except Allah. so the words  ⟪ar:اعوذ باللہ⟫means.  that I turn for spiritual help and for spiritual protection . to a diety who is Allah. who is powerful. acknowledging at the same time. that I am NOT powerful. 

So when I say ⟪ar:اعوذ باللہ⟫ . I am saying. I am accepting. that I have no power to protect myself. THERFORE I am turning to Allah who is the all powerful. I am incapable. therefore I am turning to the capable. I am weak. I am ⟪ar:ضعیف⟫. therefore I am turning to the strong . the ⟪ar:قوی⟫the ⟪ar:عزیز⟫. I am a slave. who needs protection of his master.  therefore I am turning to my master.

So my reciting the ⟪ar:استعاذہ⟫. in and of itself. contains 2 acknowledgments. the acknowledgment of my weakness. and my incapability to protect myself against the attacks of Shaytan. AND the acknowledgment of the power of my protector. my diety. my Allah. who is strong. who is powerful. and who IS capable of protecting me from my greatest enemy . Shaytan AlRjaeem. the cursed devil. And therefore my act of reciting the ⟪ar:استعاذہ⟫. my act of turning ONLY to Allah seeking his protection . BECOMES  an act of worship.  And every act of worship has a reward. So the next time you recite the ⟪ar:استعاذہ⟫think about this. and it will change the way you approach Allah's protection.  and InshaAllah. we'll look at this further in much more detail.

---

3 version of ISTIAAZA

But before we do that. let's talk a bit about the semantics and the usage of the ⟪ar:استعاذہ⟫. and why is it placed before the recitation of Quran? There are 3 common ways in which the ⟪ar:استعاذہ⟫is recited. The first is the short version of the istiaaza    . ⟪ar:أعوذ باللہ من الشیطان الرجیم⟫   .which means. I seek Allah's protection from Shaytan AlRejeem. the cursed devil. that's the simple one.

The second is one which Rasul Allah sometimes used to say even during his salaah

⟪ar-quote:أعوذ باللہ من الشیطان الرجیم مِن ھَمزِہِ وَ نَفْخِہِ وَ نَفْثِہِ⟫

I seek refuge of Allah from Shaitaan AlRajeem. from his whispering. from his prodings and from his blowings.  Let's examine these words.

The first word ⟪ar:ھَمزِہِ⟫comes from ⟪ar:ھُمَزَہ⟫which means to prod and to poke. You know how sometimes people do that too. with their words. they hurt people. they poke. they prod. kick them when they are down. They verbally stick a knife in the heart and then twist it around a bit. And they do it under the disguise of being a wellwisher. So for example. someone is already worried about their survival because they lost their job. and the ⟪ar:ھامز⟫ will go . Oh really? You lost your job? O thats so bad. especially when the economy is so horrible right now. its almost going to be impossible for you to find another. I know this family. the guy lost his job. they eventually lost the house. his wife divorced him. his kids left him. he ended up committing suicide. It's SO bad out there. but don't worry. you'll be fine.

Ever met or interacted with such people? This is one meaning of Humaza. . And Allah says.

⟪ar-quote:وَيْلٌۭ لِّكُلِّ هُمَزَةٍۢ لُّمَزَةٍ⟫

There is destruction for those who prod and poke. Shaytan is constantly proding and poking us. constantly urging us to do bad things .He is constantly pushing our buttons. Instigating us. making us angry and mean. forcing us to over react. that is all ⟪ar:ھَمزْ⟫.

Nafakha means to blow. As Allah says in the Quran in the story of Adam AS's creation.

⟪ar-quote:فَإِذَا سَوَّيْتُهُۥ وَنَفَخْتُ فِيهِ مِن رُّوحِى⟫

Once I completed the creation of Adam. I blew my soul into him. this is nafakha. to blow. Shaytan is constantly blowing his thoughts. his ideas. desires and temptations. fear and anger. jealousy and envy. He is contantly blowing these things into us. and that is all ⟪ar:نَفْخَ⟫.

And then there is Nafasa. (not with a ⟪ar:س⟫but a⟪ar:ث⟫) which is also a type of blowing. but it's one in which a little bit of spit comes out. and this worse than just blowing. This tactic is mentioned in the Quran in Surah AlFalaq

⟪ar-quote:من شر النفاثات فی العقد⟫

InshaAllah we'll look at this word in much more detail when we study the Surah. So Shaytan pokes us. prods us. blows on us. spits on hus.  He uses all these tactics and mechanations to harm us. And that's why Rasul Allah SAS would seek Allah AWJ's protection from all these tactics of Shaytan by saying.

⟪ar-quote:أعوذ باللہ من الشیطان الرجیمِ ۔  من ھَمزِہِ وَ نَفْخِہِ وَ نَفْثِہِ⟫

---

This is another varition of this same ⟪ar:أستعاذہ⟫. which was used by Rasul Allah. in which he added ⟪ar:السمیع العلیم⟫ to it.

⟪ar-quote:أعوذ باللہ السمیع العلیم من الشیطان الرجیم ۔ ⟪ar-quote:من ھَمزِہِ وَ نَفْخِہِ وَ نَفْثِہِ⟫⟫

I seek refuge of Allah who hears all and who knows all. from Shaitaan AlRajeem. from his whispering from his prodings and from his blowings. So this is the longest version of the ⟪ar:أستعاذہ⟫that our prophet would sometime use. Now two attributes of Allah ⟪ar:السمیع العلیم⟫ are used in this version. and we also use these two attributes. in every Fard namaz when we recite Wajjahtu Wajhee before we begin AlFatiha. What is the last sentence of that dua?

⟪ar-quote:علی ملت ابرھیم و دین محمد و ولایت علی و أبرؤ الیہ من أعدائہ الظالمین ۔

وَ أعوذ باللہ **السمیع العلیم** من الشیطان الَّعین الرجیم⟫

and then we recite the Basmallah and Surah AlFateha.

Now the question is. why these 2 names of Allah?. Out of 99 names of Allah. why these 2 names in particular? Its very interesting. What is the meaning of ⟪ar:السمیع⟫?. . It means the one. who hears everything! and what is the meaning of ⟪ar:العلیم⟫? The one who knows everything! So ⟪ar:السمیع العلیم⟫is the one who hears everything and knows everything.

Can you and I hear the Shaytan when he whispers to us? When he pokes us. prods us. tempts us. can we hear him speak? We cannot! But ⟪ar:السمیع⟫ can hear. You and I cannot hear. Even though a Shaytan a Jinn is whispering to us. we cannot directly hear anything. the mental thought of that evil he is proding us with. comes in our minds. the evil thought he is blowing into us. that comes in our mind. but we do not actually hear him speaking. But a ⟪ar:السمیع⟫can hear him in the very act. So when se say:

⟪ar-quote:أعوذ باللہ السمیع⟫

We acknowledge that Oh Allah. I cannot hear Shaytan. But YOU CAN. because you are ⟪ar:السمیع⟫ . and that's why YOU can protect me when Shaytan whispers to me.

and then we say ⟪ar:العلیم⟫. because Allah knows everything. What does he know in this case? He knows the level of our sincerity. our ⟪ar:اخلاص!⟫ He knows that when we recite the ⟪ar:أستعاذہ⟫. are we saying it with sincerity?. or is it just a parroted phrase that rolls off our tongue without any comprehension or intention of actually seeking His protection?. Allah ⟪ar:العلیم⟫ know whether we truly intend to turn towards him for protection or not. because He knows what's in our heart. He knows if we truly want to submit ourselves before his majesty.or if we are just saying it for the sake of saying it.  And only when the ⟪ar:علیم⟫finds us to be sincere. the ⟪ar:سمیع⟫protects us from the whispers of Shaytan.

Therefore when we recite the ⟪ar:أستعاذہ⟫. we should make sure we say it sincerely. and with the intention of actually seeking Allah's protection . We shouldn't make these merely parroting phrases that roll of our tongues without meaning. and the need for his protection must come from the heart . with sincerity. because he is ⟪ar:السمیع العلیم⟫.
