<!-- section 4 (id=5721, raw_sort=4): SUAH Al-FALAQ -->
### Review

We're studying the Istiaaza. اعوذ باللہ من الشیطان الرجیم

We studied the words Aoozu and Shaytan and Rajeem. We saw the difference between the words Shaytan and Iblees. Shaytan comes from the adjective Shatana. which means the one that is far removed. and so this adjective. this label applies to anyone. whether human or Jinn. anyone who is far removed from the mercy of Allah is called Shaytan.  We studied that Rajeem means someone who is cast away. stoned away. pelted away. is called Rajeem. So Shaytan by his NATURE is far removed from Allah's mercy. and he is Rajeem. He is pelted away. cast away because of his actions. In contrast to that. Iblees is actually an entity. He was the angel that refused the command of Allah. He refused to prostrate to Adam AS because of his pride and arrogance. and his underlying jealousy against Adam AS. And that's what earned him the name Iblees. Iblees comes from the word Ablasaa.  which means "despair". He completely gave up hope in the mercy of Allah. and that's what made him Iblees.  Iblees gave up hope in the mercy of Allah. And because of that what he wants? He wants to have everyone far removed from the same mercy of Allah. that he gave up hope in. So the goal of Iblees. is to create an army of Shayateen. An army of people who will be far removed from Allah's mercy (Shaytan).  and pelted away because of their dispicable actions (rajeem).

So the Istiaaza.  is our seeking Allahs  protection from all Shayateen. And from that we came to the two words. ⟪ar:مستعاذ بہ⟫ and ⟪ar:مستعاذ منہ⟫

Mustaaz Bihi. Seeking protection OF. meaning Allah

Mustaaz Minhu. Seeking protection FROM . meaning Shaytan AlRajeem.  So we are running FROM the Shaytan.  and we are running TO the protection of Allah. 

And then we have two Surahs. Surah AlFalaq and Surah AlNaas.  that are the surahs explaining the استعاذہ . These two surahs explain what exactly we are seeking protection from and what does it mean to actually seek the protection of Allah.

Surah AlNaas is primarily Mustaaz Bihi.  because Allah is mentioned 3 times. and protection from evil is mentioned once. Whereas we saw Surah Falaq is primarily Mustaaz Minhu. because Allah is mentioned once. and protection from evil is mentioned 3 times. So there is this beautiful symmety and prefection that we see between the two surahs.

Then we looked at the historical background of why these surahs were revealed. They were revealed together. first Surah AlFalaq and then Surah AlNaas. And it was revealed as an antidote for the magic that was perfomed on Rasul Allah (SAS) by Lubaid Ibn Asim and his daughters.  These Surahs are basically Allah stepping forward. to protect His beloved messenger. Muhammad Mustafa SAS. against the evil of the kuffar and mushrikeen.

---

Now lets start linguistically analysing Surah AlFalaq. Allah says. ⟪ar:قل أعوذ برب الفلق⟫

We've already looked at the word ⟪ar:أعوذ⟫. but lets just go over it again and then look at the word falaq. and then come back to Qul .

So the word ⟪ar:أعوذ⟫has several forms in morphology as we saw previously. ⟪ar:أعاذ، یعیذُ⟫ . you can say ⟪ar:یعوِّذ، تعویذ، أستعیذ⟫  so several forms are used. even in the Quran. for example

⟪ar-quote:فَإِذَا قَرَأْتَ ٱلْقُرْآنَ فَٱسْتَعِذْ بِٱللَّهِ مِنَ ٱلشَّيْطَنِ ٱلرَّجِيمِ⟫

Similarly Hazrat Maryam Salamullah Alaiha says.⟪ar-quote:وَإِنِّىٓ أُعِيذُهَا بِكَ وَذُرِّيَّتَهَا مِنَ ٱلشَّيْطَنِ ٱلرَّجِيمِ⟫

So there are many variations of this word. But the root word ⟪ar:عاذ⟫means to seek spiritual protection of a diety. It also means to cling to someone for protection or to hold on to someone and not let go of them.  out of the fear of something dangerous that is unseen. Like a child when it wakes up from a nightmare and clings to its mother. So it means to cling to someone out of fear of the unseen. The key word here is unseen. Dangers that are unseen.

If you want protection from an enemy that is attacking you , then the word is ⟪ar:أجارۃ⟫. ⟪ar:أجارۃ⟫ means to give protection to someone against a physical enemy.  a seen enemy. but for unseen elements like jealously. sorcery. satanic whispers. these kinds of things   the word is ⟪ar:استعاذ⟫. Hence

⟪ar:أعوذ باللہ من الشیطان الرجیم⟫

We seek Allah's protection.  ⟪ar:أعوذ باللہ⟫   against an enemy that cannot be seen. And it is also used in the meaning of clinging on to someone and not letting go of them.

We also have the word  ⟪ar:معاذ⟫. ⟪ar:معاذ is⟫ a place where you can find refuge. You might have heard معاذ اللہ . Means a place. a very secure place that has the protection of Allah from the unseen. This word was used by Yousuf AS.

⟪ar-quote:وَرَوَدَتْهُ ٱلَّتِى هُوَ فِى بَيْتِهَا عَن نَّفْسِهِۦ وَغَلَّقَتِ ٱلْأَبْوَبَ وَقَالَتْ هَيْتَ لَكَ ۚ قَالَ مَعَاذَ ٱللَّهِ⟫

When Zulekha closed the doors on him and trapped him. he said ⟪ar:معاذ اللہ⟫ . He seeked refuge of Allah for a place that could protect him from the evil intentions of this woman. so he said ⟪ar:معاذ اللہ⟫

Now. Why do linguists have a problem with the translation "I seek refuge" for the translation of أعوذ باللہ. They disagree with that translation. because if you say ⟪ar:أعوذ باللہ⟫ means I seek refuge. then how do you translate ⟪ar:أَستَعِیذُ⟫. ??

⟪ar:أستعاذا⟫in arabic means to seek. Therefore ⟪ar:أَستَعِیذُ⟫ means I seek refuge. So then what does ⟪ar:أعوذ⟫ mean?  Linguists say that ⟪ar:عاذ⟫actually means.  I am entering into the refuge. I am giving myself into the refuge of Allah.  I'm not just seeking it. Its not that I just want it. I am actually giving myself. I am surrendering myself to it. From a linguistic perspective.  it is an act of complete submission when you say ⟪ar:اعوذ⟫. You are saying I have no power to protect myself . I am therefore giving myself up to Allah (AWJ) for protection. It's one thing to say I want to do that. It would be a good idea to do that. But its a completely different thing to openly declare that I am in fact doing it. I am giving myself up to Allah for protection. because I cannot do it myself. You understand? 

⟪ar:أَستَعِیذُ باللہ⟫ means I am seeking Allah's protection. I want Allah's protection. But أعوذ means I not only want it. I'm not only seeking it. I am actually giving myself up. I am surrendering myself to Allah's protection. So Allah say in the Quran.

⟪ar-quote:فَٱسْتَعِذْ بِٱللَّهِ مِنَ ٱلشَّيْطَنِ ٱلرَّجِيمِ⟫

Seek protection from Shaytaan. and in response. we don't say OK. I'm seeking protection. we say.  ⟪ar:أعوذ باللہ من الشیطان الرجیم⟫. We say. I willingly and completely give myself up. I surrender. I submit myself  into the protection of Allah from Shaytaan.

---

### Falaq

So the first ayah says.
⟪ar-quote:قُلْ أَعُوذُ بِرَبِّ ٱلْفَلَقِ⟫
Say! I am surrendering myself for protection to the master of Al-Falaq.  Now lets look at this beautiful word Falaq. and linguists say that  Falaq is actually a cause of the word "Khalaq". which means creation.  They both are from the same phoenotic pattern. Falaq and khalaq. And so Falaq results in. or causes.  Khalaq.  And what is the next ayah we find in the Surah? ⟪ar:من شر ما؟ خلق⟫. SubhanAllah

Let me explain how the two are related.

The word Falaqa in arabic . literally means to rip something open. To tear something open such that something else comes out from inside. So if I tear open a pillow and the fluff comes out? That's falaqa. Falaq is used for the morning or daybreak because the rays of the sun literally tear through the darkness of the night . and morning comes out. that's why its called falaq. You understand? It cracks and rips through the darkness that's why its called day break.

So falaq means to rip through and then what comes out is creation. Khalaq. SubhanAllah. So Khalaq proceeds Falaq.

So Falaq is.  for example when a seed . slowly rips open and a plant comes out. Allah says ⟪ar:فالق الحب⟫ same root world . He says ⟪ar:فالق الحب و النوا⟫ . The one who tears open the seed. ⟪ar:و النوا⟫ which means the seed of a date . which is called ⟪ar:نوا⟫and when that tears open.  then the tree starts coming out of that. Allah says ⟪ar:فالق الحب و النوا⟫

Similarly the one who brings the morning out. ⟪ar:فالق الاصباح⟫ is used in the Quran as well. The night literally rips open and the day comes out. We use this word in our tasbeeh after Istamsaktu of the sunnat of Fajar

⟪ar:سبحان رب الصباح و **فالق**الاصباح⟫

Perfect is the master of morning and the one who rips open the night and brings out the morning.

So you see how beautiful this relationship is between Falaq and Khalaq? Between ripping open and creation? Because everything that is created.  is a result of something that tears open. SubhanAllah! Something that tears open

⟪ar:ما یخرج من اصلٍ کل عیون من الجبال⟫

What comes out from something else. for example springs that come out of a mountain. thats falaq also. the springs tear out of the mountain. and water comes out.

⟪ar:والامطار من السحاب⟫

and rain . ripping out of the clouds. it tears through the clouds and comes down that is also part of falaq

⟪ar:والنبات من الارض⟫

and plants ripping out of the ground. tearing the ground open and coming out.

⟪ar:والاولاد من الارحام⟫

and childrent that come out of the womb of their mother.

All acts of creation are a kind of tearing or ripping apart. through which the creation comes into existence. Like the big bang that exploded. it tore open. Singularity ripped open.  and this universe came into existence. that too is falaq. SubhanAllah

So Falaq is referring to everything that has been created that tears open. Even for example.  you study microscopic creatures that rip  that tear apart. like amoeba. and they split. This kind of tearing open happens in plants. in animals in microsopic organisms.  in the sky. Even in human beings. both in the physical as well as spiritual sense. Physically Allah tears us out of the womb of our mothers. But also Allah's guidance rips open the veils of disbelief and arrogance.  and revals the truth to the one who wishes to believe. He tears down the walls of problems and restraints. and takes the believer out of it into comfort and ease. from confusions and indecisions to clarity.  just as the dark night tears open and the day comes out. All of that is also implied in the word Falaq.

So now if you look at it from a literary stand point. Allah is saying that he is the master of birth. He owns it. He is the master of all kinds of birth and creation. Because falaq is talking about birth. It is talking about creation.The birth of the morning. the birth of a child. .the birth of a plant. the birth of an animal. the birth of rain from the cloud.

Now I want to show you how these two surahs are connected with the previous Surah. Surah AlIkhlaas. As I said earlier. There is a connection between all of these surahs as one flows into the next.  So in Surah Ikhlaas. what claim did allah (AWJ) make? ⟪ar:لم یلد ولم یولد⟫ .  He did not give birth. Nobody gave birth to him. Rather he owns the creation of birth. He is not limited by it.  because he is the master of the creation itself. He created the process of creation. which is science in my ways. Creation has nothing to do with his own existence. He is above and beyond it. So ⟪ar:رب الفلق⟫is the continuity of that subject.

Then there is the word ⟪ar:الصمد⟫. ⟪ar:الصمد⟫is someone that everyone else is in need of and he is in need of no one. Everyone needs ⟪ar:الصمد⟫and ⟪ar:الصمد⟫needs no one. That is ⟪ar:الصمد⟫.

⟪ar:صمد الیہ⟫  in Arabic is used when you turn to someone in complete desperation. It is a situation in which you need them. but and they don't need you.  Now in these 2 surahs are we desperately turning to Allah for protection? yes we are! Does Allah need our or anyone else's protection? No he doesn't! What does that make him then? ⟪ar:الصمد⟫! We have a need that we cannot fulfill ourself.  so we are asking for Allah's proteciton. SubhanAllah! So these two surah's are also.,. in many ways.  a practical manifestation of what it means to say ⟪ar:اللہ الصمد⟫. Because in Surah Ikhlaas ⟪ar:اللہ الصمد⟫ is a theorotical notion describing who Allah is. But with in Surah AlNaas and Falaq there is a practical manifestations of our declration of our need for his protection and our desperation . when allah says he is ⟪ar:الصمد⟫. in theory that means we are in need of him and he does not need us. But when we say ⟪ar:اعوذ برب الفلق⟫  .  I am giving myself up. I am surrendering myself to the master of Falaq. Then I am practically acknowledging my need for him.  My need for him and His Sufficiency without me. His ⟪ar:صمدیت⟫.  That seed.  that lesson that was taught in surah Ikhlaas. is now giving us its practical fruits in Surah Falaq and naas

Then there are several other implications of the word falaq.⟪ar:وَسعۃ بعد الضیق⟫

If you look at the entire theme of this surah it is related to darkness. It talks about the night and the things that happen in the night.  Night is considered a time of fear. darkness is associated with evil. Black magic is something dark. that implies someone wants to harm you. . Jealously is a dangerous emotion. that can cause a great deal of harm. So all these darknesses and evils mentioned in the surahs create a sense of ⟪ar:ضیق⟫. you feel constricted. And by Allah saying ⟪ar:قل أعوذ برب الفلق⟫ .  He is saying. when you feel this way. when your heart feels constricted because of whatever difficult situation you're in. come under my protection. Surrender yourself to me. I will take care of you. Because I am ⟪ar:رب الفلق⟫.  I am the master of Falaq. I will rip through. and tear through whatever problems you are facing . It is as though Allah is saying. I will provide you with openness and relaxation when you feel constricted and tight. So it's like we were imprisoned. we are constrained by our problems. our confusions. our indecisions. our procrastinations.  and we call upon Allah the master of Falaq. The one who tears things open.  He will tear open our constriction and brings us out of it to give us relaxation and create expansion for us. SubhanAllah!!

Also ⟪ar:الظلمات الی النور⟫ . This Surah talks about Sharr (evil) from beginning to end. In almost every literature in the world. evil is associated with darknes. For example if someone says he has evil intentions. many literatures will say he has dark intentions. he has a dark mind. he has a dark personality. Darkness is associated with evil. in virtually any literature in the world. And that is true with Arabic as well. So just by using the word Sharr. the Surah tacks on another dark tinge to it. Its already talking about the night and darkness.  and then on top of that. evils within the dark nights.  So Allah says.

⟪ar:من شر غاسق اذا وقب⟫ .  literally the mention of night and darkness. then another kind of darkness. ⟪ar:و من شر النفاثت فی العقد⟫ . Black magic. And then the darkness of the jealous when he is acting out his jealousy. How is jealousy associated with darkness? Because the one who is jealous will always act behind your back. They will always work in the shadows. never openly. You will remain in the dark. So Allah mentions 3 kinds of darkness in this surah. You know what other word is associated with darkness? Shirk! Associating partners with Allah.

In the words of Hazrat Luqmaan.

⟪ar-quote:يَبُنَىَّ لَا تُشْرِكْ بِٱللَّهِ ۖ إِنَّ ٱلشِّرْكَ لَظُلْمٌ عَظِيمٌۭ⟫

Oh my sons. do not associate partners with Allah. Shirk. Associating partners with Allah is the greatest darkness of all. but look at the word he used . ⟪ar:ظلم عظیم⟫ . the word used is Zulm. Injustice. which is the same root word for  ⟪ar:ظلمات⟫. darkness.

So the surah talks about darkness. And shirk is the greatest of all darkness. Now what is shirk? Isn't it the absence of tawheed? Just as darkness is the absence of light? Just as the word used for Shirk is Zulm (injustice or darkness). one of the words used for tawheed in the Quran is noor. The word NOOR is used for the tawheed of Allah.

So Shirk is a darkness and it is the greatest of injustice with Allah.  And Allah says.

⟪ar-quote:ٱللَّهُ وَلِىُّ ٱلَّذِينَ آمَنُوا۟ يُخْرِجُهُم مِّنَ ٱلظُّلُمَتِ إِلَى ٱلنُّورِ⟫

Allah is the friend of believers. he guides them from darkness to light. from shirk to tawheed.

⟪ar-quote:وَٱلَّذِينَ كَفَرُوٓا۟ أَوْلِيَآؤُهُمُ ٱلطَّغُوتُ يُخْرِجُونَهُم مِّنَ ٱلنُّورِ إِلَى ٱلظُّلُمَتِ⟫

And the rebellious shaytaan is the friend of disbelievers. he misleads them from light to darkness from tawheed to shirk.

Then again ⟪ar:من شر حاسد اذا حسد⟫. Jealousy. again a dark emotion. Its a Zulma. its a darkness.

So this entire surah has this imagery of darkness . and Allah begins this surah by ripping and tearing through the darkness and bringing light. and he does all of this with one word AlFalaq! So we call upon the lord who creates the brightness of the day. by ripping through all these elements of darkness that we are afflicted by. What a beautiful contrast presented in this surah with just one word AlFalaq.

So you see. how this Surah begins with surrending ourselves willingly to the protection of Rabb AlFalaq. It starts with قل أعوذ برب الفلق . Say I am surrendering myself to the master of Falaq! And then Falq. which means ripping and tearing through the darkness and bringing light. is then connected with all the remaining ayats

⟪ar:من شر ما خلق⟫

From the evil of all that was created. the master of Falaq will rip those evils and bring you out of it.

⟪ar:و من شر غاسق اذا وقب⟫

From the evil of the dark night. the master of Falaq will rip all those evils and bring you out of it.

⟪ar:من شر النفثات فی العقد⟫

From the evil of those that blow on knots. from the evil of black magic. the master of Falaq will rip through that magic. and take you out of it.

⟪ar:و من شر حاسد اذا حسد⟫

From the evil of the jealous when he acts out on his jealousy. the master of Falaq will rip through the harm of that jealousy and bring you out of it.

So the relation of Rabb AlFalaq with all these different kinds of evils.  Allah says that when they surround you. if you come into my protection. If you surrender yourself into my protection . I will tear open these evils and take you out of them. SubhanAllah

Then a final hadees about the word Falaq. This is a hadees in which a sahabee recited Surah Alfalaq to Rasul Allah (SAS). After he completed the recitation Rasul Allah asked him.

⟪ar:ھل تدری ما الفلق؟⟫ do you know what AlFalaq means? And then Rasul Allah himself answered

⟪ar-quote:بابٌ فی النَّار، اِذاَ فُتِحَت سُیِّرَت جھنَّم⟫. it is a door is hell fire. when it is opened. the entire hell fire gets ablazed . the flames get excited . It is one of the doors in hell fire. Again there is the imagery of the door that tears open. and then literally all hell breaks loose. Another hadees syas

⟪ar-quote:ھُوَ سِجنٌ فی جھنم، یُحبَثُ فیہِ الجبَّارُون و المتکبرون ۔۔ و اِنَّ جھنَّمَ تَتَعَوَّذُ بِی اللہ مِنہُ⟫

AllahuAkbar!! This falaq that Allah takes mastery and lordship over . the messenger says. it is a prison in jahannam. it is a prison in hell fire. In it are all the tyrants and the arrogant people.  and it is so terrible that hell fire itself seeks refuge of ALlah from this Falaq! That's how horrible that place is.

Now the question is why use this word falaq. It has all those literary meanings that we talked about and how it brings relief. but now it also seems that the word falaq is delivering punishement. the question is punishment for who? This surah . is a surah that is not just dedicated to seeking refuge. but it is also a surah dedicated to describing certain kinds of criminals. certain kinds of criminals who engage in the acts of sharr. committing the acts of various evils. There are many kinds of evils.  but in particular what ashraar are mentioned? the onest that are mentioned specifically are . sorcery (⟪ar:النفاثات فی العقد⟫), and jealousy (⟪ar:حاسد اذا حسد⟫).

⟪ar:غاسق اذا وقب⟫ is just a generic statement. the dark night may or may not be evil. because we know there are auspicious nights as well. Lailatul Qadr. Lailatul Mubaraka. so night can be good as well as bad. but sorcery and jealousy are ALWAYS ALWAYS categorically evil. So what we are learning is that on one hand. Falaq is a release. a breakthrough . a relief. a comfort for those that become victims of evil. But on the other hand for those people who engage in these acts. of black magic and jealousy.  or act out on them. then AlFalaq is a severe punishment for them. because Allah is the master of Al-Falaq. so not only is the crime mentioned . but hte punishment worthy of that crime is also mentioned . in the beginning of this surah.

So it is a glad tidings for the victims of evil. So if someone is performing black magic on us. or acting out their jealousies against us.  then this Surah brings glad tidings. happy news for us. that don't worry. Surrender yourself to me. to Rabb AlFalaq. Your master of Falaq. and I will take care of you. But if we are someone is engaged in these crimes of evil. then this same surah is a severe warning for them. it is a threat from Allah. because AlFalaq is also the door to blazing hell fire.

⟪ar:اللھم لا تجعلنا من الظالمین⟫

---

### Qul

Now lets talk about the word Qul. It's all over the Quran. [4 surahs]. You know what so amazing about it? It has a different literary context in every ayah that it is used in. There are something that are very common about the word Qul. but then there are things very particular to the context in which it is used. So now let's look at the benefits of the word Qul in the ⟪ar:معوذتین⟫.

 Notice that both these surahs start with the word Qul. Which.  from a linguistic stand point is a command. It's called ⟪ar:حرف الامر⟫ . It has an invisible exclamation mark in front of it. Say! This is a direct command to Rasul Allah. and by extension it is a command to all of us . It is a remedy for him.  and through him it becomes a remedy for all of us.

Now why did Allah want to give this command? 

He did so because he wants human begins to announce and admit their weakness with their tongues. It is one thing to realize that I'm weak. it is another to admit it. and announce it. Now when you announce your weakness. is it an act of arrogance or humility? Its an act of humility. It is an act of declaring.  I have no power. I am powerless . I need your protection. Now isn't it possible that somebody needs protection.  but their ego comes in the way? and they don't ask? They really want and need the protection.  but they don't ask because their ego gets in the way.  or even when they ask they don't say it out loud. they softly suggest it. under their breadth. Why? Because they are too embaressed to say it out loud. because when they say it out loud . it exposes how weak they are. So Allah says I want you to expose.  how weak you are to yourselves.  I want you to get rid of every ounce of arrogance that may exist inside you.  The word Qul remove from us arrogance. it removes from us what is called ⟪ar:استغنا⟫.

So let's look at the advantages of this word Qul. Because making this announcement of our need before Allah.  out loud.  is important for several reasons. In that declaration the first thing is the murder of our being impressed with ourselves. It kills our ego when we admit before Allah. I am submitting to YOUR protection.  It kills our ego.  and your false sense of . you know. I don't need any protection. I can deal with everything without Allah . It remove the fall pretenses of our capabilities and strength. It gets it out of your system.  Because having that false sense of protetion is a kind of shirk and arrogance. because Allah says.

⟪ar-quote:كَلَّآ إِنَّ ٱلْإِنسَنَ لَيَطْغَىٰٓ۔  أَن رَّآهُ ٱسْتَغْنَىٰٓ⟫

The human being truly rebels because he thinks he does not have any needs. So Allah says . QUL. declare openly that you have a need. This ensures your sincerity.

**Command**

The second thing is that Qul. is a command. So when we say Qul. when we actually accept and declare our weakness and incapability. we have now actively obeyed a command of Allah . Because the word "Rabb" necessitates the existence of an authority. You obey him because he is your Rabb. because He is your master. Now why is that important? And this is really important to understand.

It is important.  because how can it be.  that we are asking Allahs help.  while disobeying him? If I am constantly disobeying Allah. how can I ask Allahs for his help. We would never ask anybodys help.  while disobeying them and disregarding them at the same time. What we are learning here in the word Qul.  is that if we really want Allah to protect us. what must we be doing first? you must be obeying him! So the discussion begins with the comamnd of allah . and we complying with that command. and what that does.  is that it neccessitates in us the need to be in obedience to Allah. so that the proteciton can actually come to us. We are entering not only into the protection of Allah. but also into the obedience of ALlah.

And that is why Moosa (AS) through these words explains this concept. The concept of someone who kills their ego by seeking Allahs' protection. Isn't that what we're trying to do? We try to connect 2 things.  Surrendering ourselves to Allah's refuge means killing our ego. what does Moosa AS say?

⟪ar-quote:وَقَالَ مُوسَىٰٓ إِنِّى عُذْتُ بِرَبِّى وَرَبِّكُم مِّن كُلِّ مُتَكَبِّرٍۢ لَّا يُؤْمِنُ بِيَوْمِ ٱلْحِسَابِ ‎⟫

No doubt about it . I surrender myself for protection to my master. and I seek refuge from my master and yours.  from every single one.  posessed with arrogance.

This ayah connects 2 things together. seeking refuge and what? arrogance! and then he says.   ⟪ar-quote:لَّا يُؤْمِنُ بِيَوْمِ ٱلْحِسَابِ⟫   the one who does not believe in the day of judgment. the day of audit. the day of standing before Allah and presenting his case. This also tells us that not accepting our weakness. and not surrending ourselves to the protection of Allah.  directly to do with a lack of Emaan. a lack of faith. Because remember what did Rasul Allah say about Falaq in the context of punishment?

⟪ar-quote:ھُوَ سِجنٌ فی جھنم، یُحبَثُ فیہِ الجبَّارُون و المتکبرون⟫

It is a prison in jahannam. it is a prison in hell fire. In it are all the tyrants and the arrogant people. So If we do accept our weakness. and if we do not relaize a sincere need for Allah's protection. I don't need anyone to protect me! My money can protect me. My power can protect me. My family can protect me. This mountain can protect me. My knowledge can protect me. My government can protect me. If we have these egocentric mentality. then that makes us among the arrogant and it makes us among the tyrants. because that is the very thought process of a tyrant. of a Jabbar. and it's the very thought process of an arrogant mind. AlMutakkabir

⟪ar:اللھم لا تجعلنا من الجبارون و المتکبرون⟫

So this surah. Surah ALFalaq is a source of protection for the one who squashes his ego.  and openly declares his need for the protection of Allah. all covered by the word QUL. and then he understands that he is a helpless victim of various dark evils that he has no control over. He realizes he is weak. he is helpless. and so he willingly surrenders himself to the protection of Rabb AlFalaq. who tears open. rips open darkness.  and brings forth the day . who rips and tears through the veils and prisons of depression. confusion. stress. hopelessness. constrictions. and then brings out clarity. happiness. relif and expansion for us.

And at the same time this very same surah is a warning of a horrible and painful punishment in the next life. against those who commit the evils of sorcery and jealousy. again with the use of the same word AlFalaq . May Allah make us among those who genuinely surrender themselves to the refuge of ALlah and seek it sincerely.

---

### SHARR

Then the word Sharr. You know there are 3 words in the Quran that are used for "bad" . there is the word ⟪ar:شر⟫. , there is the verbal form ⟪ar:بِأسَ⟫and there is the word ⟪ar:ساءَ⟫. and then there are different variations of these words. Now any of these words could have been used here. But why Sharr specifically?

Now whats the difference between them? First of all.  from a vocabulary point of view they have different antonyms. They have different opposites

⟪ar:شر⟫is the opposite of ⟪ar:خیر⟫. and I'll define that in detail at the end. Last talk about ⟪ar:بِأسَ⟫first. ⟪ar:بِأسَ⟫is actually when you feel something is detestable or dispicable and terrible.  then you call it ⟪ar:بِأسَ⟫. For example you drink something and you go Awww. Thooooo. and you say this is a terrible drink. you say ⟪ar:بأس الشراب⟫ .  That would be ⟪ar:بأس الشراب⟫. But if you drink something that is delicious and awesome you would say ⟪ar:نعم الشراب⟫ . So the opposite of ⟪ar:بِأسَ⟫ is ⟪ar:نعم⟫. and it is used as an expression of either being.  extremely impressed with something ⟪ar:نعم⟫. or extremely disgusted by something  with ⟪ar:بِأسَ⟫.

Then theres the word ⟪ar:ساءَ⟫. it refers to something being not just extremely evil but also ugly. and its opposite is ⟪ar:حَسُنَ⟫. 

⟪ar-quote:وَسَآءَتْ مَصِيرًا⟫

⟪ar-quote:وَحَسُنَ أُو۟لَٓئِكَ رَفِيقًۭا⟫

⟪ar:ساءَ⟫ actually means deformed. disfigured. hideous. so the actions that are ugly and hideous in and of itself are called ⟪ar:سیئات⟫. the actions itself are ugly. A⟪ar:سَیِّئَا⟫ could be for example gossiping. doing gheeba. its an ugly act. through and through its ugly.  its a horrible terrible thing to do. so its called a ⟪ar:سَیِّئَا⟫

Now lets turn to the word ⟪ar:شر⟫. ⟪ar:شر⟫is something that is universally and unanimously understood as harmful or evil.  Specifically ⟪ar:شر⟫refers to something that will cause someone harm. OK?  ⟪ar:شر⟫is that which will cause someone harm.⟪ar:شَرَارَا⟫ in arabic is the spark of a flame that can burn you.  you know when a big fire is burning. these sparks and flames can come out sometimes.  and they can land on your skin and burn you. that's called ⟪ar:شَرَارَا⟫. So ⟪ar:شر⟫is literally that.  which causes somebody harm. Now the ayats in these surahs are profound.  and very explicit in declaring.

⟪ar-quote:مِن شَرِّ مَا خَلَقَ⟫

⟪ar-quote:وَمِن شَرِّ غَاسِقٍ إِذَا وَقَبَ⟫

⟪ar-quote:وَمِن شَرِّ ٱلنَّفَّثَتِ فِى ٱلْعُقَدِ ‎⟫

⟪ar-quote:وَمِن شَرِّ حَاسِدٍ إِذَا حَسَدَ⟫

⟪ar-quote:مِن شَرِّ ٱلْوَسْوَاسِ ٱلْخَنَّاسِ⟫

Surrendering to the protection of the master of AlFalaq and AnNaas . from what? from the evil. from the harm. from the ⟪ar:شر⟫. of that which got created.

⟪ar-quote:مِن شَرِّ مَا خَلَقَ⟫

This ayah is the translated the worst of all. It is translated as from the evil of that which HE created. This is the most horrible translation and the most unjust translation ever. Evil that He meaning Allah created.  Allah did not create evil. He did not create ⟪ar:شر⟫. He is the source of nothing but ⟪ar:خیر⟫. He is the source of all good that exists.

It is human freedom of choice. It is deviation of human emotions from good.  that created evil. Allah granted freedom of choice to his creation. And using that freedom of choice. it is his creation that created evil. Because what is evil? It is the absence of good! Allah did not create Iblees. He had created an angel. But then that angel because jealous of Adam AS. He became arrogant thinking .  ⟪ar:خلقتنی من نار و خلقتہ من تین⟫ . I am created from fire. Adam is created from clay.  Therefore ⟪ar:انا خیر منہ⟫. I am better than him. It was the choice of that angel.  that turned him into Iblees. Allah never created Iblees.

And that is the evil we seek Allah's protection from. Protection from the evil of his creation. Because the harm and evil is caused by the creation. And that's why we turn towards the protection of the Rabb of creation. Rabb AlFalaq and Rabb AnNaas. because the one who created the creation.  is more powerful than the creation. and therefore HE can protect us from it. He can save us from their harm. Because in the end. Allah alone is the master of the creation. Creation that is trying to cause harm by doing evil.  Allah has power over all creation. therefore he also has power over the harm that his creation is capable of producing.

So the ⟪ar:شر⟫in these ayats are not attributed to Allah. it is attributed to his creation. The bottom line in islamic studies. when it comes to the concept of ⟪ar:شر⟫. is that evil is not actually an entity in and of itself . it is only considered the lack of good.  Just like darkness . the imagery of tawheed and shirk. darkness and light. Darkness actually does not exist. there is no physics or chemistry of darkness. What actually exists is light. When you don't have light.  what do you have? you have darkness. . So darkness in and of itself is not an actual entity . its goodness that is the entity and a lack of goodness is what evil is. Therefore evil in the end is nothing. but a lack of good! You understand?

But this ayah has profound lessons in it because allah left the language open and universal. When he said ⟪ar:مِن شَرِّ مَا خَلَقَ⟫ he did not reduce it to shayaateen. to devils. 

The evil in the next surah is ⟪ar:من شر الوسواس الخناس⟫  talks about very specific creation. but when he said  ⟪ar:مِن شَرِّ مَا خَلَقَ⟫. He said . whatever was created. From the harm of whatever was created. You know what we learn from this? We learn that there is no creation.  on the face of this earth.  that comes without a flaw. the only one free of all flaw is Allah AWJ Himself. SubhanAllah! Every creation besides Allah has some inherent flaw in it.  They will have something missing. Some element of ⟪ar:شر⟫is possible from everything.

Think of the most amazing creations of allah like the sun! So many many many benefits from the sun. but are there harms as well?  Yes there are. Do people die because of sun stroke? Do plants get destroyed because of excessive heat? It's benefits are beyond measure. but then it can cause harm as well.

There are SO many benefits from water. but can water cause harm and damage as well? Floods? Sunamis?

There are SO many benefits in the earth. but are there harms in the earth too?

SO many benefits of the sky. are there harms that come down from the sky also?

So Everything that Allah has created.  has an element of harm.  of ⟪ar:شر⟫in it.  So we ask allah (AWJ) to proect us from the potential harmful elements of everything . things that are above and beyond our perceptions. you know a car. very benefecial for human beings. but can it be harmful? Can you die in a car accident? Can you get injured? That's all possible. So every element evey creation has that element of harm in it . so we ask Allah for his protection from all possible harm.  from all his creation. ⟪ar:مِن شَرِّ مَا خَلَقَ⟫

---

### GHASAQ

Then Allah says.  ⟪ar:وَمِن شَرِّ غَاسِقٍ إِذَا وَقَبَ⟫

In arabic literature ⟪ar:غَسَق⟫ is considered ⟪ar:اول الیل⟫ . the first part of the night.  In other words when the blue of the sky is gone and its all black now. thats ⟪ar:غَسَق⟫.  Allah says

⟪ar-quote:أَقِمِ ٱلصَّلَوٰةَ لِدُلُوكِ ٱلشَّمْسِ إِلَىٰ غَسَقِ ٱلَّيْلِ⟫

Allah says establish prayer from the setting of the sun till it gets deep into the night. that is ⟪ar:غَسَقِ ٱلَّيْلِ⟫.  Now the word ⟪ar:غَاسِقٍ⟫is also used in literature for that which sinks. or that which disappears. In that sense we find the word ⟪ar:غَسَق⟫used for even the sun and the moon.  for example ⟪ar:غسق القمر⟫ . when there is a lunar ecliplse. its called ghasaq alqamar.  ⟪ar:غَسَقَتْ عَیْنُہُ⟫ and the eyes became dark with tears.  when you cry too much and your eyes have bags around them. its called ⟪ar:غسق العیُون⟫

⟪ar:غسقت السمآء⟫ . when the sky becomes really dark with clouds. when its day time but it feels like night time. and there is VERY heavy rain. thats called ⟪ar:غسقت السمآء⟫. So these expressions.  what are they telling us? Allah is referring to a time in the night when its completely and absolutely dark.  but he doesn't stop there. he goes a step further and says.  ⟪ar:إِذَا وَقَبَ⟫.

He begins the ayah by saying  ⟪ar:مِن شَرِّ غَاسِقٍ⟫  from the evil and harm of the dark night itself. meaning Allah is saying there is potential harm inherently present in  the dark itself.  RasulAllah would advise his sahaba to not go out in the night. He would say. if you knew what I know.  you would not step out in the night. The shayateen have congreations and meetings in the night. And even in our society today. When is it time to act like the devil? its friday and saturday night! Watch the documentaries that are done about the ERs in America. you know WHEN the ERs are filled? Friday and Saturday night! They are filled. Car accidents. people killing each other after a few beers. drugs. alcohol. rapes. All that evil occurs when?  at night! SubhanAllah. the potential of evil is far greater in the darkness of the night. and of course that's why its dangerous to travel at night. You probably won't go out late at night. You certainly wouldn't let your kids go out or stay out in middle of the night.  Its in human nature. So we ask allah to protect us from that dark evils in the night. the evil of ⟪ar:غسق⟫.

There is something interesting I want to share with you about ⟪ar:غسق⟫. Especially ⟪ar:غسق القمر⟫. When its used for moon eclipse.  You know. some very interesting studies have been done recently about the moon. . and this used be considered folk lore . but now there are actually studies about it. That when there is a full moon. it has an effect on the tides of the ocean. the tides of the ocean change. It becomes high tide.  and they gain this tendency to become violent.  Well the human body also has fluids inside it. So do you think the magnetic pull of the full moon has any affect on the human being? There are actually studies being done on this. There are poeple that tend to become more violent when its a full moon. You know that whole genre about mythical literature.  about werewolves and things like that. its a fanatasized version of these facts. you know . they are hyperbolee of actual scientific phenomenon. where people experience psychological changes and aggrevation during certain cycles of the moon. This is actually documented physiological behaviour. SubhanAllah! People start acting crazy. And thats actually where the english word lunatic comes form. you know like crazy. lunatic. It comes from lunar. even traditionally this was understood. SubhanAllah!

So Allah says ⟪ar:من شر غاسق⟫ . but then he adds on.  ⟪ar:إِذَا وَقَبَ⟫. Now what does ⟪ar:وَقَبَ⟫mean? Because in literature ⟪ar:وَقَبَ⟫is also a referrence to darkness. so its like saying. from the evil of the dark night when it gets dark.  But its already dark!!.  so whats this getting dark over again? and why a different word for it? because ⟪ar:وقب الظلام⟫. It means that the night gets so dark.  that things start become invisible. ⟪ar:وَقَبَ⟫is used when things get so dark. they become invisible. you know.  like there is a ditch inside a mountain at night. and something goes inside that ditch. in the middle of a dark night. Now you can't see it anymore. thats actually called ⟪ar:وَقَبَ⟫. so there are things hiding in the dark that we cannot see. This includes the shayateen. I told you ⟪ar:عاذ، استعاذ، أعوذ⟫ in arabic is used for seeking protection from things that are unseen. invisible. that you cannot see.  So the ayah is using relevant and perfect language by saying.  we're seeking refuge from the evils of the dark night.  especially when it hides things inside it. when there are things lurking in the dark that we cannot see.

So we are asking protection for these kinds of things taht we do not have the ability to infer for ourself. and Allah teaches us about them.

---

### وَمِن شَرِّ ٱلنَّفَّثَتِ فِى ٱلْعُقَدِ ‎

This is specifically the context I mentioned to you. in the beginning. Allah called out ⟪ar:نفاثات⟫which is actually a feminine plural. In modern arabic this would mean. the woman who blow on knots. and scholars say this is attributed to Lubaid ibn Asim's daughters who blew spells on the knots. thats what it is referring to. But naffassat could be an adjective of ⟪ar:نُفُوس⟫or ⟪ar:أنفس⟫. meaning people! the word ⟪ar:نفس⟫in arabic is considered feminie. and its adjuecives are considered feminine too. now the word ⟪ar:نفاثات⟫. could also be referred to groups. because many times this sort of sorcery and dark magic.  things like that . these are done in groups. The word ⟪ar:نَفَثَ⟫. actually means to blow with a little bit of spit coming out. It's a soft. wet. blow.

If you blow really hard out of your mouth. the word is ⟪ar:نفخ⟫. like

⟪ar-quote:وَنُفِخَ فِى ٱلصُّورِ فَجَمَعْنَهُمْ جَمْعًۭا⟫

That is ⟪ar:نفخ⟫. when the root words are close in arabic. .the meanings are close in arabic too. ⟪ar:نَفَثَ⟫. this is sa. with 3 dots. but if you say ⟪ar:نَفَسَ⟫with a ⟪ar:س⟫. . that actually means breadth. ⟪ar:تَنَفَّسَ⟫means to draw breadth.

⟪ar:حیاتُکَ أَنفَاس⟫ the poet says. your life is nothing more than a set of breadths. You are going to take these breadths in and out.  and eventually it will all be done. so ⟪ar:نَفَثَ⟫. ⟪ar:نفخ⟫with a sa with 3 dotes and ⟪ar:نَفَسَ⟫ . with a seen. they all have shared meanings.

And BTW  ⟪ar:نفاثات⟫is the one who blows over and over and over again. engaging in the acts of trying to produce this magic ⟪ar:فی العقد⟫ into knots.

So we surrender to Allah from protection of those who perform magic. Now there are some very cool interpretations for the various words used in this ayah. So ⟪ar:ٱلنَّفَّثَتِ فِى ٱلْعُقَدِ⟫

Ones who blow on knots. So the knots exist first. and they then blow on them. and I just told you that  ⟪ar:نفاثات⟫is an act of blowing over and over and over again.Its not a one time thing.  If you just go Phooo.  that's not Nafasa. Nafasa suggests constant and repeated blowing. You understand? And blowing on what knots! ⟪ar:عُقَد⟫ . It is interpreted as those people who have the intention of creation constraints for someone. that's what knots are aren't they? Evil people who have the intention of trapping others in a situation. in an emotion. in a difficult position. That's all interpreted from ⟪ar:عُقَد⟫. And how do they do it. by constantly blowing on them. Meaning they are constantly gossipping. spreading rumors. poisoning minds of others. agasint a certain individual. in order to constrain . in order to restrict. Someone does not like someone. someone gets jealous of someone. they want to stop them from whatever they are doing. so what do they do? They try to create roadblocks. They try to stop them. And how do they do it? By quietly gossiping. instigating doubts in the minds of others. attcking their character. their knowledge. their credibility. in very very subtle ways. and over and over and over again. little by little every time.

*I mean well! I'm doing this for you.  I don't want you to get hurt by this person. I am looking out for you.*

SO all such gossip and rumors are presented for your benefit. but the goal is what? To turn you against the other person. And what happens is now you believe that it is YOU who does not like that person. You feel this sense of negativity coming from inside YOU. But it had nothing to do with you.  It was blown into you over and over and over again. until now you believe that you are the cause of that hatred. and then YOU end up creating the roadblock. YOU end up creating the obstacle. I really want you to take a moment and think about this. It was the other person who wanted to create the roadblock. It was the other person who wanted to stop this someone. But with his Naffasat fil Uqad. what does he do? He uses YOU to actually act it out for him. You end up being the one who actually CREATES the obstacles for this person. Isn't that what magic is? Does the person suffereing from magic know that he is a victim of magic? No he doesn't! He just starts feeling sick. He starts feeling ill. stressed. depressed. But all this time. it was the doing of someone else! Can you understand how sinister and horrible this evil is?⟪ar:نعوذ باللہ من ذالک⟫

May Allah protect us all from this.  This is why when you hear someone gossiping. you should put an end to it right there and then. And be aware of when this verbal magic is being done on you. Because the one who is instigating you against someone or something. against an elder. against religion. against duaat. that's exactly what he's doing. He is casting a spell on you. In order to do what? create problems and constraints and restrictions against the one he wants to harm. He will instigate. but you will become his hands! He will use you as his TOOLS to ACTUALLY perform the evil deed. He will use YOU to perform the actual evil. You will be the one to disobey the elder. to insult them. to be rude to them. You will be the one actually making fun of Islam. YOU will be the one Actually denying existence of Allah.

May Allah protect us all. first of all from committing this horrible evil act. and then from the effects of those who act in such ways against us.

---

### and the final part of it is : وَمِن شَرِّ حَاسِدٍ إِذَا حَسَدَ

Here you have to appreciate something.  You know.  there is always the problem and then there is the root of the problem.  The first part of the surah. dealt with problems. But this last ayah takes you to the root of the problem. Why would someone do magic against someone?  why would someon cast a spell on someone? Why would someone want to spread rumors and poison others against someone?  Why would soemone want to harm someone? Its jealousy! It is ALWAYS jealousy.  They don't want them to have what they have. they don't want them to succeed. they want them to fail. So the root of the problem is mentioned in the end. ⟪ar:وَمِن شَرِّ حَاسِدٍ إِذَا حَسَدَ⟫

Observe anyone who engages in the act of jeaoulsy. observe it when it manifets in you. It will always stem from you.  not being able to stand someone getting something better than you. Even at the lowest levels. A guy works as a janitor.  Another guy also works as a janitor. but he gets the metal broom and you get the plastic one. and now you want this guy fired. It could really be something pathetic like that. Or it could be about a land. money. wealth. woman.  It could be based on anything. Matters of inheritance. Matters of importance.  it could be anything. its all around us. Friends getting jealous of friends. Daughter in law getting jealous of in laws. Mother in laws getting jealous of daughter in laws. This is a REAL evil. .

I mean jealously not mother in laws.

Now its one thing to feel jealously inside . and there is another to act it out. To do something about. You know someone can feel jealous but then choose not to do something about it. I feel it but I'm not going to do anything about it. Do we say that? Have you heard others say that? .  Allah say if you actually have ⟪ar:حسد⟫inside you. . it is inevitable. that you will end up doing something bad. He didnt say.  ⟪ar:وَمِن شَرِّ حَاسِدٍ إِن حَسَدَ⟫.  From the evil of the jealous IF he acts on his jealousy. NO! He said ⟪ar:أذا حسد⟫ .  WHEN he acts out on his jealousy. Whats the differnece between IF and WHEN? If. . may or may not happen? What does WHEN mean? Its DEFINITELY going to happen. If there is a person who has ⟪ar:حسد⟫.  it will DEFINITELy manifest in one way or the other. whether it be the evil eye.  or manipulations.  or schemes.  or even in a conversation with someone else. it will surely manifest. And that's why we have to seek refuge from it.

Now if you notice ⟪ar:اذا حسد⟫ is redundant. Allah already said ⟪ar:وَمِن شَرِّ حَاسِدٍ⟫. From the evil of the jealous.  Why does he have to say from the evil of the jealous when he is acting out his jealousy.   Because ⟪ar:حسد⟫is a dormant quality. ⟪ar:حاسد⟫on the other hand. is an active quality. So this protection of Allah is not for the actual feeling of ⟪ar:حسد⟫.  its not for that feeling of dormant jealousy that a person feels. But it is for the active quality of ⟪ar:حاسد⟫. when he is actually acting out that jealousy. It is for when that droman trait.  is now manifesting itself. that's when we seek allahs' refuge.

Now. Putting this hasad in the generalized context of darkness that the surah started with. we learn something very interesting.Something we just talked about in the previous ayah.

That those who are jealous of you.  will never harm you in front of your face. They will always hide behind shadows and harm you. They will go behind your back. They will do it in ways that you will not even be able to tell who is doing it. UNSEEN again! SubhanAllah! You'll never see it coming. the guy sitting next to you could be jealous of you. He means you harm.  and you think he/she is your best friend. This again becomes  a harm that is unseen to you. that's why ⟪ar:اعوذ⟫is so perfect in this context! Because it is protection from a harm that is unseen.

Now when Allah already generalize all evils with ⟪ar:مِن شَرِّ مَا خَلَقَ⟫that why did he need to go into the specifics?  When he said ⟪ar:مِن شَرِّ مَا خَلَقَ⟫it already included all of these things!. Then whats the point of specifying all of these things?  This is Allah alerting us.  that these specific categories of evil.  are the greatest ones. So you say to allah (AWJ) that I want protection from all kinds of harms. especially these 3 biggies. The 3 big ones. The potential harms of the night.  the potential harm of people doing sorcery against me.  and the potential of the harm from the jealous when he is acting out his jealousy against me. These 3 are the big ones. so we ask allah for protection from all evils. specifically thse 3 big ones.

Now finally from a grammatical stand point. how come Allah put the ma'rifa. ⟪ar:ال⟫ only on the naffassat and not on any of the others?

⟪ar-quote:وَمِن شَرِّ غَاسِقٍ إِذَا وَقَبَ⟫

⟪ar-quote:وَمِن شَرِّ ٱلنَّفَّثَتِ فِى ٱلْعُقَدِ ‎⟫

⟪ar-quote:وَمِن شَرِّ حَاسِدٍ إِذَا حَسَدَ⟫

He did not put it on Gaasiq  ⟪ar:مِن شَرِّ غَاسِقٍ⟫  there is no AL-GHASIQ. Similary  ⟪ar:مِن شَرِّ حَاسِدٍ⟫no Al-Haasid. Only when he mentioned Sorcery he used the word AL. ⟪ar:شَرِّ**ٱل**نَّفَّثَتِ⟫

When do you use a definite article.?. When you want to make something specific. not just any book. but THE book. Why did I tell you these 2 surahs were revealed? They were revealed to solve which specific problem? The problem of sorcery that was done on Rasul Allah by Lubaid Ibn Asim.  This surah was not revealed to address the problem of the night specifically.  It was not revealed to address the problem of the jealous when he is acting out his jealousy specifically. This surah was revealed to address the problem of sorcery specifically so when he said

⟪ar:وَمِن شَرِّ ٱلنَّفَّثَتِ فِى ٱلْعُقَدِ⟫ ‎ Allah used the word AL. SubhanAllah! Can you appreciate the PERFECTION of this text?? SubhanAllah! Gives me goosebumps every single time!!.  And this all spoken text. its' not written or edited literature. How do you get this precision and perfection with spoken text?? AllahuAkbar!
