### من شر الوسواس الخناس

So now that we've talked about the protection OF part.
⟪ar-quote:قُلْ أَعُوذُ بِرَبِّ ٱلنَّاسِ مَلِكِ ٱلنَّاسِ إِلَهِ ٱلنَّاسِ⟫

Which to summarize is. ⟪ar-quote:قُلْ⟫ I openly declare. I put aside my ego. and I openly and willingly submit in obedience . ⟪ar-quote:أَعُوذُ⟫ for spiritual protection of my diety. ⟪ar-quote:بِرَبِّ ٱلنَّاسِ⟫ to the owner of people.,.  ⟪ar-quote:مَلِكِ ٱلنَّاسِ⟫. the king of people. ⟪ar-quote:إِلَهِ ٱلنَّاسِ⟫. the God of people. And now that I've submitted TO the protection of Allah. what am I seeking protection from?
⟪ar-quote:من شر الوسواس الخناس⟫

From the evil of the retreating whisperer . So there are two words here we need to understand. ⟪ar:الوسواس⟫the one who whispers and ⟪ar:الخناس⟫. the one who retreats.

Let's begin with ⟪ar:الوسواس⟫. the whisperER. And what does a whisperer do?.  He does  ⟪ar:وسوسۃ⟫. He whispers

Now. there is another word in arabic that is sued for whisper. and that is ⟪ar:ھمسۃ⟫. . which is also used in the Quran
⟪ar-quote:وَخَشَعَتِ ٱلْأَصْوَاتُ لِلرَّحْمَنِ فَلَا تَسْمَعُ إِلَّا هَمْسًۭا⟫

On that day of judgment. everyone will stand silent before AlRehman. and you will not hear anything except faint whisperings

Now the first question is what is the difference between ⟪ar:ھمسۃ⟫and⟪ar:وسوسۃ⟫?

The first difference is that the word ⟪ar:ھمسۃ⟫means to whisper anything.  it doesn't matter whether it is good or bad. I can whisper something good. or I could whisper something bad. So such a whisper. where the intention is irrelevant. the word ⟪ar:ھمسۃ⟫ is used.  But ⟪ar:وسوسۃ⟫is ONLY and ALWAYS used for evil whispering. You understand? ⟪ar:ھمسۃ⟫can be used for both good and evil whispering. but ⟪ar:وسوسۃ⟫is ONLY used for evil whispering. Thats the first difference.

The second difference is what is called.  ⟪ar:تکرار الَّفظ⟫. This may get a bit technical. but its a REALLY interesting science of the Arabic language. If there is a repetition of a syllable inside a word. it actually rhetorically alludes to the repition of the act itself. If a sound is repeated more than once in the word itself. then that alludes to the repetition of the act itself.  Now in the word ⟪ar:وسوسۃ⟫which syllabel do you hear repeated? The sound ⟪ar:وس⟫is repeated twice in the word. وس . وسۃ. So when a word in Arabic contains such repeating syllables.  that automatically implies the repetition of the act itself. It's VERY interesting.

So ⟪ar:ھمسۃ⟫is someone who whispers. Listen carefully. ⟪ar:ھمسۃ⟫. NO syllabels are not repeated. That means the ⟪ar:ھامس⟫whispers only once. But Was-Wasa. because the syllabel ⟪ar:وس⟫is repeated. that implies that a ⟪ar:وَسوَاس⟫. the whisperER.  is somone who whispers. and then whispers again. and then whispers again. and then whispers again.

So ⟪ar:الوسواس⟫is someone who whispers all the time. continuously.  until its purpose is achieved.   wass -wassaa wass-wasaa wass -wassaa. That's how that act of whispering is. it is constantly repeated until the goal is acquired.

A similar example is the word zal-zala. which means the shaking of the earth. and earthquake. But you notice the syllabel "ZAL" repeated? So zalzala means shaking of the earth. but its not just the earth shaking once. It is when the earth shakes. then it shakes again. and then shakes again. that is zal-zala. 

A series of mountains. one after the other. sil-silaa. Not just a mountain but a series of mountains one after the other.

So when a syllabel is repeated within a word. it describes continuity of the act itself. it implies repetition. You understand? So just studying the root of the word ⟪ar:وسواس⟫tells us.  that this whispering that is mentioned. is first of all taking place with evil intent.  and secondly. it is not just happening once. but repeatedly. And by repeatedly I don't mean a few times.

Now here's another subtle difference we need to understand. When I say several times . that could be a few random times and that's it. right? .  And this is why you see. Arabic is such an eloquent and sophisticated language. If the act of whispering would be repeated only a few times. then the word would have been  ⟪ar:المُوَسوِس⟫. which is the active participle.  But allah did not use the word ⟪ar:الموسوِس⟫. or ⟪ar:وِسواس⟫. The whisperer.  Notice both words ⟪ar:الموسوِس⟫. or ⟪ar:وِسواس⟫. they contain Kasra. A kasra would mean just a few sets of whispers. He would repeat his deed a few times and then walk away. But in the ayah. ⟪ar:وَسوسۃ⟫. is used. with a fatha or a zabar. This is called ⟪ar:صیغۃ المبالغہ⟫ . meaning.  The one who whispers NON-STOP. The EXTREME whisperer. one who is obsessed with whispering.  You understand?

If he was just a whisperer. he would have been ⟪ar:وِسواس⟫. But a ⟪ar:وَسواس⟫ is an obsessive compulsive whispere. he's a whisperer with OCD. He doesn't stop. He keeps going and going and going. till he accomplishes his goal.

So now you see what just happened here?. Just the word whisper. وسوسۃ . itself implied continuous reptition by the repetition of the syllabel in it. But now tack on top of it. the hyperbolized form of the whisperER. with the Fatha (⟪ar:وَسواس⟫and not ⟪ar:وِسواس⟫). That adds further strength to the act of continuous whispering. And this makes it A VERY VERY. EXTREMELY.  powerful word to use.  to describe the CONSTANT. NEVER ENDING. RELENTLESS. whispering of shaytan. This is not an easy enemy we are dealing with. We are dealing with a VERY POWERFUL enemy. and this is VERY important to appreciate. Because ONLY AFTER we truly appreciate the power of this enemy. we can understand the need of our submission to the protection of Allah. When you are afraid of an enemy that you think you might be able to take on yourself. your desperation of seeking protection against that enemy is of a differentl level. But when you know that there is NO way you can defeat an enemy. the level of your desperation in seeking protection completely changes. doesn't it?

So that's the first thing to undertand from this word. ⟪ar:الوسواس⟫. that Shaytan is someone who whispers.  and will continue to whisper non stop till the end of time.  The second thing I want you to notice is that this ayah seeks protection from the evil of the constant whisperER. Not the whisperING itself. The ayah does not say. ⟪ar:من شر الوسوسۃُ الخناس⟫ . Protection from the evil WHISPERING of Khannas. After all isn't it the whispering that is bad? . Aren't we seeking protection from the evil whispering. So why did Allah specifically mention the whisperER and not the whispering itself?. This is because the one who does the whispering.  can do more evil than just the whisper itself. You understand?

Whispering is just ONE of the tactics of Shaytan. Therefore when we ask allah.  for protection against the whisperER. we realize that his constant whispering is only ONE of the ways in which he can harm us. He could harm us in numerous other ways. the greates of which is his whispering. So we're submitting to Allah's protection against ALL of it. We're asking for protection against his whispers and also ANY other things he may do to harm us.  If the ayah just said protect me from the whispering. then that's all we would be protected from. But we are asking for protection from his whispering AND any other acts he may try to do against us. Basically we are seeking protecting against HIM. from EVERYTHING he does.  including his whisper. So it is way more comprehensive. and all inclusive to say ⟪ar:من شر الوسواس الخناس⟫than to say ⟪ar:من شر الوسوسۃ الخناس.⟫

### Khannas

Then there is the adjective that has been added to the whisperer wich is  ⟪ar:الخناس⟫. Literally the word means "The RetreatER". The one who retreats. This word is also used elsewhere in quran.
⟪ar-quote:‏فَلَآ أُقْسِمُ بِٱلْخُنَّسِ ‎⟫

⟪ar-quote:ٱلْجَوَارِ ٱلْكُنَّسِ⟫

It is used to describe stars.  that seem to the eye that they would twinkle.  and then step back and disappear.  Thats what the word ⟪ar:خَنَسَ⟫means. To step back. to Retreat.

But the ayah is not
⟪ar:من شر الوسواس **الخَانِس**⟫.

Khaanis is the one who steps back.  ⟪ar:خَنَّاسَ⟫. The one who KEEPS stepping back.  And if he keeps stepping back. then that in itself implies.  that he keeps stepping forward as well.  and then again steps back. You know what this means? It means that he's not only constantly whispering. and where did we get that from? From ⟪ar:الوسواس⟫. the one who constantly whispers. But then as soon as he whispers. what does he do? He steps back. So if somebody does that to you. Someone calls out your name from behind .  and then when you turn around he's not there.  he stepped back. That's  ⟪ar:خَنَّاسَ⟫. And then.  the moment you show him your back.  what does he do again? He steps forward and whispers again. And you would think that after several times of doing this. he would stop. right? But not according to the word ⟪ar:الخناس⟫. Because it is once again. ⟪ar:صیغۃ المبالغہ⟫. It is used in its hyperbolized form. just like ⟪ar:الوَسواس⟫.

You know the word khabbaaz. means the one who makes khubz. He makes bread over and over and over again. he does it for a living.  He does not just make one pita bread and give up. He keeps making bread day in and day out. that's why he is called al-khabbaaz. He is going to do it for a living all the time. 

Similarly someone who KEEPS on giving gifts. never stops. Keeps giving gifts over and over and over again. ⟪ar:وھَّاب⟫.  Hiba means a gift. ⟪ar:وھَّاب⟫.  one who gifts over and over and over again. And this is actually one of the names of Allah AWJ.  Another name ⟪ar:غَفَّار⟫. 
⟪ar:غَافِر⟫. someone who forgives . ⟪ar:غَفَّار⟫. someone who keeps forgiving over and over and over and over again. Its not that Allah just forgives once. or that He's forgiving.  He is ⟪ar:غَفَّار⟫.  because He CONSTANTLY forgives.  over and over and over again. Even for the same crimes that we keep repeating. as long as our intention is pure when se seek His forgiveness. So there is this hyperbolee used in these words.

So⟪ar:الوسواس الخناس⟫. is someone who keeps coming at you from behind. whispers a thought in your head. and then retreats. Comes to you again. whispers a thought in your head. and then retreats. Comes again. whispers a thought in your head. and then retreats.

Now what do you think. From a pshychological point of view. What do you think happens when someone keeps doing that to you? Someone keeps whispering to you over and over again. and keep retreating over and over again. What do you start thinking? You start thinking that these thoughts. are YOUR OWN thoughts. He instigates you. and ou think it is YOU who actually wants to do it. It is YOU who wants to see it. It is YOU who wants to feel it. You end up taking responsibility of committing the evil act. which started off with someone else's whisper. How many times in your life have you caught yourself saying. I can't believe I did that. I can't believe I said that. I can't believe I thought that?. We do it all the time.

Shaytan with his CONSTANT. Never ending whispering. with his constant retreat. He makes us do things.  which at one time we had said. I'll NEVER EVER do that. And then we end up doing those EXACT same acts. that we detested in others. And it's all because of  ⟪ar:الوسواس الخناس⟫.

So that is ⟪ar:الوسواس الخناس⟫. . He keeps whispering. retreating. and then coming back. over and over and over again. He NEVER EVER quits.

So his offense is ⟪ar:الوسواس⟫. and his defense is ⟪ar:الخناس⟫. And that's why Allah calls out to us. to give ourselves willingly . in submission to our Rabb. our Malik. and our Ilah. Because when someone tries to hurt a child. who comes between the child and his enemy? Parents stand in between. The Rabb AlNaas comes forth for protection. When civilians are being attacked by invaders. who comes forth to protect the civilians? The king does. That's Malik AnNaas. And when an enemy SO powerful. physical or spiritual. when such a powerful enemy.  that neither the Rabb nor the Malik (in the worldly sense) can protect against. When الوسواس الخناس attacks. who comes to our protection? Ilah AnNaas. SubhanAllah!  So we have both his attacks. of ⟪ar:وسوسۃ⟫as well as ⟪ar:خنس⟫covered inside these 2 words.

So from this ayah. we are learning that Shaytan.  plants himself.  right in the heart of human beings. of the sons of Adam AS. And then as soon as the human being gets lexadazical. As soon as he becomes heedless. He becomes forgetful.  Shaytan hits him with waswasa. But then as soon as he remembers Allah. As soon as he remembers his Rabb. his Malik. His Ilah.  Shaytan retreats back.  He takes a step back. 

So when we remember allah . shaytan takes a step back. and when we stop remembering allah.  Shaytan takes moves forward. and he NEVER EVER stops.  Its not like he sees an opening and says. Aaaah I'm tired today.  don't feel like it.  mood nahee hai.  I don't feel like doing waswasa today.  had a long busy few thousand years. NO !!! He doesn't do that. because he is  ⟪ar:الوسواس الخناس⟫. He never takes a break. You and I will take a break from remembering Allah.  Shaytan NEVER takes a break. He works hard at his job. he is working harder than any of us. And to defend ourselves against such an enemy. what do we need to do? We have to fight back HARD. This is not something that comes casually. This ⟪ar:استعاذہ⟫from shaytan. It does not come easily. He is really GREAT at what he does. And to be protected. we really have to appreciate the hard work he is putting in. .  to throw people into hell fire. This is serious stuff. These ayas really give us a true appreciation of what the level our defenese against him should be like.

Now what is the end goal of his constant whispering? What goal is he trying to achieve? What did we see his own problem was? It was Kibr. it was arrogance and pride. right? And thats what he wants to instill in the hearts of people. Because he knows. that's what got him into trouble. Therefore it will surely get others into trouble as well. And the easiest way to do that is anger. Anger is a manifestration of what? Of Anger. Of Ego! And shaitaan is very good at making us angry. He will work so tactfully to make you angry. He'll work on you. And then at the same time he'll work on the one he wants you get angry with. And then put you both together. and BOOM. It is CRAZY how this guy operates. He'll tell the thief to commit robbery. and at the same time tell the guard to be careful tonight. He is the greatest double agent you will EVER encounter in your life.

Even if you try to help someone. You see someon getting angry.  you go and try to remind him. Asif Mamu! please don't get angry. Calm down. say⟪ar:اعوذ باللہ من الشیطان ارجیم⟫. He'll get me mad right back at you.

*What do you mean? Are you calling me shaitan? Are you saying I am posessed by shaitan?*

He'll get that person even more angry. And then you'll get mad. I'm trying to help you and you're yelling at me??? What the hell? . And you and I are going at it.  and shaytaan is sitting there laughing. Saying.  I got them good! I even got him to stop saying   ⟪ar:اعوذ باللہ من الشیطان ارجیم⟫ SubhanAllah.

So make no mistake. Shaytan is REALLY good at what he does. and it takes humility and a lot of courage to take a step back and say.  this is not me. This is shytan whispering to me. I need to take a step back and humble myself before allah.  And realize that anger is something that is be-fitting ONLY to Allah.  and it is not something befitting to me. It is not something I should be taking upon myself. So if I'm feeling angry. I should take a step back and say ⟪ar:اعوذ باللہ من الشیطان ارجیم.⟫ . And Quran warns us to be constantly aware of Shaytan's presence
⟪ar-quote:مَا مِنکُم مِن احدٍ اِلَّا قَد وُکِّلَ بِہِ قَرِینُہُ⟫

There is not one of you , but there is a constant partner assigned with him.

Now notice the word QAREEN is used. which means associate. This hadees does not use the word shaytan. so you have to be careful about your associates. The friends you hang out with. if he can't get to you directly.  he'll get to you through your friends. Through your associate he will whisper to you.

And you know. this waswasa. is not just against Allah. Shaytan also does waswas about Rasul allah (SAS) and his Awliya. Maulana Ali. about the Imams duaat, manaseeb. Your parents. He'll do waswas about everyone. The easier attack is not to attack our eman ABOUT allah. You know what the easier attack is? Attacking our Eman IN the MESSENGER of allah. the friends of allah. he can attack those kinds of eman very easily. because shaytan brings ego in the way. 
⟪ar-quote:بشرٌ یَھدُو لَنا؟⟫

This man is going to guide us? Come on! Hes just like us. They said about Eisa AS . ⟪ar:یمشی فی الأسواق⟫. he walks in in the market just like us. He goes shoping too. How is he a messenger?. I saw him at the grocery store the other day. Hes a messenger? ⟪ar:یأکل الطعام⟫. He eats food just like I eat food. what makes him so special? Come On! You really expect me to take authority from him??

And this is the root of ego. human beings refuse to accept the authority of another human being. Thats just ingrained inside our heads. When you're in class.  you refuse to accept the authority of your teacher. and even when you do. you do it grudgingly. Uggghhh.  sit down!. FINE!  You can't stand the authority of your parents over you. Oh come on. It's MY life. Just leave me alone!!! Your life? It's your life? Who gave you this life? Who carried you for 9 months to give you this life you're so arrogant about? But we just can't stand their authority over us.

Employees can't stand listening to their bosses. The only time you say you have a good boss. is when he doesn't give you any work to do. He doesn't tell you what to do. that's when you love him.  As soon as another human being has authority over us.  we get irritated. What does he know! You get pulled over by a cop. he shows you his authority.  you get irritated. you have to go before a judge. you get irritated. human beings just don't like another human being having authority over them.

And yet here you have another human being.  the messenger of Allah.  who has been given absolute authority over you. absolute authority! We don't like it!

You know. for us the messenger is just another book. a story we read in the books. But to Maulana Ali he wasn't just a story.  He was his master. He was his authority over him. Rasul Allah SAS was Rabb and He was Malik for Maulana ALi. To Salman Farsi. Miqdad bin Aswad. Ammarey Yasir. Rasul Allah was not just another person with authority. for them he was the MESSENGER OF ALLAH(SAS). How difficult do you think it must have been for them to accept his authority over them? These are people Rasul Allah grew up with. He was their uncle, their relative their friend. Can you apprecieate how difficult it is to accept everything your best friend says no matter what? Do you know how hard that is? And you can't even call him buddy anymore. What do you have to call him now? Ya Rasul Allah! . . How hard is it for a wife to accept EVERYTHING the husband says!! EVERYTHING he says.  and not even say. MY husband said. No! Rasul Allah said! They have to say
⟪ar-quote:قال رسول اللہ صلی اللہ علیہ و آلہ وسلم⟫

Maulatina fatima doesn't say ⟪ar:قال ابی⟫! . my father said. Maultina khadeeja does not say. ⟪ar:قال زوجی⟫. my husband said. they say ⟪ar:قال رسول اللہ⟫. Because they have completely.  and willingly accepted his authority over them. they have humbled their ego. .  Accepting allah is one thing. But accepting Rasul Allah requires MUCH more humility.  Because now you have to accept the authority of another human being over yourself. Because now this person is going to be telling you what allah wants from you. right? This is why people have so much problems with Manseeb in our Jamaat. They don't know what they're doing. They don't know how to run the jamaat. You know what? Walk 2 steps in their shoes and then talk against them. Walk 2 steps in their shoes. It's SO easy to sit on the sidelines and criticize. I have 20 people in these sessions. and I've realize what a challenge it is deal with a group. They have to deal with the entire jamaat spread across continents. But we have these problems because we as human beings do not like the authority of another human being over us. And this is what Shaytan takes advantage of.

We today are living in a time of inflated egos. It is so easy to let that get in the way. That's really the psychological origin.  of not accepting a master over us. I don't want to accept Allah as my master. because then I have to do what he commands me to do. And that's not acceptable to me. Because I wanna do what I wanna do. Therefore what's the easiest way to do that? You see this play out every election time. one party criticizes and character assassinate the other one. Because that's the easiest way to win.  We do the same thing with Allah. Character assasination. What sort of an Allah is this?. How is he merciful? Look what's happening to me. Look what's happening all around me. There couldn't possibly be an Allah. I am NOT going to believe in the existence of Allah. And once Shytan gets you to do that. Once he convinces you to reject the mastery of Allah over your soul. once you do that.  you have now basically handed over your soul to the devil.

### Human beings cannot escape slavery

But sadly. you know what the most ironic thing about that is?. That in rejecting the mastery and ownership of Allah over you. inevitablly. you have now accepted the ownership and mastery of Shaytan over you. You have now made Shaytan your Rabb. He now owns you.  You're still a slave. You're still a slave. no matter what. The sad part is that now. instead of being the slave of THE MOST merciful. THE MOST compassionate master there is. You are now slave to a HORRIBLE HORRIBLE master. He will make you do things.  that even though you find pleasurable today. they will DESTROY you in the hereafter. And on that day when you are being punished. he will completely back off and disown you.
⟪ar-quote:وَمَا كَانَ لِىَ عَلَيْكُم مِّن سُلْطَنٍ⟫

Woh Woh. Dude! Don't blame me. I have nothing to do with your destruction today. I did not hold a gun to your head.
⟪ar-quote:إِلَّآ أَن دَعَوْتُكُمْ فَٱسْتَجَبْتُمْ لِى⟫

I just invited you. I simply called you to that evil. and it was YOU who responded to it.
⟪ar-quote:فَلَا تَلُومُونِى وَلُومُوٓا۟ أَنفُسَكُم⟫

Do not blame me today. Curse your own soul. Because everything you did. it was all your doing.

This is the kind of friend Shaytan is. You kids tell me. Is this friendship worth it? Is this the kind of friend we should abandon Allah for? Because Allah says about this friends. You just heard what Shaytan will say to his friends on the day of judgment. Now let me tell you what ALlah says about this friends on day of judgment.

⟪ar-quote:أَلآ إِنَّ أَوْلِيَآءَ اللَّهِ لاَ خَوْفٌ عَلَيْهِمْ وَلاَ هُمْ يَحْزَنُونَ⟫

No doubt about it. for the friends of Allah. there will be NO fear or grief for them on the day of judgment
⟪ar-quote:الَّذِينَ ءَامَنُوا وَكَانُوا يَتَّقُونَ⟫

Those who believed in him and adopted piety for him
⟪ar-quote:لَهُمُ الْبُشْرَي فِي الْحَيَاةِ الدُّنْيَا وَفِي الاَخِرَةِ⟫

For this is glad tidings in the life of this world. and in the afterlife.

And now listen to this.
⟪ar-quote:لا تَبْدِيلَ لِكَلِمَاتِ اللَّهِ ذَلِكَ هُوَ الْفَوْزُ الْعَظِيمُ⟫

There is never a change in the words of Allah. Allah never goes back on his words. And for them is greatest of all success. Notice the words Fauz AlAzeem are used here. We talked about this amazing word previously. What this success acutally means linguistically.

I just told you what Shaytan does with us. In this world he convinces us that we are his BEST friend. And in the afterlife he completely abandons us. He goes back on his words. But Allah. the true master. the Rabb . the Malik. the Ilah.  He says.
⟪ar-quote:لا تَبْدِيلَ لِكَلِمَاتِ اللَّهِ⟫

Allah never goes back on his words.  SubhanAllah!

So how incredibley foolish. how incredibly stupid would be the one. who who abandon Allah's mastery over his soul and accept Shaytan's mastery. Because make no mistake. You ALWAYS ALWAYS have someone being a Rabb over you. If it's not Allah.  it will definitely be Shaytan. If not that.  then your own desires inspired by Shaytan. But you ALWAYS ALWAYS have a master over you. Why? Because Allah says.
⟪ar-quote:وما خلقت الجن و الانس الا لیعبدون⟫

I created jinn and mankind to be MY slaves. Slavery is what we are made of. We can't escape it. Slavery of our soul. Slavery of our desires. slavery of our friends. slavery of the fleeting attractions of this world. slavery of power. slavery of wealth. slavery of women. There is nothing but slavery. We cannot escape slavery. just as much as a flower cannot escape its fragrance. and filth cannot escape its stinch.

These surahs are teaching us . that IF that's the reality. if we can't escape slavery no matter what. then accept Allah as our master. Because He is the BEST master you will or can EVER have. And InshaAllah we will talk about the nature of his mastery in details in future sessions. InshaAllah I'll show you the mercy and love of this master. You compare it to anything else and then you choose for yourself.

So the immediate question. rather concern becomes. What do we do? If Shaytan is so strong.  and his whispers are so powerful and constant and unrelentless.  What are we to do? We are pretty much doomed.  because he can get to us at anytime right? Now listen to this ayah in which Allah declares who the shaytan will NEVER be able to touch. When Iblees was asking Allah for all these allowances. that give me time till the day of judgment. I'll attack your creations from the left. from the right. etc. When he was asking for all these allowances.

There is a declaration that Allah AWJ made to him about us. He said.

⟪ar-quote:إِنَّ عِبَادِى لَيْسَ لَكَ عَلَيْهِمْ سُلْطَنٌ⟫

No doubt about it . on my slaves. the ones who ACCEPT themselves as my slaves. The one who accept me. who willingly submit to me in obedience. those who give themselves up to me. those who accept me as their Rabb. their Malik. their Ilah. you will have ABSOLUTELY no authority over them.

The moment they accept MY slavery.  your authority over them will end. You will no longer be able to harm them. As soon as they come under my protection. As soon as they submit themselves to MY protection. your game will be over. All they need to do is accept me as their master. their owner. and submit themselves to me.

This is all captured in the word Rabb. Why do you think these surahs begin with the word Rabb?

⟪ar-quote:قل أعوذ برب الفلق؛ قل أعوذ برب الناس⟫

Why do this start with Rabb? Because If Allah is rabb!.  If we have sincerely. honestly. truthfully. willingly accepted him as our Rabb. that acceptance makes us what? His slaves! That by definition makes us ⟪ar:عبد⟫. and allah says

⟪ar-quote:إِنَّ عِبَادِى لَيْسَ لَكَ عَلَيْهِمْ سُلْطَنٌ⟫

No doublt . on my slaves. on MY slaves. you will have no authority.  Look he says MY slaves? Why did he need to use the word MY here? He could have just said.

⟪ar-quote:إِنَّ العِبَادَ لَيْسَ لَكَ عَلَيْهِمْ سُلْطَنٌ⟫

Why did He say MY slave??? because we are a slave no matter what. He created us as slaves. The MY includes willful submission. Allah does not want to make us his slave. We want Allah to become our master. I'll say that again. Allah does not want to make us his slave. We want Allah to become our master. He does not need our slavery. It is WE who need HIS mastery over us! I can't wait to get to the ayats of Fateha when we discuss this slavery and mastery relationship with Allah. It's the MOST BEAUTIFUL thing I have EVER learnt in all the years I've studied.

So the call is for US to submit ourselves in Allah's slavery. That's why he says MY slave. Because accepting Allahs slavery in and of itself.  is true protection from Shaytan. To act as allahs slave. To live a life as Allah's slave is a protection from shatytan.

So Allah said.

⟪ar-quote:إِنَّ عِبَادِى لَيْسَ لَكَ عَلَيْهِمْ سُلْطَنٌ⟫

No doubt. on MY slaves. you will have no authority.

⟪ar-quote:إِلَّا مَنِ ٱتَّبَعَكَ مِنَ ٱلْغَاوِينَ⟫

You will ONLY have authority over those who choose YOU as their master. Only those will be from among the misguided.

Look at all the problems we face today. Problems with posessions. Psychological issues. Depressions . These do not happen to people who are truly slaves of Allah. one of the clear. manifest evidence of us not being slaves of allah is that we face these problems. InshaAllah I hope to do a few sessions on trials and tribulations. and what they are . and why we are put through these tests in life. OK so this was .

⟪ar-quote:من شر الوسواس الخناس⟫

---

<!-- section 7 (id=5730, raw_sort=7): Chest of Man -->
In the previous session we studied the meaning of the ayah. ⟪ar:من شر الوسواس الخناس⟫. we know in this surah. we specifically seek Allah's protection.  from ONE specific evil.  from the evil of  ⟪ar:الوسواس⟫and ⟪ar:الخناس⟫. The one who is constantly whispering.  and constantly retreating. We understood how relentless and incessant and oppressive Shaytan is in his whispers. Therefore we must constantly seek protection of Rabb AlNaas, Malik AnNaas and Ilah AnNaas from the evil of this⟪ar:الوسواس الخناس⟫ .

Now after describing this evil entity. shaytan itself. Allah proceeds to describe his evil actions.  So the surah continues to say.
⟪ar-quote:الذی یوسوس فی صدور الناس⟫. The one who constantly whispers into the chests of people.
⟪ar-quote:من الجنۃ و الناس⟫ . They are from among the jinn and mankind

Let's look at the first ayah.
⟪ar-quote:الذی یوسوس فی صدور الناس⟫. The one who constantly whispers into the chests of people.

The first thing to notice here.  is that Allah mentions whispering again. He had alread mentioned that in the previous ayah.  ⟪ar:من شر الوسواس الخناس⟫ . But now again he's saying  ⟪ar:الذی یوسوس فی صدور الناس⟫. So let's begin by understand the reason for this repetition.

In the previous ayah we see.  that Allah mentioned the IDENTITY of this evil entity. and here He is mentioning the ACTION of that evil entity. And he used the present tense ⟪ar:یُوَسوِسُ⟫for it too.

So we saw that Shaytan is ⟪ar:الوسواس⟫. that Shaytan is someone who whispers.  and will continue to whisper non stop till the end of time. The next thing I want you to know is that ⟪ar:الوسواس⟫is an Ism. its a noun. ⟪ar:الاسم یدُلُّو علی الدوام⟫ . a noun signifies permanence.

In the arabic language. just like any other language.  you can use nouns and you can use verbs.  What is the difference betwen a verb and a noun? Between nouns and verbs, which has tenses? You know present tense, future tense, past tense? Verbs have a tense . Nouns do not have a tense . There's no past tense noun or present tense noun or future against noun . Is that clear? When I say I am eating. it means I'm eating now. but at some point I will stop. a verb is tied in time. it has happened. it is happening. or it will happen. but it is temporary. it will not happen at some point. But a noun is permanent. It doesn't change state. A book is a book. was a book. is a book. will always remain a book. It's not going to change state. You understand?

### Job if Shaytan is WASWASA

Let's understand identity first. When I say to you.  I am a teacher. you know what means ? It means THAT is who I am.  thats what I do. Shaytan has been identified as ⟪ar:الوسواس الخناس⟫. Someone who constantly. incessantly. relentlessly. whispers and retreats. That is his identity. That's why in the previous ayah.  the noun. ⟪ar:الوسواس⟫ is used. But in this ayah. Allah uses a verb. ⟪ar:یُوسوِسُ⟫ . Why? Because Shaytan actually lives up to that title too. It's one thing to get the title.  but its entirely another thing to earn that title by actually doing it.

That's what the present tense ⟪ar:یُوسوِسُ⟫. tells us. Because in ancient Arabic when a present tense was used. future tense was implied within it. So this word ⟪ar:یُوسوِسُ⟫ tells us.  that not only is Shaytan known for being a whisperER. for his constant, unrelentless whispering. but he is actually doing it now.  and he will contine to do it in the future. So you better be ready!. You better always be prepared. He's never going to stop. There is never going to be a time or a moment.  when you can think that you are free from his whispers.

Which in turn also means. that there is never going to be a time. when you and I will NOT need allah's protection. We're constantly under attack. therefore we constantly need Allah's protection.  Even when you we engaged in religion activities. like salaah, fasting. zakaat hajj. He will whisper to us . every single moment.

But then allah added something quite remarkable. he said ⟪ar:فی صدور الناس.⟫

. in the CHEST of people. The word ⟪ar:صدر⟫. CHEST. according to the Arabic lexicon. it is ⟪ar:ظرف مکان⟫. It is actually a place. In the Quran. Sadar is always used in the context of a place or a space. ⟪ar:رب الشرح لی صدری⟫. Master! expand my chest. Again in the context of space.

In contrast to that.  there is the word ⟪ar:قلب⟫. which is a thing. Allah did not say.  ⟪ar:الذی یوسوس فی قلوب الناس⟫. He constantly whispers.,.  and will continue to constantly whisper in the hearts of people. Allah did not say that. He did not use the word heart. He used the word chest.  Now what's the difference?

There is actually a big difference.  between saying that he whispers in the heart.  versus saying.  he whispers in the chest. In the previous sessions. we talked about.  how the heart is the center of all human activity. Everything a man does. the desire first originates in the heart. and is then converted into action. with the help of the intellect. But the origin of desire is always the heart.

Now the imagery this ayah creates . think of it like this.  . The heart. think of it like a castle. and around the castle there is some open real estate. there is a front yart. side yard.  backyard. So there is all this real estate around the castle. The castle is your heart.  and the surrounding real estate is your chest. The heart is inside your chest.  Allah says he gave shaytan access to what? The chest.  but Allah did not give Shaytan access to the heart!

So Shaytan is chilling in the front yard. or he's sun bathing in the backyard. Basically he's all around. but he's not where yet? he's not in the heart.  the heart is locked. And the only one who has the key to the door of your heart. is You! Hes constantly knocking on the door with his whispers. He's waiting outside. patiently. He's ALWAYS there. ⟪ar:الذی یوسوس فی صدور الناس⟫. He is constantly knocking on the door of your heart. hoping one day you will open that door for him and let him enter your heart. 

Now think of  ⟪ar:استعاذہ⟫as a security guard.  that you've placed outside the door of your heart. The second you say ⟪ar:اعوذ باللہ من الشیطان الرجیم⟫ . the guard appears. and does not let the shaytan come close to the heart. He throws him back in the frontyard. But if you do not keep calling upon that guard for protection. Shaytan will keep knocking. keep knocking.keep knocking. And what will happen? Eventually you will open the door and shaytan will step inside. 

Do you know what happens next? What do you think will happen when Shaytan walks from the chest INTO the heart ??

You know people who have eman. people who have faith. You know what's the MOST beautiful thing to them? Their faith itself.
⟪ar-quote:وَلَكِنَّ ٱللَّهَ حَبَّبَ إِلَيْكُمُ ٱلْإِيمَنَ وَزَيَّنَهُۥ فِى قُلُوبِكُمْ⟫

Allah has made the love of faith. beautiful to the hearts.
⟪ar-quote:وَكَرَّهَ إِلَيْكُمُ ٱلْكُفْرَ وَٱلْفُسُوقَ وَٱلْعِصْيَانَ⟫

and has made ugly.  disbelief. ludeness. shamelessness and disobedience.  This is the original state of the hearts. It is natural for human beings to find beauty in good. It is natural for human beings to find beauty in shamefulness. in bravery. in truth. in respect. in obedience. Because this is the fitrah.  this is the nature on which Allah created us. By nature we are attracted to fragrance and repulsed by stench.

When we have Eman in our hearts. it remains soft. And something that is soft. it can be molded. It can be changed. it can be transformed.  Something that is soft is always open to change.  But once the shaytan enters the heart.
⟪ar-quote:وَلَكِن قَسَتْ قُلُوبُهُمْ وَزَيَّنَ لَهُمُ ٱلشَّيْطَنُ مَا كَانُوا۟ يَعْمَلُونَ⟫

But then. the heart becomes hard. and evil deeds start looking beautiful. they start looking tempting. they start looking good. If the rememberance of allah is in our hearts. evil deeds will naturally look ugly. ⟪ar:وَكَرَّهَ إِلَيْكُمُ ٱلْكُفْرَ وَٱلْفُسُوقَ وَٱلْعِصْيَانَ⟫. because allah made disbelief corruption and disobedience disgusting for the hearts. So if you have eman in your hearts.  those things will look disgusting. naturally. You won't even be tempted toward them. You could drive by a club and have the urge to say ⟪ar:استعفر اللہ ، لا حول ولا قوۃ الا باللہ⟫ .What a waste of humanity.  what a disgrace to the son of adam. Allah honored adam with such intellect.  and what level has his children stooped down to. Jumping like monkeys in the name of enjoyment.  What life of animals they are ready to live. you would. by your fitrah. by your nature. you would spit at it. You will be repulsed by it.  That would be your natural response. IF Eman and faith is in your heart.

But if shaytan has made its way in your hearts.   Let me just pull over and check it out a bit. Oh that skimpy dress on her looks really good. She looks really hot. They look so cool smoking and drinking. He sounds so cool using profanity. throwing the F bomb in every sentence. I should try that.  Let me dress in a way so that I can show my body to the world.  Sexuality. shamelessness. ludenss all these things becomes very attractive.when Shaytan is in our heart.

This is the difference between the heart that has kept Shaytan out. versus the heart that has invited him in. Now the question this ayah asks us.  is where do we stand?. When we see such things.  are we disgusted by it. are we repelled by it.  or are we fascinated by it. are we attracted by it. The honest answer to that question.  will give us the true state of faith in our hearts. If eman is beautiful. then disbelief, corruption and disbelief will look evil.  they will look disgusting. And if shaytan has entered the heart.  then it'll be the other way around. It is as simple as that.

So it is actually from the mercy of Allah.  that He gave shaytan access to the chest.  but not to the heart. Had he allowed Shaytan to whisper into the hearts. we would have no defense against him. we would not be able to use our will against him. That's why Allah did not give Shaytan direct access to the heart. It is you and I.  who open the doors of our heart for him. That's on us. We are the ones who do that.

Now if Shaytan is already in our hearts. what do we have to do. in order to get him out? We have to call the guard. We have to dial spiritual 911. which is the Istiaaza. ⟪ar:اعوذ باللہ من الشیطان الرجیم⟫. We have to recite these two surahs.  We have to submit to Allah . willingly. in obedience. seeking His constant protection from the constant waswasa of Shaytan. We have to call upon ⟪ar:رب الفلق⟫ . we have to call upon ⟪ar:رب الناس ، ملک الناس ، الہ الناس⟫ . in order to evict Shaytan from our hearts. And once he's out. we have to place these security guards outside our heart again.  to prevent him from entering again. That's through the constant remembrance of Allah.

---

The surah then progresses to the final ayah. ⟪ar-quote:من الجنۃ و الناس⟫

Allah classifies the evil whisperERS by saying that they belong to two categories. What's also so amazing about this surah. is that if you remember. we saw a progression when it came to the names of Allah. We saw how Rabb progressed to Malik (the king). and then Malik progressed to Ilah. Now we're seeing a similar progression here in the detials of the evil entity. Allah starts off by describing the entity itself. ⟪ar:من شر الوسواس الخناس⟫. He then progresses to describe the act . and the place he attacks.  ⟪ar:الذی یوسوس فی قلوب الناس⟫. and now He progresses to describing the two categories these evil entities belong to. ⟪ar:من الجنۃ و الناس⟫. They are from the Jinn and the mankind.  Allah uses 3 ayats to describe the protector. He then uses 3 ayats to describe the evil. we are seeking protection from.  You can see how beautifully this surah is balanced. 3 ayats talk about Allah. and 3 ayats talk about evil. And you you know why that is? Because there are fundamentally. only 3 evils in the world. If you take the common denominator of all evils. it boils down to 3 things. ⟪ar:کبر، حرس ، حسد⟫.  Pride, Greed and Jealousy. These 3 are called ⟪ar:امہات المعاصی⟫ . The mothers of all evils. Every evil that you know of in this world. stems from these 3 root evils. Pride, Greed and Jealousy. And that's why specifically these 3 names of Allah are called upon. Rabb Malik and Ilah.

Jealously is always associated with love. You love someone or something. but your lover favors somebody or something else. you get jealous. Which of the three names of Allah is associated with pure love? Rabb! That's why to protect against jealousy we say what?. ⟪ar:قل اعوذ برب الناس⟫. We seek the protection of the one. who has the ultimate love.  against the evil of jealously that stems from a deviation in love. 

Similary Greed is always associated with posessions. You have something. you want more and more of it. that's greed. Who has the most posessions of all? . A king does. That's why we call upon. ⟪ar:ملک الناس⟫. We seek the protection of the one who has the ultimate kingship over all.

And finally Pride. Who is the only one worthy of ultimate pride? It's the Ilah. The diety! Pride is only befitting the Ilah. Therefore we seek protection from pride and arrogance by turning to the Ilah. ⟪ar:الہ الناس⟫ . The ultimate. and ONLY one.  truly worthy of pride. 

So there is this beautiful symmetry between the 3 primary roots of evil. Jealously, Greed and Pride.  and the protection using these 3 specific names of Allah against those 3 evils. SubhanAllah!

So now Allah classifies the whisperERS into 2 categories. Jinn and Human beings. Now the first thing.  is the order in which these two categories are mentioned. Allah mentioned jinn first and mankind second.  Now why is that?. 

Because there are other places in the Quran. that when it came to shaytan. Allah mentions human beigns first and jinn later.

⟪ar-quote:وَكَذَلِكَ جَعَلْنَا لِكُلِّ نَبِىٍّ عَدُوًّۭا شَيَطِينَ ٱلْإِنسِ وَٱلْجِنِّ⟫

And this is how for every prophet there has been an enemy. from the devils of mankind and Jinn. In this ayah we see that Ins. human devils are mentioned first.  and the spiritual devils (jinn) are mentioned second. But in surah AlNaas. we see that the order is reversed. Jinn is mentioned first and  ⟪ar:الناس⟫  is mentioned second. Why is that?

There are several reasons. The obvious reason.  is that in the ayah I just mentioned

⟪ar-quote:وَكَذَلِكَ جَعَلْنَا لِكُلِّ نَبِىٍّ عَدُوًّۭا⟫

the ayah is talking about prophets. And when it comes to prophets. the animosity against them. always originates from human beings first. Human beings go outright against the messenger of Allah. Since they take precdence in their animosity against the prophets. human beings are mentioned first in this ayah.

But because the context of our surah. Surah AnNaas. is not animosity against prophets . it is ⟪ar:وسوسۃ⟫. against human beings. Who takes the primary role? the jinn. That's why in this surah Jinn is mentioned first and human beings later.

Another reason why Jinn is mentioned first and human beings later. is because one is spiritual and the other is physical. The jinn is just a soul without a body. it is in the spiritual form. While Naas. human beings are in the physical form. And we see that this surah is all about the attack on our soul. Surah AlFalaq was about seeking protection from physical attacks. But Surah AlNaas is about seeking protection from spiritual attacks. And because of that.  Jinn. the ones in spritual form are mentioned first . and Nass. the ones in physical form are mentioned second.

Another reason is that it is the corruption of the soul that leads to the corruption of the body. It is the evil desire. that feeling of arrogance.  contempt. of jealousy. that comes first. And what is the place in which these evil desires and feelings originate? It's the heart. which is placed where? in the chest! Which is where Shaytan attacks. So the intention of these whisperings is to corrupt the soul first. because that will inevitably lead to the corruption of phystical actions through sins. That's why the spiritual form (jinn) is mentioned first. and the physical form (Naas) is mentioned second. because corruption will happen. first in the soul.  and will then proceed into actions.

Another reason why Jinn is mentioned first. is because scholars comment. ⟪ar:وسوسۃ الجن، ھو الاصل⟫. the whispernigs of the jinn is primary.  Meaning that if a human being is whispering evil to you.  it may not even be his own whisper.  He may be plagurizing it from the whispering of HIS shaytan.

So because shaytan couldn't get to you directly. he's now using someone you're associated with. to get to you. You understand? It's possible that the human being whispering to you.  is being motivated by the whisperings of a jinn.  So when a human being does waswasa. it could be because of a jinn controlling him. But when a jinn does waswasa.,.  it is always his own doing. Thats why  ⟪ar:من الجنۃ⟫  first. and then the secondary ⟪ar:و الناس⟫ . .

So what we're learning here. is the concept of vehicles!.  Shaytan uses vehicles. This means that the waswass of shaytan can come to you through your best friend. It can come through your favorite cousin. a relative.  you hear their voice.   you don't hear Shaytan's voice . but you know what? At that point.  he is a puppet for Iblees.  And you know why you youngsters find it so challenging to fight these emotions and desires? Because the attacks of Shaytan are strongest against youngsters. Why? Because you guys are the future! If he gets to corrupt your minds. he not only has you in his pocket.  he also has what? The next generation! You guys are the greatest bang for his buck as they say.

And also because youngsters today. they don't have locks on the doors of their hearts. Forget locks. some of you guys have the entire door removed. There is this huge opening.  with a sign hanging out. Let's P-A-R-T-A-E . All Shayateen Welcome Aboard!!! 

Becaue this is how Shaytan works. Even if the guy is religious. he'll still do waswasa to him. The guy walks in a book store. sees a young beautiful girl buying a book. even if it's the Quran. He'll walk up to her. Hey! Whatchoo buyin? Oh the Quran? Nice. What's your favorite surah? Oh really? Surah Fateha. Mine too! I'm actually attending these Sunday sessions about it. Would you like to join? Can I get your number. Hahah.  Don't get any ideas. 

I'm joking. but this is really how he operates. And now he doesn't even need to use people. He's got websites and tv channels and hollywood and bollywood. he's got his work on DVD . We have fascilitated his job for him. through modern mass media.  

Now of course. mass media could be used for great things. But for the most part what is it used for? To promote shamelessnes. and evil things.

now the complication in this word naas. In the arabic language there is a word called نفر nafar. which is commonly used for a group of people. and then there is also the word رجال which is typically used for a group of people.

Quran says.

قُلْ أُوحِىَ إِلَىَّ أَنَّهُ ٱسْتَمَعَ نَفَرٌۭ مِّنَ ٱلْجِنِّ فَقَالُوٓا۟ إِنَّا سَمِعْنَا قُرْآنًا عَجَبًۭا

a group of people from among the jinn. the word nafar typically is not used for jinn. it is used for human beings. but in this ayah it is used for jinn. Similarly we have

وَأَنَّهُۥ كَانَ رِجَالٌۭ مِّنَ ٱلْإِنسِ يَعُوذُونَ بِرِجَالٍۢ مِّنَ ٱلْجِنِّ فَزَادُوهُمْ رَهَقًۭا

There used to be men from among the human beings who sought refuge from men among the jinn. so now rijaal is being used for men as well as jinn.

Now in one of the narrations it is said. that some men met a group of people who were very strange looking. so they asked themm من القوم who are you guys> What nation do you come from? they replied. أناسٌ من الجن . very interesting language. they said we are people from the jinnn. but what word did they use for themselves? the plural of naas. unaas.

So another interpreation of this ayah is that. allah says الذی یوسوس فی صدور الناس . the one who whispers into the chest of the naas. من الجنۃ و الناس . those naas. those people can be from among the jinn as well as the human beings.  So this surah is not just a protection for believers from among human beings. it is also a protection for believers among the jinn. So the word naas in this interpretations encompasses both. the human beings as well as the jinn.  So the same ayah can be taken in two completely contrasting ways.

So these are the two categories of the whisperERS mentioned in this surah. We now understand the waswasa of the jinn. that it manifests in the form of thoughts and desires in our heads. He keeps prodding and probing us and because he keeps retreating. we start thinking that these are our own thoughts. So we can understand how an invisible jinn does waswasa to us. But what about the whisperings of the human devil? Or someone who is being used as a vehicle by a jinn? How do those whispering manifest? Because this ayah mentions both.

**Whisper**

The first thing to realize is that it is a whisper. So we normally think of whisper.  as someone sitting next to us and saying something to us under their breadth. wswswswsws.  We think that is whispering. But there is another form of whispering that is WAY more common. And that happens all the time on the phone. in the form of texts. We do it all the time. and it is constantly done to us as well.  It sounds something like this. Hey! I'll tell you something about this person. but just don't tell anyone I told you OK?. Blah blah blah blah blah. Does that sound familiar? Be very careful of that.

Now if this person is telling you something in confidence. with the intention of protecting you.  or helping you. for example if someone is trying to warn you about the evil intentions of someone. who is trying to harm you. that is a different thing. That is not waswasa. that is hamasa. It is not being done with evil intent. That kind of whispering is being done with good intentions. in order to protect you. There's a difference.  that is NOT waswasa. that is hamasa. I explained the difference between the two words last time.

But more than often times. what is being done is waswasa. especially when its about a third person. Someone fills you up with anger and animosity against your friend or your cousin. and then this whisperER retreats by saying "don't tell anyone I told you". And now the next time you meet this person. EVERYTHING seems wrong about him. The way he walks. the way he's dressed. the way he talks. the way he laughs. And you're sitting there wondering. Why did I ever like this person in the first place? . Did that ever happen? .  What suddenly changed? You liked this person before. now suddenly you don't like anything about him . It's because of that silent whispering . that was done to you under the covers of. "don't tell anyone I told you". "I tell you everything because you're my best friend". "I trust you so much that I feel I can tell you anything". wswswswswswsws.  Be very careful of that!

A man once came to one of the sahabas.  and he tried to slander another muslim brother . He said. You know this man. he pretends to be a muslim. He's such a hypocrite.  he drinks alcohol and he gambles. and he does all sorts of evil deeds. and still comes and prays in the masjid.  And the sahaba replied to him. Couldn't Shaytan find a better postman than you? Couldn't he find a better messenger than you to deliver this gossip to me?.

Be very careful of that. Many people in our lives act as messengers of Shaytan. and they don't even know it. Many times WE act as the messengers of Shaytan without realizing it. Be careful! And the recitation of this surah.  gives us the insight and a reminder to recognize that. in ourselves as well as others.

So to summarize.  the protection we are seeking.  is the protection of the master of people who forget. ⟪ar:رب الناس⟫. the king of people who forget. ⟪ar:ملک الناس⟫ . The god of people who forget. ⟪ar:الہ الناس⟫. 

And this protection is from the evil entity. ⟪ar:الوسواس الخناس⟫ . Who attacks through his whispers. ⟪ar:الذی یوسوس⟫ .  and where does he attack?  ⟪ar:فی صدور الناس⟫. in the chests of people. which contains what? . the heart. And these attackers. they belong to which two categories? ⟪ar:من الجنۃ و الناس⟫ . they are from the jinns.  and human beings.

in the first meaning. the shaytan doing the whispering can be in the spiritual form as well as the physical form.

in the second meaning. the shaytan doing the whispering can whisper TO human beings as well as TO the jinns. Because we know that allah created not just human beings but also jinn for the purpose of worshipping him.

وَمَا خَلَقْتُ ٱلْجِنَّ وَٱلْإِنسَ إِلَّا لِيَعْبُدُونِ

I did not create the jinn and the human beings except to worship me. Now arent' the angels a creation of allah too? So why did he not mention them in this ayah? Aren't they created for his worship too?  why didn't he say

وَمَا خَلَقْتُ الملائکۃ و ٱلْجِنَّ وَٱلْإِنسَ إِلَّا لِيَعْبُدُونِ

I did not create the angels and jinn and the human beings except to worship me. because the angles are already doing what they are supposed to do. they are always busy worshipping him. and they are not affected by the whisperings of shaytan. shaytan cannot get to them in any way shape or form. they are always under the protection of allah. it is the human beings and Jinns that falls prey to the whisperings of shaytan. And once shaytan enters their hearts. takes over their hearts. then he uses both of them to further his cause. thats the same concept of a virus. it infects other cells. makes them like itself to furhter the cuase.
