<!-- section 9 (id=5732, raw_sort=9): Iblees plan to misguide -->
We're studying the story of Adam AS and Iblees through this passage from Surah Aeraf (7th Surah which means Hights. Or a place of elevated status). And something to realize is that even though we look at this as a primal story. the reality is that this story is still going on. This story of Adam AS and Iblees is still being played out in our lives.  over and over again. And this story.  is primarily about two characters. or two creatures. Adam AS and Iblees. Even though Hawwa is mentioned. but she is sorta joined in with Adam AS. Every place that Adam is mentioned. the word ⟪ar:ھما⟫is used. which is the dual form. implying both of them. So Allah says in Surah A'raaf.

⟪ar-quote:وَلَقَدْ خَلَقْنَكُمْ ثُمَّ صَوَّرْنَكُمْ⟫

And we created you both and fashioned you both.
⟪ar-quote:ثُمَّ قُلْنَا لِلْمَلَٓئِكَةِ ٱسْجُدُوا۟ لِآدَمَ فَسَجَدُوٓا۟ إِلَّآ إِبْلِيسَ⟫

and then we commanded the angels to bow down to you. They all did except Iblees.
⟪ar-quote:لَمْ يَكُن مِّنَ ٱلسَّجِدِينَ⟫

He was never going to be from among those who submit. We talked about in great detail what the word Sajda means. It is when the camel sits down . or submits itself. before its rider. and surrenders his control to him. The idea of Sajda being. to give up our will for the will of Allah.

So Iblees refuses to prostrate and so Allah asks him.

⟪ar-quote:قَالَ مَا مَنَعَكَ أَلَّا تَسْجُدَ إِذْ أَمَرْتُكَ⟫

What possibly could stop you from prostrating to Adam when I commanded you to do so?
⟪ar-quote:قَالَ أَنَا۠ خَيْرٌۭ مِّنْهُ خَلَقْتَنِى مِن نَّارٍۢ وَخَلَقْتَهُۥ مِن طِينٍۢ⟫

He said. I am better than him. You created me from fire and you created him from clay. And we talked about the differences between fire and clay in quite depth in the previous session.

The two most important things to take away from this ayah.  is the realization of the fact that it was the arrogance of Iblees that lead to his disobedience. ⟪ar:أَنَا۠ خَيْرٌۭ مِّنْهُ⟫. and then what followed was .⟪ar:خَلَقْتَنِى مِن نَّارٍۢ وَخَلَقْتَهُۥ مِن طِينٍۢ⟫ . You created me from fire and you created him from clay. Which was his very logical justification.  for his disobedience.  The disbelief of Iblees was not that he didn't believe in Allah as his creator. The disbelief of Iblees manifested through his disobedience.

So almost in every single case. when we want to disobey Allah. when we want to disobey a command of Allah. which we in our heart of hearts know to be true. we will always come up with a VERY good. VERY logical justification for it. And that justification will almost always be rooted in this physical world. because what Iblees used as his justification were material objects. He said. I am fire and air. and Adam is earth and water. So the elements he used to justify his superiority were all material objects. they were all physical objects. He used ⟪ar:مادۃ⟫(material) to justify his disobedience. Which is what we do too if you think about it. All desires and pleasures that lead to the disobedience of Allah.  are all grounded in this physical and material world.  And that's a very powerful realization to have. Because a lot of times we can recognize our own disobedience.  by simply examining our justifications.

So allah says to Iblees... how dare you be arrogant before me...
⟪ar-quote:قَالَ فَٱهْبِطْ مِنْهَا  ‎⟫. Fall out of here.. Leave! I am casting you out...
⟪ar-quote:فَمَا يَكُونُ لَكَ أَن تَتَكَبَّرَ فِيهَا⟫. You no longer deserve to stay in this place because of your arrogance. You cannot show pride here. In other words.  you are in the divine presence. This isn't the place for pride.  If you are aware of the glory of Allah. and if you know your place in relation to Allah.  you cannot possibly be in a state of pride before Him.
⟪ar-quote:⟪ar-quote:فَٱخْرُجْ⟫إِنَّكَ مِنَ ٱلصَّغِرِينَ⟫. Get out of here. Because you are from among the Saghireen.  Saghireen comes from ⟪ar:صغر⟫or ⟪ar:صغیر⟫. which means small. Allah says because of your pride. By being prideful and arrogant. you put yourself UNDER the one you thought you were over. So your very thinking. that you are superior to this other creature.... is what made you inferior to him.  And then Iblees says.

⟪ar-quote:قَالَ أَنظِرْنِىٓ إِلَىٰ يَوْمِ يُبْعَثُونَ⟫

He says... give me some reprieve. Give me time.  till the day these people will be raised again... Give me until the judgment day . Once again. notice that Iblees not only believes in Allah as his creator.  he also believes in judgment day. So this is not an athiest who disobeyed Allah. This is actually a FIRM believer. This is a MOMIN (one who believes) who is disobeying Allah. And this is a VERY scray reality when you think about it. Because we claim to be momins too. we claim to be believers too. don't we?? Well. Iblees was a believer. And what made him Iblees. was his disobedience! . We are Allah's creation just like him. We diobey Allah too just like him. If his arrogance and disobedience turned him into Iblees that got him cast out of Jannah. why would that same justic not apply to us? . So this is a very scary reality if you seriously think about it. How are we any different? .  when we too disobey Allah. and come up with the most logical justifications to do it.

Allah says to him...
⟪ar-quote:قَالَ إِنَّكَ مِنَ ٱلْمُنظَرِينَ⟫

Fine! I give you time till the day of judgment!

Wait. What?. What's going on here? Why is Iblees asking for time? and why is Allah giving him time? 

Before we answer these questions. Let's understand something else here. It is a very common misconception that Iblees or Shaytan is standing agianst Allah. That Iblees is somehow Allah's nemesis. (نعوذ باللہ من ذالک). That is ABSOLUTELY incorrect. Nobody can stand against Allah. Nobody has the capability to stand against Allah. Iblees is a creation of Allah. and by his own words he accepts that. And a creation cannot stand against his creator. So that's the first thing we need to understand. Iblees is not standing against Allah. Iblees is standing against Adam and the children of Adam AS. He is standing against us. He is our enemy. our nemesis. He is not Allah's nemesis. The only reason he is even being able to do what he does. is because Allah has allowed him to. He is doing what he's doing WITH Allah's permission.

Let's begin with the second part. Why did Allah allow Iblees this time.  in which he could misguide us. Wouldn't it have been awesome if he had just imprisoned Iblees right there and then?  So what made Allah accept the challenge of Iblees? Let's understand this part first.

### Adam was created as vicergent

You See.  Adam AS . and even us.  as the the children of Adam. Banee Adam. we are Allah's very special creation.  That is why he called us his khaleefa... that's why he said to the angels. ⟪ar:أنی جاعل فی الارض خلیفۃ⟫. I am going to create my representative on earth... Khalifa comes from the word. Khalaf. or Yakhlufhu.  meaning succeeding someone or  taking one's place..  A person who takes the position or place of another person is called a khaleefa. or a caliph. or deputy. Another meaning of Khalifa is the one who has been fully taught. or fully trained. Because ONLY the one who has been taught. can now take the place of the teacher. I am a software developer. If I train and teach someone everything I know about software development. that person can then take my place. He can then step into my role. He can be my Khaleefa. you understand? Now did Allah teach Adam AS something? He did.⟪ar:وَعَلَّمَ آدَمَ ٱلْأَسْمَآءَ كُلَّهَا⟫. Allah taught Adam AS all the names. Kullaha (EVERYTHING) is VERY important here. It is possible to teach someone some stuff. right? I can teach someone a few things about software development. but then that person cannot be my Khaleefa. He cannot be my representative. For someone to be a true representative. he has to be taught EVERYTHING.. You understand? If Allah had taught Adam AS a few things. He could not have been a khaeefa. The fact that he was taught him EVERYTHING. ⟪ar:وَعَلَّمَ آدَمَ ٱلْأَسْمَآءَ كُلَّهَا⟫ . And Allah taught Adam ALL the names. is what made him a Khaleefa.

And this is the reason we claim that Maulana Ali was the TRUE KHALEEFA of Rasul Allah (SAS). because of this one fact.  that it was ONLY Maulana Ali that Rasul Allah taught EVERYTHING to. Did he teach things to Hazrat Abu Bakr, Hazrat Umar, Hazrat Usman as well? Sure! But did he teach them EVERYTHING? No! That's why we believe. that they could not be the true Khaleefa. the true successors of Rasul Allah. It was ONLY Maulana Ali that RasulAllah taught EVERYTHING to. And then himself testified to it.
⟪ar:انا مدینۃ العلم و علی بابھا، فمن اراد المدینۃ فلِیَاتَ الباب⟫

And a examplory proof of that is that these 3 caliphs. Hazrat Abu Bakr, Umar and Usman. Each of them turned to Maulana Ali for guidance throughout their lives. Hazrat Umar said at least 70 times. from that which has been recorded in the Sunni books. It has been recorded at least 70 times.  ⟪ar:لولا علی ھلک عمر⟫ . If it wasn't for Ali.  Umar would have been destroyed. All caliphs turned to Ali for guidance. And not anywhere we find in the seera of Maulana Ali . throughout history. be it the history books of Shias or Sunnis. where Maulana Ali turned to anyone for guidance except Allah. Just as we see we never find one event in which Rasul Allah turned to any human being for guidance except Allah. This was because he was taught EVERYTHING by Rasul Allah. thus making him the true representative. or true replacement of Rasul Allah after him.

Anyway. Returning to our topic. We were talking about why Allah gave Ibless time until judgment day.

Allah created Adam as his khaleefa by teaching him ALL the names. And then He honored him over angels by teaching HIM everything.  ⟪ar:علم آدم اسمآء کلھا⟫ . And then he honored him again by asking the angels to prostrate to him....  Now you don't give that kind of honor to just anyone....  You don't give that honor to someone you hold to a low standard... So if he made angels bow down to him. And by his association.  to us. And not just bow down...  but prostrate.. Allah made angels prostrate before us.... That means Allah must have had some seriously high expectations from us!

And so when Iblees asked for time ... time to what? To misguide us...  to mislead us....  he granted him that time.. Why? Because Allah knew.  that he created us human beings out of his love. He blessed us with innumerable gifts. Intellect being the greatest gift of all. He surrounded us with His immense mercy. He then also sent us his message. this Quran. His messengers. His true Khulafa. His represntatives.  to expalin the Quran to us. to teach us EVERYTHING we need. And through their holy lives . he set living examples of these messages for us. In addition to all of this. he gave us the gift of free will.  the capability and the strength to stand against shaytann if we CHOSE to do so.... And then his protection on top of that. The Istiaaza.. to call upon Allah when things get difficult.

Think about it. He gave us capability though the intellect. freedom of choice. the guidance of Quran to distinguish between right and wrong. His messengers to explain the Quran to us and set practical working examples for us . And then on top of that. the Istiaaza.  to call upon Allah for His protection. Have you ever seen a more partial examiner than Allah? He's like this principal who sends teachers to teach his students everything. And then puts them in the examination room to take the exam.  and then stands in the room as the invigilator. He makes it an OPEN BOOK exam. Refer to the Quran all you want.  And then on top of that He says.  if you have problems in your exams. let me know. I'll help you. I'll give you the answers. Oh And BTW. When I grade your papers. I will be EXTREMELY lenient with you.  For every correct answer. I'll give you 10 points. and for every wrong answer. I'll deduct only one point.

Where will we find such a merciful. such a kind. such a helpful. such a lenient invigilator? Have you ever heard of an examiner like this?.  SubhanAllah. He literally gave us EVERYTHING. He covered all grounds for us. There's nothing left.

And now. after all this. if I still choose to fail His exam... then I don't deserve his rewards anyway.... just on the simple principle of justice.... Some have this christian mentality where we think ... oh he is Allah... He should be all merciful... He should just give us heaven regardless. Why do we need to prove anything?

How can that make sense?.  Where is the justice in that?
⟪ar-quote:أَمْ نَجْعَلُ ٱلَّذِينَ آمَنُوا۟ وَعَمِلُوا۟ ٱلصَّلِحَتِ كَٱلْمُفْسِدِينَ فِى ٱلْأَرْضِ⟫

Should I make the one who believes and does good deeds.  equal to the one who creates mischief on this earth?
⟪ar-quote:أَمْ نَجْعَلُ ٱلْمُتَّقِينَ كَٱلْفُجَّارِ⟫

Should I make the pious equal to the wretched?

Do you want me to make an alcoholic lying cheating adulterer.  equal to an honest, pious, god loving.  god fearing momin...  Should I give them both the same reward?.  Even OUR sense of social justice would not accept that? Then how can we attribute this trait to the one who is THE MOST just of all? It just doesn't make sense...

So what we fail to understand is that when Allah gave Iblees time. who was Allah putting his trust in? Who was Allah honoring once again? He was honoring US. He was honoring us human being once again. He honored us by putting his trust in us. Just as he had honored Adam AS before us.

More than the ability of Iblee to misguide us. He trusted us MORE.  to NOT be misguided by him. Why? Because he gave us everything we need. It doesn't make any sense why we would choose Iblees over Allah. It makes no sense to Allah. That's why he said to Iblees. Fine! Do whatever you want. You will not be able to misguide my slaves.

What a disappointment we turned out to be!!

---

So that was the second part. Now the first part of this question. Why is Iblees asking time? Allah actually explains that in the next verse.

⟪ar-quote:قَالَ فَبِمَآ أَغْوَيْتَنِى لَأَقْعُدَنَّ لَهُمْ صِرَطَكَ ٱلْمُسْتَقِيمَ⟫

This is SO interesting. Iblees says.  because YOU misguided me. because YOU led me astray. Who is he talking to? He's talking to Allah. And look what he's saying. Because YOU led me astray. ⟪ar:فَبِمَآ أَغْوَيْتَنِى⟫. He is blaming Allah (Subhanhu Wa Ta'ala) for his disobedience. Iblees is blaming Allah for his misguidance. Can you see the psychological state of this guy? Complete lack of responsibility. It's not MY fault. It's YOUR fault. YOU did this to me. You gave me a command that I was not able to obey. It's all YOUR fault. I am in this position today because of what YOU did to me.

Crazy huh?

Attack from all directions

Is it? Is it really crazy? Because we do it all the time. don't we? We displace blame all the time. Instead of taking responsibility for our lack of faith. Instead of taking responsibility for our lack of will power. we blame everything else.  and everyone else around us. It's my parents fault. Its my teacher's fault. It's this school system that is so terrible. It is Islam that is so difficult. It is SO inconvenient. Why do I have to pray 5 times a day. Why do I have to fast?.  Why do I have to pay Zakaat. It's MY hard earned money. Why do I have to give it to someone else? If Allah is SO powerful. Why can't he give it to them Himself? See. Always very logical justifications. If Allah is SO powerful. why doesn't he feed the poor. They are after all His creation? Why do I have to spend MY money??

Your money? Who gave you YOUR money? Your job? Why did you get that job? Because of your education? Who got you that education? Your parents? Who gave you those parents? And their jobs and their sustenance to enable them to get your education. which led you getting your job. which led you to make the money you make. ???

So Iblees says.

⟪ar-quote:قَالَ فَبِمَآ أَغْوَيْتَنِى⟫

Because you led me astray. because of what YOU did to me.

⟪ar-quote:لَأَقْعُدَنَّ لَهُمْ صِرَطَكَ ٱلْمُسْتَقِيمَ⟫

I will now make sure I get them into trouble with you. I will mislead THEM from your straight path...  I will sit on your straight path... ⟪ar:قعد⟫means to sit. But ⟪ar:قعد⟫with a laam... ⟪ar:لَأَقْعُدَ⟫. means to sit somewhere.  in order to ambush someboday....  You know like someone waiting behind the bushes with a baseball bat.  for his enemy to come out....  that's ⟪ar:لَأَقْعُدَنَّ⟫. So he said I will sit on your right path... waiting for them...  to ambush them.... Now someone who is waiting that way. does he expose himself? No he doesnt. And does he attack all the time... or at the right moment? He waits for the right moment.  and then he attackes... So all of that is captured inside  ⟪ar:لَأَقْعُدَنَّ لَهُمْ صِرَطَكَ ٱلْمُسْتَقِيمَ⟫ . I will lurk on your straight path... Which straight path?. The straight path that they constantly seek guidance for. ⟪ar:اھدنا الصراط المستقیم⟫. Oh Allah guide me to the straight path. This is what we constantly ask Allah for in Surah Fateha.. Iblees says. I will misguide them from THAT very straight path.  they are asking guidance for. But I will not come out all the time....  I'll find that right moment...   and then I'll slip something in and slip out from there before they can realize what happened...

⟪ar-quote:ثُمَّ لَآتِيَنَّهُم مِّنۢ بَيْنِ أَيْدِيهِمْ وَمِنْ خَلْفِهِمْ وَعَنْ أَيْمَنِهِمْ وَعَن شَمَآئِلِهِمْ ۖ وَلَا تَجِدُ أَكْثَرَهُمْ شَكِرِينَ⟫

I will then come at them from right in front of them.... What is right in front of us? It's the straight path. that leads to jannah....  I will come to them and say don't go here... You don't have to wait so long for jannah man!. That's too far... Its too much of a walk.... Why tire yourself?.   You want pleasures right??...  I'll give them to you right here.... Why do you have to wait that long? I'll give you all of it right now !. And remember what we had talked about earlier... cash vs credit! Are we people of credit or are we people of cash? Iblees says I'll give you the benefits right here... In cash.. Immediately.... Jannah is credit man. Why wait?.  Who knows whether you'll even get the rewards or not! . I'm guaranteeing you all the pleasures right here. right now. You'd be so stupid to leave this visible cash. for that invisible credit. You see? Logic again.

⟪ar-quote:وَمِنْ خَلْفِهِمْ⟫

and I'll come from behind them....  pulling them back.... They'll make progress and I'll pull them back.... Even if a million things are going well for them. when ONE things goes wrong. I'll be there. How could Allah do this to you?. Look you've been SO good. You've been so obedient. Praying 5 times a day. fasting.. giving charity. He took your loved one away? . He took your job away?. You stuided so hard. He got your injured and sick. He made you fail your exam? How could he do this to you? . This is the Allah that claims to love you so much?. Again. Logic!

⟪ar-quote:وَعَنْ أَيْمَنِهِمْ وَعَن شَمَآئِلِهِمْ⟫

I'll come to them from the right and I'll come to them from the left.... Meaning, if they're in good company... doing good things... I'll attack them... If they're in bad company doing bad things I will still attack them.... Right hand is associated with good deeds... Left hand is associated with bad deeds.... He said EVEN when they are doing good things I'll slip myself in...  even when they are reading quran I'll slip myself in... that's why allah says ⟪ar:فاذا قرأت القرآن فستعذ باللہ من الشیطان الرجیم⟫.... when you are reading quran, first seek refuge of allah from shaytan...Why? I'm doing a good deed! Why do I need protection? What has shaytan got to do with a good deed?.  No I'll come at them even then...I'll attack them when they're doing good deeds, and I'll attack them when they're doing bad deeds... I wont' stop... I'll find the opportuntiy!

⟪ar-quote:وَلَا تَجِدُ أَكْثَرَهُمْ شَكِرِينَ⟫

And then you'll see... You will see that most of them will be ungrateful to you....  You're not going to find most of them on your side at all...  In other words.  I will get them to obey ME...  and when they obey me...  they will disobey you and that means they are not grateful to you!

Now notice something here. Iblees says.

⟪ar-quote:ثُمَّ لَآتِيَنَّهُم مِّنۢ بَيْنِ أَيْدِيهِمْ وَمِنْ خَلْفِهِمْ وَعَنْ أَيْمَنِهِمْ وَعَن شَمَآئِلِهِم⟫

I will come upon them from in front of them. and from behind them. and from their right . and from their left. What's interesting is that Iblees mentioned 4 directions. North South East and West. He mentioned 4 directions. But there are 6 directions. There is also top and bottom. But Iblees did not say that. He did not say. ⟪ar:ومن فوقھم و من تحتھم⟫ . I'll come upon them from above and from below them. Why is that?

The reason for that is. and this is very interesting. what comes from above is revelation. And as long as you and I have a connection with Allah. through this revelation. he will not have access to us. He cannot cut us from Allah. unless we choose to cut ourselves from Allah. And he will not come from under us.  because that is a place of humility. It's a place of Sajdah. And Iblees is arrogant. He will never put himself under us. And so as long as we are humble. in the state of Sajdah. and connected to Allah through his revelation. Ibless cannot gain any access to us.

And BTW when does Shaytan flee according to the hadees? When you're in Sajda. because he cannot bear that. It reminds him of his own disobedience. Our Sajda. is proof of his failure. Because that is the very thing he wants to prevent us from doing. That is his end game. To prevent us from being humble. To prevent us from giving up our will for the sake of Allah's will. So when we do Sajda. He knows he is defeated.

### Horiziontal vs vertical directions

So this top and bottom directions are very interesting. What this story is teaching us. is that if we place Allah in the right position. and we place ourself in our right position. which is.  that we see Allah over us. and we see ourselves under Allah . in prostration. in this state of submission. Shaytan has no access to us.

But as long as we're wandering around in this horizontal plain. which is this duniya. This duniya is the horizontal plain. As long as we're wandering in this horizontal plain. Iblees has complete access to us. But as soon as we connect with the vertical plain. Shaitan loses all access to us. That is why Allah created human beings upright. He created human beings.  vertical. on a horizontal plain.  Allah created us vertical. on a horizontal plain.

If you go horizontal. you're lying down on the job. Then Shytan gets in there. And that's why sleep is a very easy time for him to attack. That's why we do wuzu and have all these duas that we recite at the time of sleep.  So the key is. to always operate on this vertical plain. Always keep our actions aligned with the vertical plain. As soon as actions fall into the horizontal plain. for the duniya. Even if it is salaah. or Saum (fasting). as soon as it becomes horizontal. done to impress people. Iblees gets in there. And this is what happens when you decide to make a change in your life. As soon as you try to get vertical. he tries to bring you back to the horizontal plain. What about your friends? What will they say? What about your job? What about money? what about your house? What about kid's tuitions right? All concerns of the horizontal plain.

---

### Iblees blames Adam for his humiliation

So this is what Iblees says to Allah. Now I always imagine.  if I was in the place of Adam AS. What would my reaction be? . My reaction would be like. Dude. What the hell? (Maybe not hell. ) What the heck?. What did I do? It was Allah who taught me EVERYTHING. It was His decision to make me his khaleefa. He taught me everything. He asked the angels to prostrate to me. You disobeyed Him. He's kicking you out. What did I do? What did I do in any of this. Why are you mad at me??? Comeon man. Angels. Adam. Bhai Bhai. You know.. I mean seriously. right? What did poor Adam AS do in all of this. Why is he so mad at him?

I'll give you an example so you can understand this. Let's say you and your sister (or brother) are playing video games... Its your turn to play.... but your sister is not handing you the remote control... You get upset about it and you start fighting about it with her....  Your parents walks into the room....  They find out what happened....  and they yell at your sister. You need to learn to share. You have no responsibility . You're supposed to be kind to your siter.  Shame on you. The whole 9 yards. And then they snatch the remote control from her.  and hand it to you .  and then they walk out...

Now even though your sister got in trouble with your parents... But who does she look at with eyes that are now shooting lasers?.  She blames you! Its all YOUR fault! I HATE you so much! Because of YOU! I got into trouble. Everything was fine before you came in my life!. Everything was great before YOU were born. My life was great!. You screwed up my life!. There is nothing wrong with me... I DONT HAVE AN ANGER PROBLEM. Its YOU that made me look bad.... You understand?

Iblees asks allah for time.... why? Because he got into trouble with Allah BECAUSE of Adam AS. because of this human species... He believes that had it not been for the creation of Adam.. he would always have retained his elevated status.... It doesn't make sense right? . But that's the thing. Iblees is insane. He's in a state of constant. never ending rage. And when you're angry, what happens? . You can't think straight.  So he now has this serious grudge against the human race... In his mind ... he blames us... Iblees was extremely close to Allah...  and now he has been humiliated because of the presence of who? Human beings! So he develops this severe hatred for human beings... so now he says.. Oh Allah... Let me prove to you.  that you made the wrong choice! Let me prove to you ...  you should not have honored them... You should have honored me!. I'll prove to you. that you made a mistake. I should not have been the one in trouble... THEY should be the one in trouble.. Just give me time until judgment day... and I will prove it to you! You will see that MOST of them are not going to be grateful to you.

⟪ar-quote:وَلَا تَجِدُ أَكْثَرَهُمْ شَكِرِينَ⟫

And that's why he asks Allah for time.

⟪ar-quote:قَالَ أَنظِرْنِىٓ إِلَىٰ يَوْمِ يُبْعَثُونَ⟫

Give me time until judgment day . and I'll prove it to you. that they are not worthy of this honor you bestowed upon them.  Allah says

⟪ar-quote:قَالَ إِنَّكَ مِنَ ٱلْمُنظَرِينَ⟫

Fine! I give you time till that day!

So Iblees challenges Allah. and He accepts his EVERY challenge? And why wouldn't He? It's not like Allah is scared of Iblees. But when Iblees challenges Adam and his children. Allah accepts to put them to the test. Because like I said. He gave them EVERYTHING they will ever need to meet this challenge. Why would they not choose Allah over Iblees?

And you know. in Hadees. this dialog between Iblees and Allah has been much further explained. Syedna Ghulam Hussain Sahab QR. he writes in his book Qatrunnida. He writes that Iblees actually didn't just ask for time. he asked for strength and power from Allah. Iblees said Allow me the power to dominate these human beings through their desires. Allah said.  I'll allow that for you. Iblees said. for every son that Adam has. allow me to have two sons. so that I am double in strength than them.  Allah said I'll allow that.. Iblees said. Allow me to make a home in the chest of the children of Adam. and allow my influences to flow through their lives.  just as their blood flows through their veins. Allah said I'll allow that. Iblees said. Allow me to attack them with my ground as well as air forces. meaning use both humans and jinn to attack them. so that we can mix and mingle into their wealth and to confuse them with false hopes and vain promises. Allah said I will allow that too.

When Adam AS heard all this. He sorta freaked out. Oh Allah. What are you doing? You've allowed Iblees and his army to become SO powerful. I and my children will get crushed under his attack. How are we going to defend ourselves against him?

Allah said. Don't worry Adam. With every child of yours. I will assign a protector. whose only job will be to protect him against the attack of Shaytan.  if he chooses to listen to him. (that's our conscience) . 

Adam says. Ya Allah give us more. Allah says. OK Listen. For every good deed that they do. I will record it as 10 good deeds . and every siin they commit. I'll record it only once. and if they repent on it. I will completely erase it.

Adam says. Ya Allah give us more. Allah says. OK Listen.Go Tell you children. to never despair in the mercy of their master. My mercy will always accompany them no matter how disobedient they are.

Adam says. Ya Allah give us more. Allah says. OK Listen.Go tell them I will never close the door of repentence on them. Till their very last breadth they will have the opportunity to repent and seek my forgiveness and when they do. I WILL forgive them.

Adam says. Ya Allah give us more. Allah says. OK Listen. Go tell your children. that no matter how many times they repent and seek my forgiveness. I will keep on forgiving them over and over again. and I will not even maintain an account of how many times I've forgiven them for that very same sin. 

That's when Adam AS said. That's enough my master. What you have given us is now more than enough for us to stand our ground against Iblees and his army.

---

After accepting Iblee's challenge. Allah says.
⟪ar-quote:قَالَ ٱخْرُجْ مِنْهَا مَذْءُومًۭا مَّدْحُورًۭا⟫

Allah says get out of my paradise. with disgrace and as someone who has been expelled. Leave like someone who has been humiliated. and do whatever you want to do to misguide the children of Adam.
⟪ar-quote:لَّمَن تَبِعَكَ مِنْهُمْ⟫

Whoever follows you among them.... Now look. Allah didn't say whoever disbelieves in me....  that's not the condition he palced... The only conditioin he put here is that whoever listens to you... Whoever pays attention to you and follows you from among them..
⟪ar-quote:لَأَمْلَأَنَّ جَهَنَّمَ مِنكُمْ أَجْمَعِينَ⟫

I will fill hellfire with all of you together.

Wait. What???. Fill hellfire with all of you???? . Where did that come from? . Allah is talking about Iblees and his army. He should have said. I will fill hellfire with them. But he didn't say. ⟪ar:منھم اجمعین⟫... . He said. ⟪ar:منکم اجمعین⟫. He doesnt' say all of THEM... he says all of YOU!.  This is actually ⟪ar:لی الطوعیۃ⟫ to scare you.. ⟪ar:لی التحدید⟫  to challenge you ...  The one reading quran is like.. wait!. Where did YOU come from? I thought allah is going to say...  I will fill hell fire with THEM....  he says I will fill hell with you!.  You're reading the book and all of a sudden its pointing at you! Its pointing at you and me! Wait ME???? OMG I better not follow Iblees! Because the only way its pointing at me.. is if I follow Iblees.... So this switch in subject.  is actually a means of warning and terrifying us.... And its used all over the place in Quran.

---

### Allah giving Adam everything

Now after expelling Iblees. Allah addresses Adam and Hawwa. and says

⟪ar-quote:وَيَٓـَٔادَمُ ٱسْكُنْ أَنتَ وَزَوْجُكَ ٱلْجَنَّةَ⟫

Adam, you and your wife settle down in Jannah. Now notice this word Zawj. The word Zawj. actually means "companion". or partner. Allah referred to Adam and Hawwa as partners. The reason I'm pointing this out is because some men have this thinking. Some mother in laws have this thinking for their sons. that when it comes to their perfect sons. that husband wife relationship is a master slave relationship. It's not. If it were.  Allah would have said.  ⟪ar:وَيَٓـَٔادَمُ ٱسْكُنْ أَنتَ وَعَبدُک⟫. Oh Adam. You and your slave settle down in Jannah.  He didn't say that. He used the word Zawj. partner. a companion.

Anyway. Allah says. ⟪ar:ٱسْكُنْ أَنتَ وَزَوْجُكَ ٱلْجَنَّةَ⟫. And Allah did not even say Fil Jannah. meaning he did not point to a specific place or a location in Jannah. He said AlJannah... Meaning all of heaven.... Allah says your new home is Jannah itself..  You're not moving into one house. inside a city. within a state of Jannah. The whole thing is your house..  Every building there, every house there, every location there, all of it is your house. Adam and Hawwa. take it. Take all ofit !. And then he says .

⟪ar-quote:فَكُلَا مِنْ حَيْثُ شِئْتُمَا⟫

Eat and drink from whatever you desire! You don't have to check the label on any thing! Everything is haalal..  Eat and enjoy. And it's not like.  one thing is going to be like.. ahh..  That was not so good..  We should go to that one! That's us and restaurants..  Sometimes the biryani comes out good sometimes it doesn't. But in Jannah, eat whatever you want.. Everything is going to be AWESOME. ALL THE TIME. But then he says:
⟪ar-quote:وَلَا تَقْرَبَا هَذِهِ ٱلشَّجَرَةَ فَتَكُونَا مِنَ ٱلظَّلِمِينَ⟫

But do not go near this one tree or you will be from among the wrong doers.  Allah forbids them to go near one tree.... Not much attention is paid to the word ⟪ar:هَذِهِ⟫... THIS tree! Allah did not say: ⟪ar:تلک شرجۃ⟫... That tree! He did not say THAT tree.  He said THIS tree. What's the difference between this and that?.  This is near... So the harraam is always near ... the haraam. the forbidden.  is ALWAYS near.... Allah said to them. You have a LOT of options. in what is permissible.  But don't think the forbidden is far.  it's always going to be near..  And if it is near.  you have to watch out for it..  So you can never say I'm far from the haraam...  As big as this universe of Jannah is.  BTW how big is jannah? Allah says...
⟪ar-quote:وَجَنَّةٍ عَرْضُهَا ٱلسَّمَوَتُ وَٱلْأَرْضُ⟫

It's size is something like all seven heavens and the earth combined... The Size of jannah.  is the size of all seven heavens and the earth combined! And that would be something that compared to Jannah but not exactly... Today we have telescopes that provide us with magnification into the universe that humanity has never seen before....  And Allah says. this huge expanse still does not compare to the size of Jannah. And even though Jannah is so huge. Allah uses the word THIS to indicate the forbidden tree. He made this closeness. this accessibility to the forbidden. a part of the challenge for humanity.  That the forbidden will ALWAYS be close to you. It will ALWAYS be accessible to you.  and it will pique your curiosity!

I know it's Haraam ....I'm just curious! I'm not doing anything.  I'm just wondering! I wonder when beer tastes like? I'm never going to drink it! I just want to know what it tastes like!. I want to know what smoking feels like. I'll give it up after one. I'm just curious.  You know.  just wondering. Just wanna try it once.  So this is: ⟪ar:وَلَا تَقْرَبَا هَذِهِ ٱلشَّجَرَةَ⟫

And by the way.... something very interesting. Allah did not say. لا تأكل من هذه الشجرة.  He did not say. Do not EAT from this tree. He said. do not go near this tree. The command is not . Because it's not the tree we're interested in, right? We're interested in eating the fruit. Allah says don't even go near the tree. My command is not about the fruit. My command is for the tree. Do not even go near the tree. You know what that means? . It's not don't drink alcohol. It means don't even go near alcohol. It doesn't mean don't do drugs. It means don't even go near drugs. It's not don't get involved in shameless. It means don't even go near shamelessness.

And if you do. what happens?
⟪ar-quote:فَتَكُونَا مِنَ ٱلظَّلِمِينَ⟫

You will become from among the wrong doers.

Look. We can't wrong Allah. We can't harm Allah. It's not like there is anything we can do to hurt Allah. But we can transgress on a Haqq. On a right of Allah. we can transgress on what is due to Allah. And what is due. is that Allah is obeyed when he tells us to do something. That is his right on us as our creator. and that is His right on us as our master and benefactor.

---

⟪ar-quote:### how did Iblees humiliate Adam?

فَوَسْوَسَ لَهُمَا ٱلشَّيْطَنُ⟫

Now this is the verse that I actually want to share with you. If we understand this.  then we understand the true intentions of Iblees.  Now so far.  we've established that he is our worst enemy.. Iblees or Shaytan hates us. and he is out for revenge. Now what was the worst thing that happened to him? He got kicked out? Yes!.  But getting kicked out of Jannah was the half of it!. The real thing is. when that happened.... how do you think he felt inside?.  He felt humiliated... and humiliation is one of the greatest pains that creation can suffer.... Any creation with dignity can feel humiliation.... Animals don't feel humiliated because they don't have any digntity....  Apparently Iblees had dignity too.... He had a sense of resepect for himslef.... And when he was thrown out of jannah.  he felt humiliated.... And for that humiliation he wants to take revenge against humanity...

Now what would be the ultimate revenge against humanity? Because if some how.  he could get human beings to get humiliated... If he could somehow do that... He can feel he has accomplished something...  So how does he do that? Through waswasa...

⟪ar-quote:فَوَسْوَسَ لَهُمَا ٱلشَّيْطَنُ⟫

So shaytan does waswas to both of them....  Now what Allah could have said here is. ⟪ar:فَوَسْوَسَ الیہم⟫. Shytan whispered To them. But instead he said.⟪ar:فَوَسْوَسَ لَهُمَا⟫ .  and the usage of lahuma . indicates a very specific intent. In other words Shaytan had a very specific goal here.⟪ar:فَوَسْوَسَ لَهُمَا⟫ . He whispered to them for a very particular reason. I told you earlier. He does waswasa in SO many ways. In uncontable ways. Anger. jealousy. greed. pride.. contempt. so many different ways. But ultimate he has ONLY one single goal. What is that? Allah tells us as the ayah continues. ⟪ar:لی.... لِيُبْدِیَ لَھُمَا  ...⟫

You notice this Laam before ⟪ar:يُبْدِیَ⟫. This Laam with a zer. This word ⟪ar:لی⟫has a mountain within it....  It tells us everything.... It tells us the ULTIMATE goal of shaytann...  Allah says.. ⟪ar:فَوَسْوَسَ لَهُمَا ٱلشَّيْطَنُ⟫ Shaytan whispered to both of them... LEE.  for the reason....

Why do you think Shaytan whispered to them? What do you think was his ultimate agenda? Now I would guess.  Because he wanted them to disobey allah.... or Because he wanted to get them both kicked out from janna... or Because he wanted them to disbelieve.... or Because he wanted them to go to hell fire....  or because because because... right?

But Allah says let me tell you what his ultimate agenda was....

⟪ar-quote:لِيُبْدِىَ لَهُمَا مَا وُۥرِىَ عَنْهُمَا مِن سَوْءَتِهِمَا⟫

So that.  he could expose to them ... THAT which was covered of their ugliness. . .  Shaytans ultimate agenda.  was to get clothes removed from Adam and Hawwa AS....  That's what he wanted.... We really have to stop and think here.... I was thinking that Allah would say.... Shaytan wanted them to eat from the tree... right? Because Allah had said don't go near this tree! . Therefore I thought shaytan would want them to eat from the tree.... Allah says.. NO!.  That was not shaytan's real agneda....  His real agneda was humiliation... And he knew.  through his own personal expreience.  that disobeying allah would end up in humiliataiton.... And what would be the ULTIMATE form of humiliation? The ultimate humiliation would be....  that the greatest gift of jannah... The libaas... the clothes of jannah be removed from them.  Because if you are disqualified from jannah... What are you no longer qualified for? The clothes of jannah! 

The clothes that adam and Hawwa were wearing.  were the clothes of jannah...  Clothing was a gift from allah... It was the FIRST gift given to Adam AS to honor him.  because before him no one had ever worn clothes. Allah did not create us with clothes... When we come into the world... we do not have clothes on.... Animals are born with their clothes. Animals are born with their fur or leather or whatever. We are not. Clothing is the first GIFT our parents give us... by covering us and our private parts.... Because when Allah created human beings. you know what he said to the angels?.

⟪ar-quote:وَإِذْ قَالَ رَبُّكَ لِلْمَلَٓئِكَةِ إِنِّى خَلِقٌۢ بَشَرًۭا⟫. And when their master said to the angels. I am creating bashar. You know what the word bashar comes from? It comes from bishar... meaning skin....  Allah created a creature that was just skin... But then Allah clothed that creature... He gave him a gift of his own... that human beings were not originally created with... so clothing itself is a divine gift... and Shaytan wants those clothes removed...  Now let's look at the ayah. word by word...

⟪ar-quote:لِيُبْدِىَ لَهُمَا مَا وُۥرِىَ عَنْهُمَا مِن سَوْءَتِهِمَا⟫

⟪ar:لِيُبْدِىَ لَهُمَا⟫. so he could expose to both of them... ⟪ar:مَا وُۥرِىَ عَنْهُمَا⟫. what was covered up .. wrapped up .. and kept a secret... ⟪ar:مِن سَوْءَتِهِمَا⟫. This word just bafles me... Allah could have used so many different words... ⟪ar:من جسمیھما ، من اعضائھما ، من بدنیھما⟫.. from their bodies.. from their body parts... but he said  ⟪ar:مِن سَوْءَتِهِمَا⟫

⟪ar:سوئا⟫is used in arabic for something that is ugly... Something that is disgusting... Something that is evil....  Humans beings explosed without clothes...  in public...  is something evil, something ugly...  something disgusting ...  It is something indecent inherently...  You know.. ⟪ar:سوئا⟫is also used in the Quran for a decaying corpse... Allah says..

⟪ar-quote:فَبَعَثَ ٱللَّهُ غُرَابًۭا يَبْحَثُ فِى ٱلْأَرْضِ لِيُرِيَهُۥ كَيْفَ يُوَرِى سَوْءَةَ أَخِيهِ⟫

When qabeel killed habeel AS... Allah sent a crow to show qabeel how to hide the ⟪ar:سوئا⟫the decaying corpse of habeel AS...  A corpse is not something you wanna look at... It is someting that is inherently ugly...

You know in the nature. in the fitra of the human beings... It is not tempting to look at nudity....  but when our nature gets corrupt... . .  Allah created us with a beautiful nature...  but when that nature gets corrupt... when it gets distorted the desire to look at nudity rises...  and if we have that temptation over whelming us....  then that means something is corrupted in our nature...  something has been removed... Because inherently nudity is called ugliness in the quran... Nudity itself is called uglines.. ⟪ar:سوئاتھما⟫.. Thats what its called.... .  something really to think about...

And what better revenge. than to humiliate human beings by getting them to disboey Allah... Because what happens when we disobey Allah. What does it result in? It results in our clothes!. the very thing that honors us over beasts. The very thing that makes us look beautiful. These clothes get stirpped off of us.

The story of adam AS teaches us that Shaytan's ultimate agenda is to humiliate us.  by having humanity remove its clothes.... When dresses get shorter and shorter.... clothes get tighter and tighter.  When images get filthier and filthier... When ads generally start promoting...  there's no harm in showing a little skin... When the porn industry becomes trillions of dollars...  Then shaytan sits back and says....  I am accomplishing my goal... I am getting my job done... This is what I always wanted to do....  For the children of Adam to remove their clothes... and be delighted in exposing their bodies.... WOW! I am now finally getting my revenge.  for my humilation. because now I've taken their dignity away... Because what is the sign of dignity? Shame! Shame is the sign of dignity... And shaytan says I've taken their shame away..

Look what's happening in the world of design today? Look what's happening in the world of enterntainment today? How are we justifying ourselves watching shows that say... Following has explict content... We're like.... Oh.. it said SOME sexual content... It had the word SOME in it... I can forward that part... (after I've watched it)... Or I'll just watch the begining of it... and then say Ohhh. Astaghfirullah... that was disgusinting...

But you see. This is what shaytan wants....  He knew that human beings will lose their dignity if they lose their clothes....  Today we live in times...  where losing clothing is celebrated!.  it's literally celebrated...  Why do most youngsters work out today? To show their 6 pack abbs. And you can't show your abs with your clothes on can you? Girls dressing in provocative manners. so that they get the attention of boys. Really? Do we really need to take off your clothes to get attention? Is our self-esteem really that low?  You know women of a certain profession used to dress that way no too long ago. And that was their only purpose. to get attention.

Look guys I'm just talking to you like your mamu or khaloo . or like your older brother...  I'm not telling you what to do....  I'm just pointing things out... as the Quran is stating it to us.  I'm not enjoying talking about this. any more than you're enjoying listening to it. This is not easy stuff to talk about. But if I don't say this. If I'm afraid to point this out. Then what am I doing here?. What are we doing here. if we're not willing to have these difficult conversations?

My daughter will have to hear this from me too... I'm just telling you like it is...  like the Quran says it... And the point of telling you all this is not so that I call you out... The point is that you call yourself out... YOU have to make that choice... that you are not going to let shaytan trick you into believing that this is the way in which you will look beautiful....  Because it is not... It really is not.... Exposing yourself for the attention and the dirty looks of other men.That's sad. It's pathetic that we feel the need to expose our bodies in public.  just to look beautiful....  This is for people who don't have anything higher to aim for.  this is for people who cannot find any other meaning in life... This is for them... This is not for us as Muslims.... This is not for us momins.  We have a purpose...  We have a higher goal... We have a direction...

And I'm not saying you should not dress nicely.... Girls have a natural tendency to dress nicely.... By all means... Look. We guys have no problem dressing like homeless people. We're fine with that . Girls want to look beautiful.. That's great! Look beautiful... but look beautiful by means of your clothing...  not by removing it.  You don't have to look beautiful by being provocative.  and you're smart enough to know the difference...

Because we are playing right into the hands of Shaytan. We are doing EXACTLY what he wants us to do. When we lose our clothing. Imagine if accidentally your clothes fell off before your parents. imagine how embaressed you would feel. And He wants us to lose our clothing before Allah. He is dishonoring us before Allah. And we are constantly making his job easy. This is REALLY something to think about.

We looked at the difference between fire and clay. remember? Nudity is the very nature of fire. hence the term "a naked flame". Soil or clay. its very nature is to veil and cover up. We momins. we Sulemani's . we are not people of fire. we are people of clay. We are not children of Iblees. We are children of Adam. The world is playing with fire. because they have chosen to follow the one who is made from fire. Who is going to end up in fire and take all of them with him. May Allah guide them too.

But we are not people of fire. We are people of clay. The one we follow is not made from fire. he is made from clay.

These people who are blindly following their passsions. atleast they have a reason. At least they have a reason of misguidance.. They don't know any better.. They don't have access to the wisdom of Quran. But you and I do. So our lives . our thinking needs to be different.

⟪ar-quote:وَلَقَدْ خَلَقْنَكُمْ ثُمَّ صَوَّرْنَكُمْ ثُمَّ قُلْنَا لِلْمَلَٓئِكَةِ ٱسْجُدُوا۟ لِآدَمَ فَسَجَدُوٓا۟ إِلَّآ إِبْلِيسَ لَمْ يَكُن مِّنَ ٱلسَّجِدِينَ⟫

⟪ar-quote:قَالَ مَا مَنَعَكَ أَلَّا تَسْجُدَ إِذْ أَمَرْتُكَ ۖ قَالَ أَنَا۠ خَيْرٌۭ مِّنْهُ خَلَقْتَنِى مِن نَّارٍۢ وَخَلَقْتَهُۥ مِن طِينٍۢ⟫

⟪ar-quote:قَالَ فَٱهْبِطْ مِنْهَا فَمَا يَكُونُ لَكَ أَن تَتَكَبَّرَ فِيهَا فَٱخْرُجْ إِنَّكَ مِنَ ٱلصَّغِرِينَ⟫

⟪ar-quote:قَالَ أَنظِرْنِىٓ إِلَىٰ يَوْمِ يُبْعَثُونَ⟫

⟪ar-quote:قَالَ إِنَّكَ مِنَ ٱلْمُنظَرِينَ⟫

⟪ar-quote:قَالَ فَبِمَآ أَغْوَيْتَنِى لَأَقْعُدَنَّ لَهُمْ صِرَطَكَ ٱلْمُسْتَقِيمَ⟫

⟪ar-quote:ثُمَّ لَآتِيَنَّهُم مِّنۢ بَيْنِ أَيْدِيهِمْ وَمِنْ خَلْفِهِمْ وَعَنْ أَيْمَنِهِمْ وَعَن شَمَآئِلِهِمْ ۖ وَلَا تَجِدُ أَكْثَرَهُمْ شَكِرِينَ⟫

⟪ar-quote:قَالَ ٱخْرُجْ مِنْهَا مَذْءُومًۭا مَّدْحُورًۭا ۖ لَّمَن تَبِعَكَ مِنْهُمْ لَأَمْلَأَنَّ جَهَنَّمَ مِنكُمْ أَجْمَعِينَ⟫

⟪ar-quote:وَيَٓـَٔادَمُ ٱسْكُنْ أَنتَ وَزَوْجُكَ ٱلْجَنَّةَ فَكُلَا مِنْ حَيْثُ شِئْتُمَا وَلَا تَقْرَبَا هَذِهِ ٱلشَّجَرَةَ فَتَكُونَا مِنَ ٱلظَّلِمِينَ⟫

⟪ar-quote:فَوَسْوَسَ لَهُمَا ٱلشَّيْطَنُ لِيُبْدِىَ لَهُمَا مَا وُۥرِىَ عَنْهُمَا مِن سَوْءَتِهِمَا⟫

Deception of IBLEES - through Logic

⟪ar-quote:وَقَالَ مَا نَهَىٰكُمَا رَبُّكُمَا عَنْ هَذِهِ ٱلشَّجَرَةِ⟫

Iblees said to them. The only reason Allah prevented you from approaching this tree.  is because if you did that.  two things could happen.
⟪ar-quote:إِلَّآ أَن تَكُونَا مَلَكَيْنِ⟫

Either you would turn into angels. 
⟪ar-quote:أَوْ تَكُونَا مِنَ ٱلْخَلِدِينَ⟫

or you will become people who live in the janah forever.  And Allah obviously doesn't want that for you.

This logic sound familiar? The only reason my parents are stopping me from doing this is because. dot dot dot. Obviously they don't understand. Obviously they don't love me. right?

Now let's try to understand, what tempted both of them.  We already learned in Surah Baqarah.  Allah said :
⟪ar-quote:وَإِذْ قَالَ رَبُّكَ لِلْمَلَٓئِكَةِ إِنِّى جَاعِلٌۭ فِى ٱلْأَرْضِ خَلِيفَةًۭ⟫

And Allah said to the angels, I am going to create a representative that is going to live on earth. Live where? . Earth. That was Allah's declaration right from the start. That I am creating a representative. a caliph for the earth. not for the heavens. not for Jannah. .  But Adam was living currently where? In Jannah.  And in Jannah, you would think that they would live forever.  But Allah said:
⟪ar-quote:وَقُلْنَا يَٓـَٔادَمُ ٱسْكُنْ أَنتَ وَزَوْجُكَ ٱلْجَنَّةَ⟫

And Allah said to Adam, Settle! Settle here! ⟪ar:ٱسْكُنْ⟫. Allah did not say ⟪ar:اُخلُد فیھا⟫.  Those of you who read the quran. You know how when Allah describes a Jannah, he does not say ⟪ar:فیھا ساکنین⟫،  instead what does He says ⟪ar:فیھا خالدین⟫.khalid means to live for ever! .

So when Allah described the creation of Adam to the angels. He said I'm creating him for the earth. And also when he spoke to Adam and Hawwa about their stay in heaven. He said. Settle here!. ⟪ar:ٱسْكُنْ أَنتَ وَزَوْجُكَ ٱلْجَنَّةَ⟫ and the word sakana actually comes from sukoon. Not the urdu sukoon. بڑے سکون سے بیٹھے ہوئے ہیں۔ . not that sukoon.  When you learn to read the quran.  there is fatha, kasra, damma, shadda and sukoon.  what is sukoon? When you temporarily stop moving.  you stop temporarily on the letter that has sukoon on it.  so sukoon means to stop temporarily.  So there was motion before as you were reading.  and then you stop.  That does not indicate necessarily.  that the stop is permanent. If the stop was permanent.  than the word used would have been: ⟪ar:خُلد⟫. You understand?

Instead of saying. ⟪ar:ٱسْكُنْ أَنتَ وَزَوْجُكَ⟫ . Allah would have said ⟪ar:أُخلُد أَنتَ وَزَوْجُكَ⟫. So when Allah announced to adam AS and his wife Hawwa. Settle down here.  He said stop here.  But he did not say stop here forever.  And He already did announce to the angels earlier.  that I am creating Adam for where? for the earth. ⟪ar:إِنِّى جَاعِلٌۭ فِى ٱلْأَرْضِ خَلِيفَةًۭ⟫

So the ANGELS. actually knew.  that Adam AS was created.  not for Jannah.  but for the earth.  They knew that he is going to play that role until he finally makes it back to Jannah.  This was all part of Allah's original plan.  Now even though the angels knew. Did Adam AS know that? . NO!. Because all this dialog. between Allah and the angels.  happened BEFORE Adam was created. So the specific details about their eventual residence. the angels knew. Iblees knew. But Adam and Hawwa did not know. Because when Allah made this announcement to the angels, they hadn't been created . But when Allah spoke to both of them. and told them to settle temporarily in jannah. they knew that their stay in Jannah is temporary. and not permanent.  You understand? . They knew their stay is temporary. but they had no idea that they were never created for Jannah in the first place.  And that is what Iblees took advantage of.

So Iblees came to Adam, and said.  Hey guys! Listen.  The two conditions for people who get to live in jannah forever are. ⟪ar:إِلَّآ أَن تَكُونَا مَلَكَيْنِ⟫. either you are angels.  OR  ⟪ar:أَوْ تَكُونَا مِنَ ٱلْخَلِدِينَ⟫you need to have permanent residence.  You need to have a green card in order to live here.  Now you are clearly not any Angels!.  Therefore the only way that you can live here.  is that if you get a green card.  And the way to get that green card.  the way to get that permanent residence.  is to eat from this tree. Because the permanent residents are called Khalideen.  So if you're not an angel.  and I'm pretty sure you're not going to become an angel anytime soon. so the ONLY other option you have. the only play you have.  is that you apply for a green card.  And the way to do that is what? . Eat from the tree.  That is IF you like Jannah!. That's all I'm sayin.  I'm sure you enjoyed a little bit here didn't you? .  Look man!. I mean well! I'm your friend! and I really like you guys.  I want you to stay in Jannah! . But unfortunately.  the only two options that you guys have.  is to either be an angel.  which is obviously not gonna happen .  or you eat from the tree . So the way I see it. you guys really don't have a choice.

So this is how Iblees approached them. With logic of survival. You see. This is the greatest challenge of all. Iblees comes with perfect logic that is grounded in the seen. and he makes that conflict with faith that exists in the UNSEEN. He makes us choose between cash and credit. making CASH. the only SMART choice. That's a REALLY CRAZY challenge. a REALLY CHALLENGING test we as human beings are put into.

So this is how Iblees tries to confuse them. But they both don't believe him. So what does Iblees do? He swears to both of them.
⟪ar-quote:وَقَاسَمَهُمَآ إِنِّى لَكُمَا لَمِنَ ٱلنَّصِحِينَ⟫

And then he swore to both of them that I am from your well-wishers. Iblees swore to them by Allah. ⟪ar:اُقسِم باللہ⟫.

Now you see. this is Iblees. He'll go to any lengths to do what he needs to do. So he lies to both of them. And you have to understand something here. Adam and Hawwa. they did not have any concept of lies. All they ever knew was the truth.  Because they had never heard anyone lie before. And also in this ayah. Iblees says.
⟪ar-quote:إِنِّى لَكُمَا لَمِنَ ٱلنَّصِحِينَ⟫

Now in balagha. in Arabic rheoteric. when you say ⟪ar:أِنی. انی یقول ھذا.⟫ That's called ⟪ar:مُترَدِّد⟫. means you're speaking to someone who is doubting you. He's not sure. maybe he believes you . maybe he doesn't. So when you use ⟪ar:انی .⟫It's like saying. I know you doubt me. but I'm assuring you that I'm telling you the truth. But when you use a Laam. the second time along with Inni. .⟪ar:إِنِّى **لَ**كُمَا **لَ**مِنَ ٱلنَّصِحِينَ⟫.  He didn't say. ⟪ar:مِنَ ٱلنَّصِحِينَ⟫ . He said. ⟪ar:**لَ**مِنَ ٱلنَّصِحِينَ⟫ . That's for someone who does not believe you AT ALL. So Iblees used that to say. I know you don't believe me AT ALL. but I'm swearing to the utmost. that I'm telling you the truth. That's the language he's using. In other words. believe me. I swear I'm sincere with you.

Now here's two people who don't even know what a lie is. because they're in that pure state. and then they see this creation of Allah. swearing by his creator. ⟪ar:وَقَاسَمَهُمَآ⟫. It was simply unthinkable to them . that somebody could swear by Allah and lie. That was something that was completely unthinkable to them. . that's what they fell for. Iblees tempted them for the longest time.  as we'll learn in the next ayah. They did not immediately fall into temptation.  But when Iblees swore by Allah.  they believed him. That's how he got to them. The point is Iblees will go to any extremes.

We think. how could he deceive me. How could she wanna hurt me?. She's my best friend. He's my best friend. NO. You can't put anything past Shaytan. Or someone who is under the control of Shaytan.  He'll go to the most extreme ends to do what he needs to do.

---

⟪ar-quote:فَدَلَّىٰهُمَا بِغُرُورٍۢ⟫

⟪ar:دلا⟫in arabic is a verb.  ⟪ar:تدلیۃ⟫. the infinitive verb is actually used when you have a bucket.  and you have a rope attached to that bucket.  and then you pull the bucket slowly. little by little by little. If you pull it immediatley. if you pull it hard and fast.  it's ⟪ar:ادلا⟫.  if you pull it slowly. then its ⟪ar:دلا⟫. In the story of Yusuf AS when his brothers left him in a well. a caravan passed by and put a buket in the well for water.  and when they pulled it out.  a boy came out sitting in the bucket. in that ayah what did Allah says.
⟪ar-quote:وَجَآءَتْ سَيَّارَةٌۭ فَأَرْسَلُوا۟ وَارِدَهُمْ.  فَأَدْلَىٰ دَلْوَهُ⟫

Here the word Adlaa is used. implying that they pulled the rope hard and fast. and the bucket.  with the boy in it came up rather quickly. Now you and I know a boy is not that light. so it must still have taken some time to pull it up right? But that is still ⟪ar:ادلا⟫. . But when Iblees is described figuratively.  that when he took adam and hawwa AS . and he yanked them out of jannah.  like a bucket is pulled out of a well.  Allah uses the word ⟪ar:دلا⟫. meaning.  he took his sweet time.

You guys are like modern age kids.  I don't know if you ever watched old school cartoons like Tom and Jerry!. Tom is a cat. Jerry is a mouse. Tom has a piece of cheese in a bucket.  and there is a rope tied to the bucket.  Jerry smells the cheese and then as he approaches the bucket.  Tom slowly pulls the bucket towards him.  and then a little more, and a little more. and a little more. And Jerry does what?. He keep walking towards Tom until he finally catches jerry.  So Tom is using the bucket.  to lure Jerry. very very slowly. very unnoticable.    That in Arabic is called ⟪ar:دلا⟫

In other words. Iblees didnt just walk up to them and say Hey! That fruit on that tree. .aaaa haa haaa haaa. so tasty man!!. Eat it . Do it! Do it!. It didn't happen that way. And it's also not like he walked up to them and said. Hey you! Eat from that tree. and they both said.  Ahh OK! No no no no no. He did waswassa to them over and over and over again. he came in the morning. he came in the evening.  he came at night. Hey! You hungry? you guys hungry? I know this one tree. Now jannah has countless trees . right? Jannah is way bigger than the earth. so how difficult would it have been to find this one haraam tree? Think about that!. Of all the trees in the entire universe of jannah. there is one that is haraam. And shaytan had to first GPS them back to that one haraam tree.  little by little.  Hey why don't you take this turn? why don't you go over here? Hey check those strawberrys out. they look pretty yummy. don't they?. Drink from this river. it's so sweet. 

So ⟪ar:دلا⟫suggests.  he didn't immediately call them to the haraaam.  He got them to it very slowly.  in a calculated manner. Hey. checkout this water fall. go to that mountain. taste this mango. then go over here. then go over here.  And they're listening to him. and they're thinking this has nothing to do with what? A larger plan!. .  They don't see it.  that this is part of a larger plan! And Allah is teaching us that is exactly what Shaytan does! . This is what he did to them. and this is what he does to us.

He tempts you into doing something.  And when you do it at first. .  "It's not haraam!.  I mean its not like TOTALLY haraam. It's not like its ABSOLUTELY TOTALLY COMPLETELY haraam". At least I'm not doing dot dot dot.  that's where you fill in your creativity.  So what if I have a girl friend? So what if i have a boy friend. We're just friends. We're having a fun time together.  I enjoy talking to her.  I enjoy talking to him. At least we're not . dot dot dot. It's just a cigarette. It's not even lit. I just like holding it. It's not like I'm dot dot dot. I'm in love with her. I'm in love with him. What sort of a religion comes in between two lovers. All very compelling logic.

But the thing is.  shaytan will not get you to the destination immediately. He only wants you to get to the first milestone. because from there.  he will work on you for a month or two.  to get you to the next milestone. And then to the third one . and then to the fourth. Eventually you will end up doing THAT very thing.  that you said in the beginning. at least I'm not doing dot dot dot. You'll now be doing EXACTLY that. And guess what. When you do it. You will still have a GREAT logical justifications for it.

But he won't get you to that point immediately. he will work on you slowly. very slowly. That's  ⟪ar:فَدَلَّىٰهُمَا بِغُرُورٍۢ⟫. He lures very slowly using deception

He'll work on a guy and a girl to develop an illicit relationship very slowly. He'll start things in the most innocent manner. Oh she's just my study partner. She's just helping me with my biology assignments. It's all good. We'll meet in this house. we'll study right in front of you. we'll keep the door open. We're just two friends studying. it's not like we're. dot dot dot. right?

And then slowly. after a few weeks. So what movie do you like?. Who's your favorite actor. Oh really ??? Mine too!. Hey his movie is playing tonight. wanna check it out?. Now parents ask. why are you going to the movies with him? . . Why is it haraam? Is watching a movie harram?.  I can't even watch a movie?. Does Islam say it's haraam to watch a movie with another person?. 

Now parents cant tell you that its haraam. But it's not the movie they're worried about. are they? . Becaue they know what shaytan is doing. just a little . just a tiny turn here and there. So are you on facebook? Of course I am. Actually I already looked you up. Little by little. and then the late night texting begins. oh we're just texting. Is texting haraam? I can't even text someone now? Is whatsapp haraam???.  It was just a picture we shared. wasn't even a video. One justification. then another justification. It's just a dinner.  its with the whole school group. It's about learning Biology.  UmmmHmmmm. Yeah. I know! I know what biology you're learing. One thing leads to another . then to another. then to anther.  and then the elders get the phone call.  Oh I really need to marry her. like ASAP. Why what happened?. Oh you know.  that shaytan.  ⟪ar:فَدَلَّىٰهُمَا بِغُرُورٍۢ⟫   . he got us. Now I really need to marry her.  but I'm only 13 years . hahaha.

He will get to you. no matter how long it takes. in the end he will get to you. And you WILL end up doing what you said in the beginning. Remember? I'm just studying biology . it's not like we're . dot dot dot. Well . dot dot dot.  That's Shaytan for you.

### Tasting the tree

Then Allah says.

⟪ar-quote:فَلَمَّا ذَاقَا ٱلشَّجَرَةَ⟫

So they eventually. BTW. ⟪ar:اذا⟫when they did it. ⟪ar:حین⟫when they did it. .  ⟪ar:فلما⟫Eventually when they did it. so again.  this didn't happen immediately.  ⟪ar:ذَاقَا ٱلشَّجَرَةَ⟫both of them tasted the tree .  Now a lot has been said about not going near the tree!.  Don't go near the tree!.  And now allah says they both eventually tasted the tree.  Have any of you tasted a tree before? Have any of you been tempted ever to taste a tree.  What is on a tree that you are tempted by? It's the fruit! The fruit of the tree. Not the tree itself!. And typically is the fruit easily accessible? No it's not! Fruit is usually hanging on a branch.  The tree itself may be accessible.  You can touch the bark of a tree.  But to get to the fruit, you've got to climb a tree. And then get to the fruit.  Did Allah tell Adam. Do not eat the fruit? Did he say, do not approach the fruit? No! . Did he say, do not climb up on the tree? No! . He said do not go NEAR the tree! ⟪ar:فلا تقرب ھذہ الشجرۃ⟫

In Surah Isra we learn that  فلا تقرب ھذہ الشجرۃ turns for humanity into ولا تقرب الزنا.

لا تقرب ھذہ الشجرۃ turns into لا تقرب الزنا. We will inshallah talk about that later.

So when Allah says. ⟪ar:فَلَمَّا ذَاقَا ٱلشَّجَرَةَ⟫. So they tasted the tree. Meaning they didn't even get to the fruit. The implication is just by reaching out to the tree. they diobeyed Allah. because the command of Allah was not to approach the tree. And Iblees made them approach the tree. This is VERY important to understand!. You know why? Because as revelation proceeds. ⟪ar:فلا تقرب ھذہ الشجرۃ⟫ . turns into

⟪ar-quote:وَلَا تَقْرَبُوا۟ ٱلزِّنَىٰٓ.  إِنَّهُۥ كَانَ فَحِشَةًۭ وَسَآءَ سَبِيلًۭا⟫

Do no go near Zina. Indeed it is the most extreme form of shamelessness. and the ugliest path to walk on. Do you see the usage of the word Saa'a here? Ugly? Remember what Iblees wants?. To remove our clothes and expose our what? Ugliness.  ?? Allah does not say do not commit zina. do not commit adultry. He says. Do not go near Zina. Do not go near adultry. What does that mean? Don't even take the first step that will eventually. Falamma. lead you to zina.

So they both tasted the tree. and then what happened?

⟪ar-quote:بَدَتْ لَهُمَا سَوْءَتُهُمَا⟫

their ugliness got exposed. Iblees completed his mission. What did Allah say Iblees wanted?. Why did he do waswas? What was his ultimate goal?

⟪ar-quote:فَوَسْوَسَ لَهُمَا ٱلشَّيْطَنُ لِيُبْدِىَ لَهُمَا مَا وُۥرِىَ عَنْهُمَا مِن سَوْءَتِهِمَا⟫

He whispered to them IN ORDER TO expose their ugliness to them. And now Allah says. He was sucessful in doing what he intended to do. He got their clothes removed. He got them dishonored before Allah. Iblees got their ugliness exposed. The clothes of Jannah is what made them look beautiful.  and the removal of those clothes.  exposed their underlying skin.  which is referred to as ugliness. ⟪ar:سوئا⟫.  Because it is unnatural for human beings to be naked. especially After Allah honored them with the gift of clothes.

⟪ar-quote:وَطَفِقَا يَخْصِفَانِ عَلَيْهِمَا مِن وَرَقِ ٱلْجَنَّةِ⟫

So now they are trying to wrap themselves using the leaves of Jannah. A state of desperate humiliation.

And Allah calls upon them.

⟪ar-quote:وَنَادَىٰهُمَا رَبُّهُمَا⟫

⟪ar-quote:أَلَمْ أَنْهَكُمَا عَن تِلْكُمَا ٱلشَّجَرَةِ وَأَقُل لَّكُمَآ إِنَّ ٱلشَّيْطَنَ لَكُمَا عَدُوٌّۭ مُّبِينٌۭ⟫

Did I not forbid both of you from that tree? Did I not tell you both.  that no doubt. Shaitan is your clear enemy?. Did I not tell you that?  Why did you go back there? . Notice how Allah says here. THAT tree.  What did he say before? ⟪ar:فلا تقرب **ھذہ**الشجرۃ⟫. he used the word THIS. ⟪ar:ھذہ⟫.  He said this tree! But now Allah says that tree. ⟪ar:تلک الشجرۃ⟫. Did I not forbid you from THAT tree.  In other words. you both were doing so good. you were getting further and further away from the forbidden. Why did you let Iblees rope you back to it? . Why did you have to come close to that tree again?.  You had gotten away from it.  You weren't even tempted by it. Why did you go back? And had I not said to you, that Shaytan is your clear enemy? Why did you believe him? . Even if he swore to you. Even if he gave you all the rational logical explanations of the world. Why did you choose to believe him over MY command? . Why did you choose to trust HIM over ME??. What we're learning here.  is that Allah's command supercedes ALL of Iblees's logic.

Now does this mean we don't use logic? . Of course not. Use All the logic you need to come to the conclusion that Allah is your master. Take all the time you need. Make use of ALL the signs Allah has created. both inside and outside of this book. Use your intellect. Use you heart.

Allah says. Take as much time as you need.  to come to the conclusion that I am your master!. But once you've come to that conclusion. then submit to me. And what does submission mean? . Giving up MY logic. to the will and command of my MASTER. That's true submission. Ya Allah. I accept.  I admit. that nobody else is my master. You are my one and only master. ⟪ar:لا الہ الا اللہ⟫ . I have NO master except you!. And now I submit my intellect. my logic. my will. to YOUR logic. to YOUR intellect. to YOUR comamnd. That is true submission. That is true Sajdah. Just as the camel submits to its master. I will not longer go wherever I want to go. Once you're on my back. I will go wherever. YOU want me to go. That's sajdah. But that requires immense amount of trust. So study the message. Study the miracles. Understand how and why all this is beneficial ONLY for you. That's why I sent this message in the first place. That's why I sent my messengers. to explain everything to you. But once you submit. then give up your logic to go aginst my commands.

You know. when you join college. and you have multiple offers. you have options. You can pick which school you want to join. When you apply for jobs and you get multiple offers. You have options. You can pick which job you want. You can take the tour. You can visit your college. Look at the class rooms. meet the teachers. look at the acedemic structure. You can talk to other graduates. With a job. you can visit the building. meet with other employees. Find out what's what. You have that option. But once you accept an offer. Once you join the school. or accept the job. Once you sign the dotted line. do you still continue investigating? No. Because you made a very conscious choice before you joined that institution. Now you happily do whatever is required of you. Isn't that true? . Same with religion. It's really not such a difficult thing to understand.

The thing with Iblees is. He will not prevent you from joining Islam. Once you've joined. He will force you to use YOUR own logic. against the commands of Allah. He'll make you think of the most perfect arguments.  based on your incomplete knowledge of the facts. mixed in with your experential biases. and he will make you submit to your desires. and your passions and your caprice. that will go against the commands of Allah.

This is what he did with Adam and Hawwa علیھم السلام . He got them to disobey Allah AFTER they signed the dotted line. He got them to lose their clothings. He got them to get dishonored before Allah.  He brought them down from the ultimate honor. where angels are prostrating before them. to this level of humiliation where they are patching themselves up with leaves. There is remarkably imagery here.  Look at their state of desperation. Trying to patch themselves with leaves. Can you imagine that helplessness.  Allah didn't put them in that state did He? NO. He was the one who robed them with beautiful garments of jannah.  He put clothes on them. And then he also warned them! Look don't follow Shaytan! He's your enemy. He's going to try to get you out of jannah. Don't let him fool you!

But they didn't listen.  they disobeyed allah.  The natural consequence of which was their honor being removed from them.  and now they're helpless . trying to hide themselves again. with leaves. How can the inferior leaves compare with the robes and beautiful garments of jannah.  A picture of intense desperation is illustrated here. How desperate we as creations are in need of our creator. If he takes his blessings away. look at what pathetic state we would fall to. SubhanAllah!  And look at what state Iblees wants to bring us down to. (نعوذ باللہ من الشیطان الرجیم)

And so Allah repremands them. Did I not ask you to stay away from that tree? Did I not warn you that Shaytan is your clear enemy?

### Difference between reactions of Adam and Iblees

⟪ar-quote:قَالَا رَبَّنَا ظَلَمْنَآ أَنفُسَنَا⟫

They said, master we have wronged ourselves. Now they are both crying.  they're repenting and they're saying.
⟪ar-quote:رَبَّنَا ظَلَمْنَآ أَنفُسَنَا⟫

Master . we have wronged ourselves.
⟪ar-quote:وَإِن لَّمْ تَغْفِرْ لَنَا وَتَرْحَمْنَا لَنَكُونَنَّ مِنَ ٱلْخَسِرِينَ⟫

and if you don't forgive us. for OUR mistake.  and you don't have mercy on us. we will definitely become from the losers.

Now in this ayah.  we also learn about this staunch difference between Adam and Iblees.  They both disobeyed Allah. They both disobeyed Allah. They both disappointed Allah. Iblees was asked to do something. that he didn't do. Adam and Hawwa were asked NOT to do something. which they did. Both forms of disobediences occurred in this story. What we learn from this story is that disobedience to Allah. happens in both forms. There is disobedience of commission. and there is disobedience of omission. There's disobedience. when we don't do what we are commanded to do by Allah . And there is disobedience when we DO . what we are are commanded NOT to do. That's the first thing.

But the greatest lesson in this story. is their response to their disobedience. It's an incredible lesson. Iblees disobeys Allah. Allah asks him why did you disbelieve?
⟪ar-quote:قَالَ مَا مَنَعَكَ أَلَّا تَسْجُدَ إِذْ أَمَرْتُكَ⟫

Why did you now prostrate. when I commanded you to do so?. What was his reply?
⟪ar-quote:ۖ قَالَ أَنَا۠ خَيْرٌۭ مِّنْهُ خَلَقْتَنِى مِن نَّارٍۢ وَخَلَقْتَهُۥ مِن طِينٍۢ⟫

I am better than him. You created me from fire and you created him from clay. right? Arrogance was his reply. Justifications for his disobedience was his reply. Rationalization was his reply. Lack of accountability. Lack of taking responsibility was his reply. Ego . Pride. Jealousy. Greed. was his reply.  Correct?

Now do Adam and Hawwa also disobey Allah? Yes!. Does Allah question them both as well about their disobedience? . He does!
⟪ar-quote:أَلَمْ أَنْهَكُمَا عَن تِلْكُمَا ٱلشَّجَرَةِ وَأَقُل لَّكُمَآ إِنَّ ٱلشَّيْطَنَ لَكُمَا عَدُوٌّۭ مُّبِينٌۭ⟫

Did I not tell you.  not to go near that tree and did I not tell you that Shaytan is your clear enemy.  right? But look how they both respond to Allah's question.

⟪ar-quote:قَالَا رَبَّنَا ظَلَمْنَآ أَنفُسَنَا⟫

Master WE . WE have wronged ourselves. We admit. We take complete responsibility for our actions. You are right. We are wrong. SubhanAllah! . What a beautiful response. What a beautiful response. Complete accountability. Complete responsibility. WE are the one's who wronged our souls. . . Not. It was Iblees who wronged us. Not. that Ya Allah. he swore by you. We did not believe him. He kept trying for months and months. and we didn't believe him. It was ONLY when he lied to us . and swore on your name. we believed. .You should punish him not us!

Ya Allah. come on. You can understand . we don't know what lies is. we've never experienced deception before. So you can understand why we got fooled despite the fact that you told us. despite the fact that you warned us. Could they have done that? They ABSOLUTELY could have. But instead what do they say?
⟪ar-quote:قَالَا رَبَّنَا ظَلَمْنَآ أَنفُسَنَا⟫

Master . it is WE who wronged ourselves. period! We are at fault. We take full responsibility. We messed up. They don't even MENTION Iblees. Think about that. They don't even mention Iblees. SubhanAllah. Because NO Ya Allah. You commanded us . WE disobeyed you. Khalas. We are the wrong doers. Doesn't matter why we did it. or who made us do it. In the end we disobeyed YOUR command. and WE are responsible for our actions. What a beautiful response of a true slave . And what a befitting response to such a glorious master!. SubhanAllah. And then.
⟪ar-quote:وَإِن لَّمْ تَغْفِرْ لَنَا وَتَرْحَمْنَا⟫

And now if you don't forgive us. and if you don't have mercy on us. ⟪ar:لَنَكُونَنَّ مِنَ ٱلْخَسِرِينَ⟫we will be doomed. We will be destroyed. Complete humility. Not a shred of arrogance. Ya Allah we are completely dependent on YOUR mercy. And we are completely dependent on YOUR forgiveness. Without those two things from you. we are done!

This is the greatest lesson for us. What we're learning here is that disobedience can happen by anyone. It can happen by a jinn. it can happen by a human being. Disobedience WILL happen. It will happen because of our desires. because of our caprice. because of the heat of the moment. because of anger. because of haste. because of not thinking things through. because of deception from others.  like in the case of Adam AS. because of making the wrong kinds of friends. because of listening to the wrong kinds of poeple.  or simply because our lack of knowledge. Disobedience will happen. But it is NOT the disobedience. but our RESPONSE to the disobedience. It is our response. after realizing a mistake. how we respond. that's what will differentiate us  between becoming Iblees or Adam.

This is the difference between Adam and Iblees. they both made mistakes. Adam faultered. We are Bani Adam. We are the children of Adam. You and I make mistakes. We will continue making mistakes.  Look! making a mistake. comitting a sin is no big thing before Allah's mercy.  Being arrogant and persisting in it.  That is what's destructive! Coming up with justifications to continue a life in sin. THAT is what's disasterous.  It's not possible for us human beings NOT to sin! It's part of our nature. it's part of our very fabric. The only person who does not sin is a corpse. a dead person. Other than that we all sin. The question is.  when we realize our mistake. how do we respond? . That's what it all boils down to.  Do we choose to persist in that act or not. That's the measuring stick.

If we choose to persist. If we choose to justify. If we choose to rationalize. If we choose to NOT take responsibility and blame others.   then that's arrogance. That's the path of Ibless. So what if I smoke? Everybody smokes! So what if I drink? Everybody drinks! That's what's really dangerous. that's the path of Shaytan. and if we follow the path of Shaytan.  then we necessarily will end up at the same final destination that he ended up in. which is hell fire. On the other hand, if we accept our fault.  and we change our path. stop doing what we're not supposed to do. Or we start doing what we're supposed to do.  then we're walking the path of adam and hawwa AS and we end up at their destination in the end. which is Jannah again.

But that can only happen if we believe in two things. The immense FORGIVENESS of Allah. and the immense MERCY of Allah. Those who choose to continue a life of sin. they are the ones who reject and deny the forgiveness and mercy of Allah.
