⟪ar-quote:قَالَ ٱهْبِطُوا۟ بَعْضُكُمْ لِبَعْضٍ عَدُوٌّۭ⟫

Fall down from here. Descend from this place. From this day on you are enemies to each other. meaning Shaytan and Adam.  But then Allah says
⟪ar-quote:وَلَكُمْ فِى ٱلْأَرْضِ مُسْتَقَرٌّۭ وَمَتَعٌ إِلَىٰ حِينٍۢ⟫

I have appointed a fixed time for you all. and I have given you means to enjoy life.  ⟪ar:متاع⟫means material that you can enjoy.  Then he said. . ⟪ar-quote:قَالَ فِيهَا تَحْيَوْنَ⟫   in this world you will live   ⟪ar-quote:وَفِيهَا تَمُوتُونَ⟫   and in it you will die  ⟪ar-quote:وَمِنْهَا تُخْرَجُونَ⟫   and from it you will be taken out again.

Children of ADAM

---

⟪ar-quote:يَبَنِىٓ آدَمَ⟫

Oh Children of adam! Who is he talking to now?
⟪ar-quote:يَبَنِىٓ آدَمَ⟫

O children of Adam. He just told us the story of our parents.  and now Allah says. Were you listening? Were you listening?.  That was your parents I just described. I just told you the story of your parents. YOU listen now.
⟪ar-quote:يَبَنِىٓ آدَمَ قَدْ أَنزَلْنَا عَلَيْكُمْ لِبَاسًۭا يُوَرِى سَوْءَتِكُمْ وَرِيشًۭا⟫

SubhanAllah! What does the MOST merciful.  the MOST loving do again? What is the first thing he does again for us. After sending us to this world?
⟪ar-quote:قَدْ أَنزَلْنَا عَلَيْكُمْ لِبَاسًۭا يُوَرِى سَوْءَتِكُمْ وَرِيشًۭا⟫

We have sent down clothing upon you. so that you can cover up your ugliness.  Some of the most beautiful words of the quran.  ⟪ar:قَدْ أَنزَلْنَا عَلَيْكُمْ لِبَاسًۭا⟫ we have sent down ⟪ar:انزلنا⟫. clothing upon you. .  Quran is revelation from the sky. that is sent down upon us. Rain is a gift from allah that is sent down upon us. Angels that descend from the sky.  protect us and pray for us.  They are a gifts from allah. These are all gifts from allah that He sends down upon us!.  And Allah sent down clothing upon us. Allah says you didn't make clothing! I sent clothing down for you! I sent down for you all the material that you can use to make clothing. Clothing. the concept of covering up.  is actually part of revelation. 

Look at the words  ⟪ar:قَدْ أَنزَلْنَا⟫  where have we heard the word ⟪ar:أَنزَلْنَا⟫before?  ⟪ar:انا انزلناہ فی لیلۃ القدر⟫. We revealed the quran . We sent down the quran in lailatul Qadr. And here he says
⟪ar:قَدْ أَنزَلْنَا عَلَيْكُمْ لِبَاسًۭا⟫  Subhan Allah!!.  Allah gave clothing the same status.  as He gave his revelation.  Clothing is a revealed gift!.  Disregarding clothing.  is disregarding a piece of revelation.  Quran was sent down.  clothing was sent down.  If we really try to understand.  if we really fathom what Allah is saying here. we will have a completely different appreciateion when we dress up from now on.

What was the first thing that was given to Adam and Hawwa in jannah? Clothes.  What was taken away from them as a result of their disobedience? Clothes! . What is the first thing given to us again.  when we're sent to this world? Clothes! Allah honored us again! with clothes. ⟪ar:قَدْ أَنزَلْنَا عَلَيْكُمْ لِبَاسًۭا يُوَرِى سَوْءَتِكُمْ⟫. Here is my gift to you again .  I'll cover your shame up again.  I'll cover your ugliness again.  ⟪ar:يُوَرِى سَوْءَتِكُمْ⟫ . Just as I did for your parents.

Now BTW . clothing could have been hideous right? If the intention of clothing was just to cover private parts.  it didn't need to be pretty. did it?.  It could have a been ugly.  it could have been hideous. but allah says. I'm not just giving you clothes to cover your uglinesss. I'm also giving you clothes to look beautiful.
⟪ar:يُوَرِى سَوْءَتِكُمْ وَرِيشًۭا⟫

Reesh is the arabic word for beautiful feathers. peackock feathers.  when it opens up its feathers. its called Reesh.! When archers put feather on their arrows . ⟪ar:قَبلَ الرَّمِی یُرَاش السَّھَمُ⟫ before shooting the arrow.  you feather the arrow. because it gets better navigation. So reeshan is used for beautification.  Allah says we sent down clothes for you to cover you ugliness AND AND for fashion! to dress nicely.  to look beautiful. to accessorise.  all of that is reeshan. You don't need to take off your clothes to look beautiful. You can look beautiful BY MEANS of your clothes.

And another thing we're learnign from this ayah is . dress nicely. dress nicely. especially boys and men. Allah didn't just give us clothes to cover our body. If we look like bum. we are not appreciating allah's gift. it doesn't have to be expensive. just iron the shirt once in a while. don't look like. you know. what you look like HAHAHA. dress nicely. see this is another waswasa of shaytah. Islam wants us to look ugly. Shaytan says. the more clothes you take off. the tighter clothes you wear. the more skin you show. the more beautiful you will look. the tighter TShirt you wear. Its ok. show some skin. you look sexy. expose yourself. you look beautiful.

The real question is beautiful to WHO? Beautiful to Shaytan! Beautiful to the followers of shaytan. Not to Allah! definitely not to allah. because in this ayah allah says you don't need to expose your body to show your beauty. I've given you clothes for that. so clothes are not a means of making us look ugly. clothes are a means of making us look beautiful.  وَرِيشًۭا

and then he adds.
⟪ar-quote:وَلِبَاسُ ٱلتَّقْوَىٰ ذَلِكَ خَيْرٌۭ⟫

and the clothing of taqwa. being aware of Allah at all times. THAT is the best clothing for your soul. He honored us with clothing for the body. he honored us with clothing for the soul. SubhanAllah! Taqwa is the ultimate outfit you can dress your soul in.  Every single day Shaytan is taking both our clothings off.  and we don't even realize what we're doing.

So Allah says the concept of clothing. is not just physical. It is also spiritual. Physical clothing will protect your bodies. And spiritual clothing. Taqwa. piety.  will protect your soul.
⟪ar-quote:وَلِبَاسُ ٱلتَّقْوَىٰ ذَلِكَ خَيْرٌۭ. ذَلِكَ مِنْ آيَتِ ٱللَّهِ لَعَلَّهُمْ يَذَّكَّرُونَ⟫

That is from the great signs of allah.  so that they can make an effort to remember allah. To remember Allah. EVERY single time we put on clothes. EVERYTHING I have shared with you about the Istiaaza. EVERYTHING is supposed to flash through our minds.⟪ar:لَعَلَّهُمْ يَذَّكَّرُونَ⟫. So that you can remember Allah through clothing. When I put on my clothes. I am supposed to remember this is an HONOR for me from Allah. Just as I am covering up my shame. my ugliness with clothes. I need to cover up my soul in piety. I have to protect myself from Shaytan. who is going to try to remove my clothes. Not directly by taking my clothes off. But by putting me on a path. that will result in my clothes being removed before Allah. SubhanAllah.

then he says.

---

⟪ar-quote:يَبَنِىٓ آدَمَ لَا يَفْتِنَنَّكُمُ ٱلشَّيْطَنُ كَمَآ أَخْرَجَ أَبَوَيْكُم مِّنَ ٱلْجَنَّةِ⟫

Oh children of adam. don't let shaytan do to you. what he did to your parents. In other words. learn the lesson from the story of your parents that happened before you. The arabs say.
⟪ar-quote:السَّعِیدُ مِنَ الطَّعَتْ بِغَیرِہِ⟫

True happiness is for the one who learns his lessons from other people. They don't have to prove those lessons for themselves. This is the idea that those who don't know their history. are condemned to repeate it over and over again.

This is why we're being told this story. because with us on this earth. there is this struggle that is going on. And there are two components of this struggle. YOUR desire. Because if you didn't desire the thing in the first place. then nobody could convince you to even try it. So YOU and I have this thing called ھوی. Caprice or desire. and then there is an unseen element working in the world . which is suggesting to us. to explore that hawa. to test it. to try it. That's ذوق. or ذاق. The desire to check it out. see what it is like. That's what got our parents expelled from Jannah.

You see they had the desire in them to live in Jannah forever. If they did not have that desire. they would never have listened to Iblees. EVEN when he swore before them. they wouldn't have listened. If they had NO desire. But they DID have that desire. and Shaytan made them explore it. But it was just the taste. the Zawq. that constituted as their disobedience.

And then Allah says.
⟪ar-quote:يَنزِعُ عَنْهُمَا لِبَاسَهُمَا لِيُرِيَهُمَا سَوْءَتِهِمَآ⟫

He pulled off their clothes. so that he could expose their ugliness . Look at these words. ⟪ar:يَنزِعُ⟫.  he pulled off their clothes. The word ⟪ar:نزع⟫means to pull out. You know how when someone is about to die.  in their last moments . they say he is in the state of ⟪ar:نزع⟫.  It means his soul is being pulled out of their body.  This ayat says.  Shaytan pulled their clothes off of them. Now that would indicate that Shaytan had more power over them! Yes or no?.  Suggesting to take off clothes is something else.  pulling off clothes is something else.  So how come Allah says Shaytan pulled off their clothes?

This ayah is teaching us. and please listen to this very carefully. This ayah is teaching us that diobeying allah.  grants authority to shaytan. Disobeying allah.  grants power to shaytan over us. Evertime you and I dress inappropriately. in both the physical and spiritual sense.  we give more and more power to shaytan.  Shaytan gets more power over you and me. 

EVERY single time we disobey allah.  the more we disobey Allah.  the more shaytan gets power over us.  until the point where he can simply tell us what to do.  and we comply like his slave. He will simply command and we will obey. 

The only power Allah had gave shaytan ORIGINALLY. was to do waswasa. to whisper.  but WE give him the real power of command.  by accepting.  listening to and complying with his whisper. And the more we do it. the more power he gets over us. He keeps getting strong and stronger and stronger. until he gains complete authority over us. He can now simply command us to do something. Because Allah says.

⟪ar-quote:ٱلشَّيْطَنُ يَعِدُكُمُ ٱلْفَقْرَ وَيَأْمُرُكُم بِٱلْفَحْشَآءِ⟫

Shaytan promises you bankrupcy . bankrupcy where? Before allah!.  He promises that by the time you stand before Allah.  I promise.  you will not have a single good deed to your name.
⟪ar:يَعِدُكُمُ ٱلْفَقْر⟫َ    and how does he do that?  ⟪ar:وَيَأْمُرُكُم بِٱلْفَحْشَآءِ⟫ ۖ  . He commands you to ludeness. to shamelessness. Allah didn't say
⟪ar:یُوَسوِسُ لکم الفحشاء . یَنسِحُو لکم ان تفشحو⟫ .

He suggested ludeness to you. He whispered to you. No no no no no.  Allah says. He said he COMMANDS you to shamelessness.  How does he command you? People have come to me and said. I can't stop watching porn.  I can't stop smoking.  I know you can't!.  Because shaytan is commanding you! Cause you keep disobeying Allah. You have to cut it off. That's the only way for shaytan to let go of you.  is you've got to stop. You and I have to take back that control. by giving that control to Allah. where it belongs.  because Allah said to the shaytan.
⟪ar-quote:‏إِنَّ عِبَادِى لَيْسَ لَكَ عَلَيْهِمْ سُلْطَنٌ⟫

You will have no authority over my slaves. what does that mean?. If they're not really MY slaves. you will have complete authority over them.  ⟪ar:‏إِنَّ عِبَادِى لَيْسَ لَكَ عَلَيْهِمْ سُلْطَنٌ⟫. this is our legacy in this world.

Then Allah says.

⟪ar-quote:إِنَّهُۥ يَرَىٰكُمْ هُوَ وَقَبِيلُهُۥ مِنْ حَيْثُ لَا تَرَوْنَهُمْ⟫

He is constnatly watching you. He and his tribe of followers.   Did he not say to allah that he will sit on the straight path. waiting to ambush us?. And when somebody is waiting to ambush can you see them or no? Allah says I made that part of your test! He is watching you! He and his entire tribe.  ⟪ar:مِنْ حَيْثُ لَا تَرَوْنَهُمْ⟫. from a place wher eyou can't even see them.

⟪ar-quote:إِنَّا جَعَلْنَا ٱلشَّيَطِينَ أَوْلِيَآءَ لِلَّذِينَ لَا يُؤْمِنُونَ⟫

All the devils. and legions of them have made friends with people who don't believe.  People who don't believe will accept that whisper. and they will enjoy that whisper.  The guy will say.  my parents aren't home right now. I can watch whatever I want. I can do whatever I want. Nobody will ever know. I can smoke. I can take a tic tac later. Nobody will know.  Allah will know.

So after narrating the entire story of Adam and Iblees. Allah talks to us. the children of Adam. and warns us. Don't repeat the same mistake your parents made. Don't listen to Shaytan. He got your parents kicked out of jannah. He will do the same to you. So be careful. don't repeat the same mistake. I warned them too. they didn't listen. I'm warning YOU now. Be careful!. Don't disobey me. And if you do end up disobeying me. then follow the pattern of your parents. by accepting your fault. by accepting accountability for your actions. and then after taking complete responsibility for your action. repent before Allah. Don't follow the pattern of Iblees and come up with logical reasonings to justify your disobedience. Because he will entice you. He will attack you. And once you give him power by your constant disobedience to me. and your constant obedience to him. he will then make you his slave. He will command you to sin. and you will comply. Because he wants to dishonor you before Allah. He wants to take off your clothes. Clothing. that I have equated with revelation. Clothing for your body as well as your soul. I have made physical clothing. not just a covering for your ugliness. but also means of adornment for you. So that you can look beautiful. And I have made piety. taqwa. a clothing for your soul. so that it not only covers up your sins . but also adorns your personality and makes you respectable before Allah and his creation. And this spiritual clothing of taqwa is better between the two. ⟪ar:وَلِبَاسُ ٱلتَّقْوَىٰ ذَلِكَ خَيْرٌۭ⟫ . Why? Because in order to be pious. you will need to dress appropriately. You will need to dress modestly. You can't dress in a lude manner and be pious. That's why it is better between the two. Also because it adorns your soul. which is going to return to me. Your body is going to decay in the dirt. So what's more important is the clothing of the soul. But you can't have one without the other.

And how do you create this spritual clothing? What's the raw material for you to create this spiritual clothing?. this taqwa. It is this revelation. That's why I sent down revelation. and I sent down clothing.

All excuses will fail on judgment day

now look at this. allah continues. now these are comments on the mushrikoon of mecca. this is actually a commentary on all society.

وَإِذَا فَعَلُوا۟ فَحِشَةًۭ  when they did something shameless قَالُوا۟ وَجَدْنَا عَلَيْهَآ آبَآءَنَا

they said. our parents did this. what are you talking about? this is totally normal. there is nothing wrong with this. our parents used to dress like this. why can't we dress like this? Whats the big deal? my parents watched indian movies. we watch american movies. so what's the big deal. I've been raised watchign a guy go after a girl; a girl go after a guy. so what if I did it in college? this ayah is not just talking about Quraish. it's not just talking about the disbelievers of mecca. its talking about you and me. because these are the words your and my children will say when they grow up. if we don't change ourselves today. this is what we will have to hear our children say one day. what will you do then? what will I do then? What's happening at weddings today? The dresses the functions? and what do we say. it's all good. its all normal. but normal for who? Allah or shaytaan? This then develops further into . so what if I have a girlfriend? So what if I have a boy friendd? so what if I watch this filth on the internet. anybody and everybody does it. its' not such a big deal.

Now let me tell you something. on judgment day. this social circle you're using as an excuse. those friends you are using as an excuse. even your parents that you're using as an excuse. on judgment day you will not be able to stand before allah and say. I did it because they did it. they are the reasons for which I am messed up. it won't work.

يَوْمَ يَفِرُّ ٱلْمَرْءُ مِنْ أَخِيهِ  on that day each person will run away . abandon his own brother

وَأُمِّهِۦ وَأَبِيهِ   and his mother and his father

وَصَحِبَتِهِۦ وَبَنِيهِ   and his wife and his children

these are very scary. very powerful words. these are not words for you and me to take lightly.  because people of quraish tried that. they said. our ancesstors did it so what if we did it?  وَٱللَّهُ أَمَرَنَا بِهَا

God wants us to be like this. they went even a step further and said it is allahs' will that we are doing this. if he didnt' want us to dress like this. do all this stuff why would he allow all this to happen. ??? God wants us to be happy! Theres nothing wrong with wanting to be happy. to look sexy. god wants us to be happy bro!  that's why I love her. thats why I love him! those people went as far as to say وَٱللَّهُ أَمَرَنَا بِهَا  allah wants us to do all this stuff! allah wants us to be like this.

  ۗ قُلْ إِنَّ ٱللَّهَ لَا يَأْمُرُ بِٱلْفَحْشَآءِ ۖ

Tell them. Allah does not command you to shamelessness. he does not want you to be lude or indecent. Theres another lesson here. when people deviate from allahs path. they become so arrogant that they start speaking on behalf of allah.  Allah doesn't want us to be so harsh. allah doesnt' want us to be so conservative. don't be so hard on yourself. but allah forgives. where does allah say in the quran you have to do this or that or the other? Ever heard that one before? I'll show you where allah say all of that! You wanna know where allah says in the quran? I'll show you! because when someone says that. you know what the truth is? They've alrady made up their mind to disobey allah!

so as we grow in arrogance. we start speaking on behalf of allah. and we start saying there is nothing wrong with that. thats totally fine. Allahs says.

 أَتَقُولُونَ عَلَى ٱللَّهِ مَا لَا تَعْلَمُونَ    Are you saying things against allah that He has no knowledge of ?  Tell them قُلْ أَمَرَ رَبِّى بِٱلْقِسْطِ

Tell them. my master commands to fairness. to justice.  وَأَقِيمُوا۟ وُجُوهَكُمْ عِندَ كُلِّ مَسْجِدٍۢ

Now look. allah was talking about ludeness and indecency and now the subject changed to justice and prayer. he says قُلْ أَمَرَ رَبِّى بِٱلْقِسْطِ ۖ وَأَقِيمُوا۟ وُجُوهَكُمْ عِندَ كُلِّ مَسْجِدٍۢ

Tell them my master comamnds to justice and to face towards the masjid. meaning establish prayers. establish salaah. what this is teaching us that shamelessness will lead us to injustice and shamelessness will lead us to giving up our prayers.

now you tell me. is the filth industry . an injustice and mainuplation of women? is this industry built upon the violation of dignity of women? Yes or no? and BTW the old form of it was prostitution. was that not a form of injustice to women? was that not an opression to women? That was a subject that the quran actually attacked. it talked about prostitution and how it should come to an end. because shamelessness because an industry and a vehicle through which injustice is spread and allah says. he does not command to injustice. and thats just at the societal level.

but at the personal level . how will you stay away from shamelessness? You will remain upright before allah and do justice with yourself and allah. through the means of salaah. now what does salaah have to do with staying away from shamelessness? EVERYTHING! Every thing. Salaah has EVERYTHING to do with shamelessness. Allah explicity says that in the quran.

ٱتْلُ مَآ أُوحِىَ إِلَيْكَ مِنَ ٱلْكِتَبِ وَأَقِمِ ٱلصَّلَوٰةَ ۖ إِنَّ ٱلصَّلَوٰةَ تَنْهَىٰ عَنِ ٱلْفَحْشَآءِ وَٱلْمُنكَرِ

Keep reciting the book that was revealed to you and establish prayer. Indeed. no doubt about it. Prayer prevents you from all forms of shamelessness and other evils.

People say. I pray 5 times a day but I still can't keep away from filth. my answer to that is. you are not really praying. You are not really connecting with allah. you're just going through the motions. because according to this ayah. allah say. ان. no doubt! Absolutely! 100% If you are praying. if you really are connecting with me. it will protect you from shamelessness. So if you pray but still struggle with shamelessness. you need to really examing and evaluate your prayers.

1:16:52

Allah created us in comfort

Allah says in the Quran to human beings.

وَلَقَدْ مَكَّنَّكُمْ فِى ٱلْأَرْضِ وَجَعَلْنَا لَكُمْ فِيهَا مَعَيِشَ.  قَلِيلًۭا مَّا تَشْكُرُونَ

We settled you down on the earth. and we gave you good housing. Makanna means good housing.  and especially for you وَجَعَلْنَا لَكُمْ . especially for you.  we put all means on this earth so that you could live well.  معایش  is actully from معیشۃ which means life that is well lived.  in urdu we use this word عیش . .

بڑے عیش سے رہ رہے ہیں. That's an arabic word.  means to live very well. العیش have is a good life. Allah say we put means of a good life for you on this earth. So that's the first misconception addressed. People think Islam has so many rules.  it doesnt want us to live a good life. Allah doesn want us to enjoy ourselves. Allah is telling us. that he created us on this earth in order for us to have a good life.

You know this same word عیش is used to describe the paradise. فھو فی عیشۃ راضیۃ. They will live a great life in jannah. And there is a glimpse of that even in this world. There are glimpses of معائش  . means of living really really well on this earth. enjoying ourselves.

And by the way.  where does enjoyment come from? Enjoyment happens when you get what you desire. X2.

It's very simple.  you have a craving.  and you fulfill that craving and that is what enjoyment is. I'm really craving to play some tennis. I got to play. I enjoyed myself. I'm craving playing a video game.  I got to play.  I enjoyed myself. right? I'm craving some chocolate icecream. I was able to have it. I enjoyed myself. cravings!  When cravings are fulfilled. that's when enjoyment happens. You have an itch. you scratch it. that's enjoyment. enjoyment does not happen outside of that.

And so our temptations are also a cravings. The attraction a man has towards a woman is also a craving. And allah says in this world. I gave you means by which you CAN enjoy yourselves. You can fulfill all your craving in a legitimate way. I've given you provisions for all of that. All of that is covered.

وَجَعَلْنَا لَكُمْ فِيهَا مَعَيِشَ
